  nārāyaṇam nikhila pūrṇa guṇa eka deham nirdoṣam āpyatamam api akhilaiḥ su vākyaiḥ asya udbhavāt idam aśeṣa viśeṣataḥ api vandyam sadā priyatamam mama sannamāmi tam eva śāstra prabhavam praṇamya jagadgurūṇām gurum añjasā eva viśeṣataḥ  me parama ākhya vidyā vyākhyām karomi anu api ca aham eva prādurbhūtaḥ  hariḥ vyāsaḥ  viriñca bhava pūrvakaiḥ arthitaḥ paravidyā ākhyam cakre śāstram anuttamam guruḥ gurūṇām prabhavaḥ śāstrāṇām bādarāyaṇaḥ yatas tad uditam mānam aja ādibhyaḥ tad arthataḥ vaktṛ śrotṛ prasaktīnām yad ā āptiḥ anukūla tā āpta vākya tayā tena śruti mūla tayā tathā yukti mūla tayā ca eva prāmāṇyam trividham mahat  dṛśyate brahmasūtrāṇām ekadhānyatra sarvaśas  atas  na etādṛśam kiñcid  pramāṇatamam iṣyate svayam kṛtā api tadvayā ākhyā kriyate spaṣṭa tā arthataḥ tatra tārātha mūla tvam sarva śas astrasya ca iṣyate sarvatra anugata tvena pṛthak oṅkriyate akhilaiḥ otatva vācī hi oṅkāraḥ  vaktayasau tad guṇa ūtatām sa eva brahma śabda arthaḥ  nārāyaṇa pada uditaḥ sa eva bharga śabda arthaḥ  vyāhṛtīnām ca bhūmataḥ bhāvanāt ca eva sutvāt ca saḥ  ayam puruṣa iti api sa eva sarva veda arthaḥ  jijñāsyaḥ  ayam vidhīyate jñānī priyatamaḥ  atas  me tam vidvān eva ca amṛtaḥ vṛṇute yam tena labhya ityāt yukti balena hi jijñāsā uttha jñāna jāt  tad prasādāt eva mucyate dravyam karma ca kālaḥ ca svabhāvaḥ  jīva eva ca yad anugrahataḥ santi na santi yad upekṣayā na ṛte tvat  kriyate kiñcid iti ādeḥ na harim vinā jñāna svabhāvataḥ  api syāt muktiḥ kasya api hi kvacid  ajñānām jñāna daḥ  viṣṇuḥ jñāninām mokṣa daḥ ca saḥ ānanda daḥ ca muktānām sa eva ekaḥ  janārdanaḥ iti ukteḥ bandha mithyātvam na eva muktiḥ apekṣate mithyātvam api bandhasya na pratyakṣa virodhataḥ mithyātvam yadi duḥkha ādeḥ tad vākya agratas  bhavet  mithyāyāḥ sādhaka tvam ca na siddham prativādinaḥ tad ca mithyā pramāṇena satā vā sādhyate tvayā satā ced  dvaita siddhiḥ syāt na siddham ca anya sādhanam sādhaka tvam sataḥ tena sākṣiṇā siddhim icchatā svīkṛtam hi aviśeṣasya sādhyā sādhaka tā punar  tad ca āviśeṣa mānena sādhyam iti anavasthitiḥ anaṅgīkurvatām viśva satyatām tad na vāditā tasmāt  vyavahṛtiḥ sarvā satyā iti eva vyavasthitā vyāvahārikam etasmāt  satyam iti eva ca āgatam vyavahāra sataḥ ca api sādhaka tvam tu pūrvavat  sattra evidhyam ca mānena siddhayet  kena iti pṛcchyate tasya api ukta prakāreṇa na eva siddhiḥ kathañcana vailakṣaṇyam sat asatoḥ api etena niṣidhyate vailakṣaṇyam sataḥ ca api svayam sadbheda vādinaḥ asataḥ ca api viśvasya tena aniṣyam katham bhavet  yadi ucyate api sarvasmāt iti sadbheda saṃsthitiḥ sat mātra tvam brahmaṇaḥ  api tasmāt  tad api naḥ bhavet  jñāna bādhya tvam api tu na siddham prativādinaḥ vijñātasya anyathā samyak  vijñānam hi eva tad matam asat vilakṣaṇa jñaptyai jñātavyam asat eva hi tasmāt asat pratītiḥ ca katham tena nivāryate anyathātvam asat tasmāt  bhrāntau  eva pratīyate sattvasya āsata evam hi svīkārya eva pratīta tā tasya anirvacanīya tve syāt eva hi anavasthitiḥ nirviśeṣe svayam bhāte kim ajñāna āvṛtam bhavetaḥ mithyā viśeṣaḥ  api ajñāna siddhim eva hi apekṣate nacāa varaṇam ajñānam asatye tena ca iṣyate aprakāśa svarūpa tvāt jaḍe ajñānam na manyate ajñāna abhāvataḥ śāstram sarvam vyarthībhaviṣyati ajñānasya ca mithyātvam ajñānāt iti kalpane anavasthitiḥ tathā ca syāt anyonya āśrayatā athavā svabhāva ajñāna vādasya nirdoṣa tvāt na tad  bhavet  avidyā durghaṭa tvam ced  syāt ātmā api hi tādṛśaḥ atas  adhikāri viṣaya phala yoga ādi varjitam ananta doṣa duṣṭam ca heyam māyā matam śubhaiḥ satya tvāt  tena duḥkha ādeḥ pratyakṣeṇa virodhataḥ na brahma tām vadet  vedaḥ  jīvasya hi kathañcana yajamāna prastara tvam yathā na arthaḥ śruteḥ bhavet  brahma tvam api jīvasya pratyakṣasya aviśeṣataḥ sārvajñi ādi guṇam jīvāt  bhinnam jñāpayati śrutiḥ īśam tām upajīvya eva vartate hi aikya vādinī upajīvya virodhena na asyāḥ tad mānatā bhavet  svātantrye ca viśiṣṭa tve sthāna mattya aikyayoḥ api sādṛśye ca aikya vāc  samyak  sa avakāśā yathā iṣyataḥ avakāśa ujkhitā bheda śrutiḥ na atibalā katham ajñāna asambhavāt eva mithyā bhedaḥ  nirākṛtaḥ atas  yathārtha bandhasya vinā viṣṇu prasādataḥ anivṛtteḥ tad artham hi jijñāsā atra vidhīyate yathā dṛṣṭayā prasannaḥ san rājā bandha apanoda kṛt evam dṛṣṭaḥ sa bhagavān kuryāt  bandha vibhedanam kārya tā ca na kācid  syāt iṣṭa sādhana tām vinā kāryam na hi kriyā vyāpyam niṣiddhasya samatvataḥ na bhaviṣyat kriyā kāryam srakṣyati īśa iti hi api kāryam syāt na eva ca akartum aśakyam kāryam iṣyate sāmyāt eva niṣiddhasya tad iṣṭam sādhanam tathā kāryam sādhanam iṣṭasya bhagavān iṣṭadevatā mukhyeṣyam vā sumanasām preyaḥ tad iti ca śrutiḥ prāṇa buddhi manaḥ kha ātma deha apatya dhana ādayaḥ yad samparkāt  priyā āsan  tatas  kaḥ  nu aparaḥ priyaḥ ityādi vākyaiḥ ākāṅkṣā sannidhiḥ yogya tā yatas  asmin  eva samastasya itīṣye vyutpattiḥ iṣyate attya pūpān  tava bhrātā iti ādauvau  āpataḥ  api ca udvāpāt  vartamāna tvāt ākāṅkṣa ādi balāt api bālaḥ  vyutpattim apyeti nānayā ityādi vākyataḥ ānīyamāna dṛṣṭayā eva vyutpatteḥ sambhave sati eṣyat ānayanāya ayam kuta eva pratīkṣate vyutpannaḥ  vartamāne tu kriyā śabde bhaviṣyati punar dṛṣṭyā eva śabda śrut paścāt  vyutpattim eṣyati vartamānam atītam ca bhaviṣyat iti ca kramāt  ākāṅkṣa ādi yutam yasmāt  vidheḥ vyutpādanam kutas  dṛṣṭyā jñāta padārthasya pada ākāṅkṣā bhaviṣyati vyutpattiḥ prathamā tasmāt  vatarmāne gate tatas  iṣṭam ākāṅkṣate sarvaḥ  na pravṛttim apekṣate aparokṣam parokṣam vā jñānam iṣṭasya sādhanam kvāpi ceṣyā tad arthā syāt attiḥ hi rasa vittaye vākya artha jñāna mātreṇa kvacid iṣṭam bhavet api na ca srukasruva vahnayā dāvatāt paryam śruteḥ bhavet  yad kiñcit karaṇa rasya api yajña tā eva anyathā bhavet  tasmāt upāsana artham ca sva arthe tātparyavat  bhavet  iti śabda unnaye agnau  iti unnīte smṛtiḥ bhavet  iti śabda vyapetāni hi api santi vacāṃsi alam ātmānam eva ityādīni yoge agnau  api tad  samam eka vākyatva yoge tu vedasya api hi aśeṣatas  vākya bhedaḥ  na yuktaḥ syāt  yogaḥ ca syāt mahā phale iti brūyāt iti vacaḥ  gatam agnau samīpa gam kalpanā gauravam ced  syāt  pṛthak  tātparya sambhave kalpanā gauravāt eva padārthā na syuḥ eva hi pramāṇa avagata tvam ced  tātparyāṇaśaṃ tathā eva hi tasmāt  padārthe vākya arthe tātparyam ubhayatra ca pṛthak eva ca vākya tvam pṛthak anvayataḥ  bhavet  avāntara tvāt  vākyānām vākya bhedaḥ  na dūṣaṇam aṅgīkṛta tvāt api taiḥ padārthānām pṛthak  pṛthak  kriyā padena anvayasya vākya bhedāt hi dūṣaṇam pratyakṣa ādi virodhe atas  gauṇa arthasya api sambhavāt  atātparyam padārthe api na kalpyam avirodhataḥ atas  jñāna phalāni eva karmāṇi jñānam eva hi mukhya prasāda dam viṣṇoḥ jijñāsāyāḥ ca tad  bhavet  kartavyā tena jijñāsā śruti prāmāṇya yogataḥ pratyakṣavat ca prāmāṇyam svata eva āgamasya hi anavasthā anyathā hi syāt aprāmāṇyam tathā anyatas  mithyājñapti pralambha ādeḥ tena veda virodhi yad  na mānam api vedānām aṅgī kāryā hi nitya tā na hi dharma ādi siddhiḥ syāt nitya vākyam vinā kvacid  avipralambhaḥ tad jñānam tad kṛta tvāt ayaḥ  api ca kalpyā gaurava doṣeṇa puṃvākyam jñāpakam na tad  pratyakṣaḥ kasyacid  dharmaḥ  vastu tvāt iti codite na buddhaḥ  dharmadarśī syāt  puṃstvāt iti anumāhatiḥ adharma vādinaḥ  vākyam aprayojanam eva hi dharma abhāvaḥ  api naḥ tena pratyakṣa avagataḥ  bhavet  atas  saṃśaya sampattau vākyam pratyakṣavat  pramā śaktiḥ ca eva anvite sva arthe śabdānām anubhūyate atas  anvita abhidhāyi tvam gauravam kalpane anyathā naca aśakyā abhidhāyi tvam pravṛttiḥ ca dvidhā anyathā etad  sarvam tarka śāstre brahmatarke hi vistarāt  uktam vidyā pṛthaktavāt tu saṅkṣepeṇa atra sūcitam pramāṇa nyāya sa  śikṣā kriyate tarka śāstrataḥ māna nyāyaiḥ tu tad siddhaimīmāṃsā meya śodhanam brahma tarkam ca bhagavān sa eva kṛtavān prabhuḥ pañcāśat koṭi vistārāt nārāyaṇa tanau kṛtāt  uddhṛtya pañca sāhasram kṛtavān bādarāyaṇaḥ atas tad artham saṅkṣepādata iti abhyasūcayat  yatas  anubhavataḥ sarvam siddham etad atas  api ca devaiḥ ca durgama artheṣu vyāpṛtaḥ  na ati vistṛtim cakāra etā hi avajñeyā yuktayaḥ pratipakṣa gāḥ pratyakṣekṣa akṣamaḥ pakṣam kam eva atra abhivīkṣate tasmāt akṣama pakṣa tvāt mokṣa śāstre abhyupekṣitaḥ svayam bhagavatā viṣṇuḥ brahma iti etad  purā uditam sa viṣṇuḥ āha hīyante deva śāstrasya tena hi ādi antam deva śāstrasya svayam bhagavatā kṛtam madhyam tad ājñayā pailaśeṣābhyām kṛtam añjasā atas tatra eva viṣṇutva siddheḥ brahma iti asūcayat doṣa ara  chidra śabdānām paryāya tvam yatas tatas  guṇā nārā iti jñeyaḥ tadvān nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ brahma śabdaḥ  api hi guṇa pūrtim eva vadati ayam atas  nārāyaṇasya eva jijñāsā atra vidhīyate siddha tvāt  brahma śabdasya viṣṇau spaṣṭa tayā śrutau ambhasi apāra iti uktaḥ  nārāyaṇa pada īritaḥ āpaḥ  nārā iti hi āha sa eva apsu antarīritaḥ kāmataḥ  vidhi rudrā ādi pada dātṛyā svayam śriyā yoni tvena ātmanaḥ  viṣṇoḥ tiṣṭhanti iti uditasya ca yasmin devāḥ  adhi iti uktavā samudram sthānam eva ca nāma ca akṣaram iti eva ṛca iti uditam tu yad  yatas  prasūtā iti uktavā ca tad eva brahma ca abravīt  antar samudra gam viśva prasūteḥ kāraṇa ṭha tu yad  sūkta upaniṣad ādi uktam janma ādyasya iti lakṣyate sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiḥ ca saṃhāraḥ  niyatiḥ jñānam āvṛtiḥ bandha mokṣau  api hi āsu śrutiṣu uktā hareḥ sadā yam nāmāni viśanti addhā yaḥ  devānām iti hi api śruteḥ nāmāni sarvāṇi viṣṇoḥ eva yatas tatas  atas  na mukhyataḥ nāma tad anyasya hi kasyacid  guṇāḥ śrutā iti hi asmān na doṣaḥ  arthaḥ śruteḥ bhavet  prītyā mokṣa paratvāt ca tātparyam na eva dūṣaṇe sarveṣām api vākyānām mahātāt paryam atra hi tad virodhe na māna tvam phalam muktiḥ hi vākyataḥ na purāṇa ādi māna tvam viruddha arthe śruteḥ bhavet  darśana antara mūla tvāt moha artham ca ājñayā hareḥ na sarva nāma tā anyeṣām śrutau  uktā hi kutracid  adoṣa vacanāt ca eva niyamena hareḥ śrutau ajñānam pāratantryam ca praḷaye abhāva eva ca aśaktiḥ coditā ani eṣām sarveṣām api ca śrutau janma ādyasya iti tena etad  viṣṇoḥ eva sva lakṣaṇam asya udbhava ādi hetu tvam sākṣāt eva sva lakṣaṇam kṛṣṇaddhayāna  chalena eva svayam bhāgavate abravīt  atas  jīva aikyam api sa nirācakre jagadguruḥ na hi janma ādi hetu tvam jīvasya jagataḥ  bhavet  hita akriyā ādi doṣam ca vakṣyati eva svayam prabhuḥ nirguṇa tvam ca tena eva niṣiddham prabhuṇā svayam bhedena eva tu mukhya artha sambhave lakṣaṇā kutas  katham nitya guṇasya asya syāt aikyam guṇa hānataḥ sadā eva guṇavat tve asya bhinnam syāt nirguṇam sadā na ca mithyā guṇa tvam syāt anirvācyasya dūṣaṇāt  nirguṇa tvam tadā ca syāt āsura tvam naca anyathā lakṣya lakṣaṇayoḥ bhedaḥ  abhedaḥ  vā yadi vā ubhayam iti pṛṣṭe tad aikyasya gatiḥ eva na vidyate aikya abhede na śāstreṇa jñeyam tad  sva prakāśataḥ bhede mithyātvataḥ  bheda satya tvam syāt  balāt api bheda abhedau yadi tadā syāt eva hi anavasthitiḥ sva nirvāhaka tā ced  syāt  bāhyam bāhakam iti api paryāyaḥ  bhedavān vā syāt anavasthā ubhayatra ca satya jñāna ādike api eva na vyāvṛttyā prayojanam vyāvṛttasya aviśeṣa tve tad akhaṇḍam ca khaṇḍitam nirviśeṣa tvam etena mūkaḥ  aham itivat  bhavet  abhinne api viśeṣaḥ  ayam balāt āpatati hi atas  viśeṣa tadvatoḥ ca eva sva nirvāhaka tā bhavet  bheda hīne tu aparyāya śabda antara niyāmakaḥ viśeṣaḥ  nāma kathitaḥ saḥ  asti vastuṣu aśeṣatas  viśeṣāḥ te api anantāḥ ca paraspara viśeṣiṇaḥ sva nirvāhaka tā yuktāḥ santi vastuṣu aśeṣatas  atas  ananta guṇam brahma nirbhedam api bhaṇyate evam dharmān iti śrutyā tad abhedaḥ  api udīryate śaiva ādi āgama samprāpta dṛṣṭa gena phalena tu tad vākya upamayānyat ca pramāṇa tve anumīyate īśa vākya tvata iti ced  tad gavyabhicāriṇā aprāmāṇya anumā ca syāt na pṛthak  ca anumeśvare puṃstva hetu balāt eva pūrva uktena eva vartmanā śāstra yoni tvam etena kāraṇasya balāt  bhavet  na aveda vinna tarkeṇa matiḥ ityādi vākyataḥ tarkaḥ  jñāpayitum śaktaḥ  na īśitāram kathañcana vana kṛt tvā ādi rūpeṇa pakṣa bhūtasya ceśituḥ kiñcid jñānam hi puṃstvena śakyam sādhayitum sukham vṛkṣa kṛt na akhilam vṛkṣam vetti puṃstvāt hi caitravat  ityādi anumayā spardhi na anumānam pareśituḥ śaktam vijñāpane ca atiprasaṅgaḥ  anumaya īdṛśā vastu tvāt  turagaḥ śṛṅgī puṣpavat  kham sutaiḥ yutā citriṇī ca rasaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ  rasa tvāt  sa uttaraḥ  bhavet  upakrama ādi liṅgebhyaḥ  na anyāsyāt anumā tatas  ta eva anvaya nāmānaḥ taiḥ samyak  pravicārite mukhya arthaḥ  bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarva śāstrasya na aparaḥ īkṣaṇīya tvataḥ  viṣṇuḥ vācya eva naca anyathā lakṣya tvam kvāpi dṛṣṭam hi kim tad iti anavasthitiḥ mādhurya ādi viśeṣāḥ ca tad śabdaiḥ uditāḥ sadā vākya arthaḥ  api hi vākya artha śabdena eva uditaḥ  bhavet  na avācyam tena kiñcid  syāt  yata iti ādikaiḥ vadan avācya tvam katham brūyāt mūkaḥ  aham itivat  sudhīḥ yena lakṣyam iti proktam lakṣya śabdena saḥ  avadat  ekasya api hi śabdasya gauṇa artha svīkṛtau satām mahatī jāyate lajjā yatra tatra akhilā ravāḥ amukhya arthā iti vadan yaḥ tad mārga anuvartinām katham na jāyate lajjā vaktum śābda tvam ātmanaḥ ātma brahma ādayaḥ śabdāḥ sākṣāt  pūrṇa abhidhāyinaḥ janma ādi kāraṇam brahma lakṣitam ca yadā tadā vandhyā putra upamam māyā śabalam vācyam iti api kalpayitvā vinā mānam lakṣyam śuddham vadan padaiḥ ātma śabda uditasya eva jñānam muktāvasādhanam āha śruta parityāgaḥ syāt ca asya aśruta kalpanam syāt  sarvatra ca yatra ekam api lokaḥ  jugupsate niyamena ubhayam syāt hi yasya sva parayoḥ mate alaṅkṛtaḥ sadā eva ayam durghaṭaiḥ eva bhūṣaṇaiḥ andhantamaḥ  nityu duḥkham tasya syāt  vasana dvayam anandā nāma te lokā andhena tamasā avṛtāḥ tān  te pretya abhigacchanti avidvāṃsaḥ  budhaḥ janāḥ asuryā nāma te lokā andhena tamasā avṛtāḥ tān  te pretya abhigacchanti ye keca ātma hanaḥ  janāḥ ityādi śrutayaḥ  mānam śataśas  atra samantatas heyatva avacanāt ca eva na ātmā gauṇaḥ śrutau śrutaḥ tam eva ekam jānathā anyā vācaḥ  muñcatha ca iti ha ukta ātmā katham gauṇaḥ  heya pakṣe hi asau śrutaḥ parivāra tayā grāhyā api heyāḥ pradhānataḥ pūrṇasya pūrṇam ādāya pūrṇam eva avaśiṣyate iti svasya eva pūrṇasya pūrṇe api aya udāhṛtaḥ katham māyā vyavacchinnaḥ pūrṇaḥ  mukhya tayā bhavet  padam ca nirguṇa iti katham gauṇam vadiṣyati guṇa abhāva upalakṣyam ced  padam tad api vācakam atas  anavasthiti mukha sarva doṣa mahā āspadam katham etad matam sadbhiḥ ādriyeta vicakṣaṇaiḥ na ca sāṅkhayaniḥ ākṛtyai sūtrāṇi etāni acīkḷpad  bhagavān na hi aśabda tvam pradhāne aṅgīkaroti asau samanvaye pratijñāte śabda gocara tā eva hi prathama pratipādyā syāt  tad abhāve kutaḥ anvayaḥ katham ca lakṣaṇauvādī brūyāt  brahma samanvayam yaḥ  asau śabdasya mukhya arthaḥ tatra eva syāt  samanvayaḥ janma ādi kāraṇe sākṣāt āha devaḥ samanvayam uktam tad eva jijñāsyam kva avakāśaḥ  atra nirguṇe kathañca asambhavaḥ tasya mukhya arthasya nirākṛtau mānena kena vijñeyam avācyā jñeya nirguṇam ameyam ced na śāstrasya tatra vṛttiḥ kathañcana tasmāt śāstreṇa jijñāsyam asmadīyam guṇa arṇavam vāsudeva ākhyam advandvam param brahma akhila uttamam vijñeya vācya lakṣyatva pūrva aśeṣa viśeṣataḥ nirgatam manasaḥ  vācaḥ  yadi tad  syāt agocaram astu tad mā vadet  vādī naca asmad śāstra gam tu tad  avācyam vācyam iti uktavā kim iti unmattavat mṛṣā asmad śāstrasya cauryāya yatate svokti dūṣakaḥ janma ādi kāraṇam yad tad sākṣāt nārāyaṇa abhidham vadantu śrutayaḥ brahma śāstram ca etad  tad arthataḥ sva prakāśa tvam api tu yaiḥ jñānasya nivāritam katham sarvajña tā tasya sva jñāna adhigamam vinā pravṛttamastu avācyam te mā eva brūyāḥ kathañcana sarva śabdaiḥ avācyam tad uktavā tad viṣayam punar  vayam tvām śruti yuktibhyām baddhvā asmad śāstram añjasā vicārayāmaḥ śrutibhiḥ yuktibhiḥ ca eva sādaram adbhuta tvāt avācyam tad atarkya ājñeyam eva ca ananta guṇa pūrṇa tvāt iti ūde paiṅginām śrutiḥ avācyam iti loke api vaktayāḥ cāryatamam bhuvi evam śāstrau  agamya tve vibhāgena samanvayam ānanda maya ityādinā adhyāyena vadati ajaḥ tatra anyatra prasiddhānām viṣṇau  eva samanvayam śabdānām prathame pāde guṇi sāmānya vācinām guṇa vācinām ca prathamam āha devaḥ samanvayam samudra śāyinam sarva prasūti prasavam śrutiḥ tad eva brahma paramam iti sāvadhṛtiḥ jagau yatas  atas  brahma śabdasya tatra eva niyata tvataḥ yaḥ  annam brahma ityādi rūpāt abhyāsāt taittirīyake anyāsu ca etad rūpāsu śākhāsu api sahasraśas  ānanda maya ityādyaiḥ śabdaiḥ vācyaḥ  hariḥ svayam upalakṣaṇa tvam śabdānām ānanda maya pūrviṇām sūtrasya alpa akṣara tvena sarva śākhā vinirṇaye punar ca prāpakāt hetoḥ tatra adhikaraṇa antaram sarve vedā āmananti yad  padam tu iti hi śrutiḥ ānanda maya rūpe tu brahmaṇaḥ puccha tā uktitaḥ samasta abrahma tā prāpteḥ ānanda maya nāma hi brahma śabdasya ca abhyāsāt  pañca rūpa ādiṣu sphuṭam brahma tā avayave api syāt  tathā avayavini svatas  yathā eva kṛṣṇa keśasya kṛṣṇasya brahma tā akhilā darśitā ca eva pārthāya niḥsīmāḥ śaktayaḥ asya hi ṛtam satyam param brahma puruṣam kṛṣṇa piṅgalam viṣṇu ākhyam uktam anyatra hi ūrdhvaretam ca tad  prati virūpākṣa ākhyam avaram brahma uktam tad vrate sthitam samāna adhikṛta tvam ced uttaram nīlalohitam kṛṣṇa piṅgala rūpeṇa punaruktam bhaviṣyati brahma adhipatiḥ iti atra tāpanīya śrutau puras  svarita brahma śabda antam bahuvrīhi tvam eṣyati svāhā indra śatru vardhasva yad  bahu vrīhitām agāt  mahāvyākaraṇe sūtram iti svara vinirṇaye pūrva anta svarite puṃsoḥ bahuvrīhitvam eṣyati mahāvyākaraṇe sūtram iti svara vinirṇaye ṛtam satyam param brahma ityādi uddeśya dvitīyakā vibhaktiḥ ūrdhvareta ādiḥ prathamā rudra gocarā tasmāt  viṣṇum param brahma prati rudraḥ  vrate sthitaḥ ūrdhvaretāḥ  iti hi eva śruti arthaḥ  avasitaḥ  bhavet  ṛtam satyam param brahma prati viṣṇum sadāśivaḥ ūrdhvaretāḥ  dhyāyati ha śaṅkaraḥ  nīlalohitaḥ iti artham etam eva āha nīlagrīva śrutiḥ parā ārtharvaṇī param brahma tasmāt ekaḥ hariḥ śrutau tad eva ṛtam iti prāha katham eva anyathā śrutiḥ avadhārayantī tasya eva hi ṛtatva ādikam añjasā ekaḥ  nārāyaṇa āsīt na brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ vāsudevaḥ  agra eva āsīt na brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ na indra sūryau na ca guhaḥ na somaḥ  na vināyakaḥ ityādi vākyataḥ  viṣṇoḥ utpattiḥ avatāra gā mukhyam brahma hariḥ tasmāt  prastāvaḥ param iti api mukhya brahma grahe yukte na amukhyam yujyate kvacid  asambhave hi mukhyasya gauṇa artha aṅgīkṛtiḥ bhavet  prācurya arthāḥ ca mayaṭaḥ sarve atra pratipāditāḥ bhogya tvam atra ca adya tvam upajīvyatayā hareḥ mahābhoktā mahā bhogya iti arthaḥ  anna maye bhavet  mahā prāṇaḥ  mahā bodhaḥ mahā vijñānavān api viśeṣa sāmānyatayā vijñānam mana iti api ekasya jñāna rūpasya hareḥ uktiḥ vibhāgataḥ abhede api viśeṣeṇa eva anya iti uditaḥ  hariḥ bheda śabdā viśeṣam tu harau  anyatra bhinna tvāt  brūyuḥ hareḥ jīva jaḍaiḥ api bhedam hi mukhyatas  brahma tarkavacaḥ  api evam ata ekaḥ sa pañcadhā uktaḥ  anna maya ityādi bhṛgoḥ ca etad  vadiṣyati prāpya tvena mayaṭprokteḥ na tatra api anyat ucyate pracura at na ādiḥ eva atas  hi annam at namayā iti api ucyate hi aviśeṣeṇa na anyat  kiñcid iha ucyate mahā ānandatva eva asya hetuḥ kaḥ  anyāt iti sphuṭam uktaḥ śruti antare yasmāt  sukham labdhvā karoti ayam karoti na asukhī bhūmā sukham na alpe sukham bhavet  iti uktam yad  pravṛttiḥ ca nṛtta gāna ādikā sukhāt  duḥkhāt  rodādikā ca eva sarva kartṛ tvatas  asya ca sarva śakteḥ  na duḥkham syāt atas  kevala līlayā pravartakaḥ  na ced eṣa prāṇyāt anyāt ca kaḥ pumān brahma vid  param āpnoti iti yad  prathama sūcitam tad eva mantra varṇena satyam jñānam anantavat lakṣitam tatra satya tvam sṛṣṭayā anna prāṇayoḥ api uktam jñānam tu manasā vijñānena api udīritam ananta tvam tathā ananda maya vācā api udāhṛtam sadbhāvam yāpayet  yasmāt  satyam tad  tena kathyate iti sṛṣṭiḥ iha proktā jagat sadbhāvayāpakam brahma iti sthāpanāya eva sattvam jīvanam eva ca viśīrṇa tā ca sattvam syāt  sannam iti āhuḥ eva yad  atas  adyatāt tṛta anna tvam satya śabda artha eva hi prāṇam devāḥ  anuprāṇanti manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ ca ye āyuḥ prāṇaḥ  hi bhūtānām iti yad  gati jīvane ukte saditi dhātu arthaḥ  gatiḥ ca atas  hi satyatā prāṇa tvam avabodha arthaḥ  manudhātuḥ prakīrtitaḥ na alpe sukham iti proktayā eva ānanda maya tā uktitaḥ ananta tvam sunirṇītam pūrṇa ānandaḥ  hi na alpake atas  hi mantra varṇa ukta vistṛtiḥ tu samastayā kriyate parayā yasmāt itaraḥ  atra na kathyate puruṣam vetti yaḥ  mucyet na anyaḥ panthā hi vidyate iti śruteḥ anyavedī katham muktim prayāsyati puruṣaḥ para ātmā ajaḥ  brahma nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ mahān ānanda ud viṣṇuḥ bharga oma iti īryate svayam nārāyaṇaḥ  devaḥ  na anyasya etāni kasyacid  tasmāt om iti udāhṛtya yajña dāna ādi kurvate sūktena pauruṣeṇa enam yajanti adhyātma kovidāḥ iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ tena na anya jñānāt  vimucyate brahma śabda udite tasmin  ātma śabdam prayujya ca tasmāt ākāśa sṛṣṭim ca provāca atra catuvirdhām bhūtam bhūta abhimānī ca tad dehaḥ  antar niyāmakaḥ hariḥ ca ākāśa śabda uktaḥ  mukhyataḥ hariḥ eva ca ā samantāt  kāśate yad ākāśaḥ  mukhyataḥ hariḥ bala jñāna svarūpa tvāt  vāyuḥ agniḥ agam nayan āpa āpālanāt ca eva pṛthivī prathitaḥ  yatas  uṣyānām āśraya tvena sa eva ūṣadhi nāmakaḥ oṣadhīṣu sthitaḥ  viṣṇuḥ kṣudhitaiḥ āśritaḥ  bhavet  puri śete yatas  saḥ  atha puruṣaḥ ca iti gīyate kriyā pravartaka tvena prādurbhāvaḥ  hareḥ janiḥ ākāśa ādiṣu na anyā asti hi abhimānaḥ  abhimāninaḥ abhimāni śarīrasya sākṣāt  bhūtasya ca udbhavaḥ evam deha ādi paryantam āgatam harim eva tu parāmṛśati tasya eva pañca rūpatva vittaye tyaktavā bhūta ādikam sarvam sa vā eṣa iti śrutiḥ sa iti ātma pada uddiṣṭa eṣa jīva śarīra gaḥ sārāt namaya eva ayam na loka anna mayaḥ prabhuḥ iti tam rasa śabdena viśinaṣṭi śarīra gam idam iti eva nirdeśaḥ  vastra prāvṛtavat  vibhoḥ śira ādeḥ bhavet jīvaśira ādau vyavasthiteḥ tam viditvā asya muktiḥ syāt na anya jñānāt kathañcana āditye puruṣe ca ayam iti bheda upadeśataḥ na asya abhedaḥ  asti jīvena na anumā kāma cāriṇī vimatāni śarīrāṇi mad bhoga āyatanāni yad  śarīrāṇi iti ādikā tu tattva jñāne hi apekṣyate pratyakṣa ādi viruddha tvāt akṣa āgama bhaya ujkhitā anumā kāma vṛttā hi kutra na avasaram vrajet  jaḍa ātmā eva vastu tvāt  prameya tvāt jaḍam citiḥ ghana ākāśa ityādyā vāryante kena hetunā na jīva bheda sūtrāṇām śaṅkayā atra punarukta tā vākya antara dyotaka tvāt  pṛthak iti atra pūrṇa tā yogam annamaya ādyaiḥ yad  phalatvena asya śaṃsati sthāna dvaye api atas  kośā eta iti ati sāhasam upasaṅkramaṇam ca eva dvitīya uddeśitam prati atikramam vadantam tam upaśabdaḥ  nivārayet  aśrutasya ati śabdasya sthānam dadyāt  katham punar  śruta aśruta parityāga kalpane vigata hriyām mṛtau  eva parityāgaḥ kṛtaḥ  hi anna mayasya ca ye annam brahma ityādi upāsām sāmāna adhikaraṇyataḥ uktavā pañca svarūpāṇām punar tad prāpti vādinī sthāna dvaya gatā vedavāṇī tad apalāpinām tamasaḥ  anyatra saṃsthānam katham eva saheta sā adhīhi bhagavaḥ  brahma iti uktaḥ  anna prāṇa pūrvakam āha brahma katham tad na dvāram tad iti vādinaḥ upasattim katham vidyuḥ upasannāya hi triśas  vaktavyam brahma guruṇā catur vāram atha api vā sakṛt  vā iti āgamā brūyuḥ sampradāya vidaḥ  api ca tad  yad kiñcit katham brūyāt upasannāya dikpatiḥ na vadet  brahma ca katham māyāvī na hi vārirāj  caṣṭa iti eva tad cakṣuḥ śravaṇāt śrotram ucyate vacanāt eva vāc  brahma sṛṣṭi sthiti ādi kāraṇam tad ca vāghūla śākhāyām aṣṭa rūpam udāhṛtam vijñāna ānanda sahitam pṛthak  sṛṣṭayā ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ āvāpa udvāpa taṣa śākhā yata āhuḥ param padam yatas  bhūtāni jāyanta ityādyaiḥ lakṣaṇaiḥ svayam lakṣitam guruṇā paścāt  tapasā eva aparokṣataḥ dṛṣṭvā ekaikam svarūpam tu samasta ukta anudarśanam icchatā ajñām guroḥ prāpya tapasā evāra ukṣitam abrahma iti eva vadatām śruta hānyaśruta grahau sākṣāt lakṣaṇa tām prāptau  iti lajjā tad uktiṣu samīpe saha bhogasya mukti tvena uktitaḥ  asakṛt  bhedaḥ  jīveśayoḥ mithyā iti eva mithyā svayam bhavet  etena mayaṭaḥ ca eva dvaividhyena artha kalpanāt  tad anyeṣām matam api sat saṃsatsu na bhāsate atas  nārāyaṇaḥ  devaḥ  niḥśeṣa guṇa vācakaiḥ guṇi sāmānya vacanaiḥ api mukhya tayā uditaḥ adhyātma gaiḥ ca prāṇa ādyaiḥ tathā eva hi adhibhūta gaiḥ anna ādi śabdaiḥ bhagavān ekaḥ  mukhya tayā uditaḥ janma ādyasya iti sūtreṇa guṇa sarva sva siddhaye brahmaṇaḥ  lakṣaṇam proktam śāstra mūlam yatas tatas  anvayaḥ sarva śabdānām guṇa sarva sva vedakaḥ śabda pravṛtti hetūnām tasmin mukhya samanvayāt  anya artheṣu alpatā hetoḥ tad nimitta tvataḥ tathā tad vācaka tvam śabdānām bahula ati prayogataḥ rūḍham iti eva sādhyam syāt  rūḍhiḥ hi dvividhā matā avidvat vidvat āptyā eva mukhyā hi viduṣām tu sā vidvat rūḍhiḥ vaidikā syāt  sā yogāt eva labhyate tasmāt mukhyā artha tā viṣṇoḥ iti kṛtvā hṛdi prabhuḥ samanvayam sādhayati devānām tatra śakta tām āśaṅkaya tatra rūḍhim ca tad śabdānām api svayam samudra anta sthitatva ādyaiḥ tad dharmaiḥ viṣṇu rūḍha tām sādhayitvā abhidām taiḥ ca punar eva nyavārayat  ceṣṭā hi cetanānām yā sā bhavet  tad prasādataḥ acetana svabhāvaḥ tu vivara ādiḥ katham tatas  iti śaṅkā nivṛtti artham ākāśa iti nāma ca paratas  api varīyaḥ tu apūrvāt liṅgāt hareḥ bhavet  iti śaṅkā nivṛtti artham ākāśa iti nāma ca paratas  api varīyaḥ tu pūrvāt liṅgāt hareḥ bhavet  prāṇa ādi hetuta adṛṣṭeḥ ati deśaḥ  hi tādṛśaḥ liṅgam balavat eva syāt  prerakaḥ  asya api yad hariḥ nitya tvāt eva śabdasya tad svabhāvaḥ katham hareḥ katham prasiddha bahula śabdānām ayathārtha tā iti ced  tad hareḥ eva bāhulyāt śruti liṅgayoḥ tādṛśa tvāt ca tad śakteḥ bāhulye śruti liṅgayoḥ anyasya mukhya vācya tvam iti tad na atra gasya hi viṣṇoḥ eva tu liṅgāni prāṇa sthāni tu sarvaśas  prāṇa saṃvāda pūrvāṇi mukhyataḥ jīvagāni ca abhyārcat śata varṣāṇi prāṇa vaṃśa tvam iti api tasmāt anyatragaiḥ śabdaiḥ ukta nyāyaiḥ samantatas ekaḥ  nārāyaṇaḥ  devaḥ  bhaṇyate na atra saṃśayaḥ vāsudeva ādi rūpeṇa catur mūrtiḥ ca sarvaśas  athavā pañcamūrtiḥ sa proktaḥ  adhikaraṇam prati pratisūtram pratipadam pratyakṣaram atha api vā taiḥ taiḥ yukti śruti nyāya viśeṣaiḥ yogya tā yathā bṛhat tantra pramāṇena bahu artham api saṅgrahāt  ucyate nara buddhīnām api kiñcid graha arthataḥ granthaḥ  ayam api bahu arthaḥ  bhāṣyam ca atyartha vistaram bahu jñā eva jānanti viśeṣaṇa artham etayoḥ tasmāt mahā guṇa u viṣṇuḥ nāmnā āya punaruktitaḥ liṅga ātmakānām śabdānām vṛttiḥ nārāyaṇe pare cintyate sarvaga tvam tu prathamam pravicāryate tatra tatra sthitaḥ  viṣṇuḥ tad tad śakti prabodhakaḥ dūratas  api atiriktaḥ sa līlayā kevalam prabhuḥ iti jñāpayitum karma kartroḥ utsarga taḥ  bhidā abhedaḥ  api viśeṣe syāt  balī saḥ  api anapoditaḥ etad  bhāva abhidham liṅgam kriyā liṅge tatas  param antaryāmī antaraḥ ca iti kriyā bhāva ākhyam ucyate adṛśyatva ādi abhāva ākhyam śrutiḥ liṅga adhikā parā anitya tvāt  kriyāṇām tu katham eva svarūpa tā iti ced  sa viśeṣaḥ  api kriyā śaktayā ātmanā sthiraḥ śakti tā vyakta tā ca iti viśeṣaḥ  api viśeṣavān abhinnaḥ api kriyā ādiḥ ca svabhāva iti hi śrutiḥ jñānam nityam kriyā nityā balam śaktiḥ para ātmanaḥ iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ ca āha śakti sadbhāva eva tu kriyā ādi nitya tā jñeyā tad anyatra tu anitya tā iti sat tattva vacanam dvi tvam ca ekasya yujyate yaḥ setuḥ iti ca ekatva vacanena viśeṣaṇāt  antar  sthitvā ramaṇa kṛt antaraḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ramaṇam ca ātma śabdena ādeyam māti iti ca ucyate viśiṣṭa sukhavat tvāt ca brahma tvam ca viśiṣṭa tā anyonya niyatiḥ ca īśa ni yame na anyathā bhavet  cetanānām viśeṣaḥ  yaḥ svabhāvaḥ  api īśvara apirtaḥ anyonya niyame tasmāt anavasthiti asambhavau īśvaraḥ ced niyantā ca sa eva prathama āgataḥ kim iti apodyate kasmāt  vṛthā avasthiti kalpanā doṣavatī eva tasmāt  sā na eva kāryā kathañcana ramaṇam na ati yatnasya vikṣepāt eva yujyate iti ced  sarva niyamaḥ  yasya kasmāt na śakyate ātmanā aniyatam vastu pratīpam hi ātmanaḥ  bhavet  svādhīna sattā śaktayā ādi katham ātma pratīpakam guṇa kriyā dayaḥ  bhāvā yad ivā syuḥ abhedinaḥ abhedaḥ  abhāva dharmāṇām brahmaṇā yujyate katham na abhāvaḥ  bhāva iti ca viśeṣaḥ prāyaśas  bhavet  atadbhāvaḥ  anya tā ca iti na viśeṣaḥ  asti kaścana doṣa abhāvaḥ  guṇa iti prasiddhaḥ  laukikeṣu api adṛśyatva ādikān  tasmāt  guṇān āha svayam prabhuḥ bhāva abhāva virodhaḥ  api na tu sarvatra vidyate tad abhāvaḥ  hi tad bhāva virodhī na tatas  aparaḥ pṛthaktava abhāva tad rūpān bhedān  trīn kalpayanti ced  kalpanā gaurava ādyāḥ tu doṣāḥ tatra virodhinaḥ pṛthak tava anyatva bhedāḥ tu paryāyeṇa eva laukikaiḥ vyavahriyante satatam vaidikaiḥ api sarvaśas  dṛṣṭa hāniḥ adṛṣṭasya kalpanā iti eva dūṣaṇam yadā tad adhikaḥ  doṣaḥ  vidyate kaḥ  nu vādinām bhāva abhāva svarūpāḥ tu viśeṣā eva vastunaḥ abhinnā eva saṅgrāhyā vyavahāra prasiddhaye yathā ekaḥ samavāyaḥ  api bheda abhedau ca vastuni aṅgīkāryā viśeṣeṇa sthāneṣu vyavahartṛbhiḥ akhaṇḍa vādinaḥ pi syāt viśeṣaḥ  anicchataḥ  api asau vyāvṛtte nirviśeṣe tu kim vyāvartyabahutvataḥ bahu liṅga samāyuktaiḥ bahubhī rūḍha nāmabhiḥ prasiddhaiḥ anya ga tvena vācyaḥ sākṣāt janārdanaḥ vaiśvānara ādayaḥ śabdā api tad vācinaḥ tatas  tāni liṅgāni te śabdā api tad gā hi sarvaśas  bahulāpyajña rūḍhiḥ tad prajñā ārūḍhim na bādhate tatra anyatra ca siddhānām liṅganāmnām punar hariḥ viśeṣāt mukhya taḥ vṛttim svasmin  eva atra vaktaya jaḥ viṣṇau  eva ātma śabdasya rūḍha tvāt na śiva ādikān śrutiḥ vakti akhila īśa tvāt  bhūmā viṣṇuḥ sukha adhikaḥ atas  viruddhavat  bhātam api vyākhyāya tattvataḥ yojanīyam harau vākyam viruddhaiḥ lakṣaṇaiḥ yutam brahmā eva tāni liṅgāni tad anyatra tvasanti api avirodhena govinde santi asthūla ādikāni ca anya vastu svabhāvānām sthaulya ādīnām apākṛtim nārāyaṇe śrutiḥ vakti na tu tasya asvabhāva tām sarva dharmā sarva nāmā sarva karmā guṇāḥ śrutāḥ doṣāḥ śrutāḥ ca na ityādyā pramāṇam śrutiḥ atra ca liṅgam sādhāraṇam śabdau sthānam liṅgam anugrahaḥ punar  śabdā liṅga śabdau vicāryā dvi sthitā iha bāhulyam liṅga śabdānām anuktiḥ ca viruddha tā adṛṣṭiḥ anvaya abhāvaḥ  viparīta śruti bhramaḥ liṅga avakāśarāhiti bhramaḥ tādṛś  dvayam tathā bahu tādṛktavam uktasya virodhaḥ  arthāt  tathā gatiḥ samastam etad iti atra pūrva pakṣeṣu yuktayaḥ tā eva balavantaḥ tu gati antara vivarjitāḥ siddhānta yuktayaḥ jñeyā dṛśyante tāḥ ca sarvaśas  mukta upasṛpyatā prāṇāt ādhikyam sarvatas tathā vailakṣaṇyam svabhāvasya prekṣā pūrva kriyā tathā arasya ṇyasya ca īśa tvam sūrya ādi anukṛtiḥ tathā vāmana ākhyā sarva kampaḥ tad śabda an anya siddha tā anāma rūpa tā bhedasya upajīvya pramāṇa tā sarva aiśvarya ādika ādyāḥ tā veda īśena pradarśitāḥ adhikāraḥ ca tad hāniḥ prasaṅgāt eva cintitau tad phalāya vidhiḥ siddhe ca upāsāyā nirākṛtaḥ yatas  jaimininā anya artham asiddhe arthe vidhiḥ tathā vidyā adhirājasya matam avirodhaḥ tayoḥ tatas  mokṣe phala viśeṣaḥ  asti na ca sarvam prakāśate sarvadā tena devānām api yuktā hi upāsanā nityam vṛddhi kṣaya apetam viṣṇoḥ pūrṇam tu vedanam spaṣṭa ati spaṣṭa viśadam brahmaṇaḥ  aśeṣa vastu gam anyeṣām kramaśas  jñānam mita vastu gatam sadā ityādayaḥ  viśeṣāḥ tu sadā vidyā pateḥ hṛdi jaimini ādyāḥ tu sāmānya vettṛ tvāt tad  tathā avadan vidyeśa matam etasmāt na eva sadbhiḥ viruddhayate duḥkhi baddha avarā ādyāḥ tu tad adhīnatva hetutaḥ śabdā brahmaṇi vartante rājñi yadvat  parājayaḥ svātantryam tad gata tvam ca śabda vṛtteḥ hi kāraṇam svātantryam tatra mukhyam syāt  kutaḥ rājñi jayaḥ  anyathā na hi bhṛtyasya vijayi śabdaḥ tāvat  prayujyate yāvat  rājñi anya ga tve api svātantrya ābhāsa mātrataḥ bhṛtya bandha ādikam rājñi rājñaḥ  bandha ādi yogyataḥ kāraṇam saṃśayasya syāt iti na eva prayujyate amaṅgala tvāt śabdānām rājñā yogāt amaṅgale apriya tvāt tu śabdasya syāt  prayoga nivartanam guṇāḥ tu tādṛśā yatra prayujyante akhilā api pūjyeṣu eva viśeṣeṇa svātantryam mukhya kāraṇam tatas  doṣa atidūra tvāt saṃśayasya api asambhavāt  doṣāṇām viṣṇu ga tvasya prājña buddhi vyapekṣayā svātantrya artham abhipretya doṣa śabdāḥ ca viṣṇavi vāsudeva śrutiḥ ca āha na eva viṣṇau  amaṅgalam maṅgala amaṅgale anyatra tatas  na amaṅgalam vadet  svātantrya apekṣayā viṣṇau doṣaḥ  na amaṅgala uktitaḥ bahu bhuktavam yathā doṣaḥ  nṛṣu na eva harau kvacid  evam duḥkhya ādi śabdāḥ ca svātantrya apekṣayā uditāḥ na eva doṣā harau tad gabuddhayā uktā doṣa kāriṇaḥ tasmāt  te doṣa śabdāḥ ca tatra eva guṇavācakāḥ jāta motam harau yasmāt jyotiḥ ṣaḥ prāṇa rūpataḥ āyajñetas ca ayajeta u vasantiḥ ca vasantatas vigata  chādana tvāt  tu gaccha bhūta kṣayaṅkaraḥ bhuṅkṣā iti uktaḥ  hariḥ  hum ca hutam asmin jagad yatas  sphuṭa tvāt  phaṭ iti proktaḥ kava rakṣaṇa iti atas  kavacam vata ṛte yasmāt  ṣaḍguṇa tvena sarvadā vaṣaṭ  tad gatvataḥ teṣām vauṣaṭ iti iva kathyate svīyam svīkurute yasmāt  svāhā iti uktaḥ  janārdanaḥ namanti asmin guṇā yasya annama iti eva kathyate iti aśeṣa kriyā nāma śabdaiḥ ekaḥ  janārdanaḥ ucyate mukhyataḥ yasmāt  pada varṇa svara ādibhiḥ tasmāt ananta guṇa tā śruti tāt paryataḥ asya hi vijñāna artha tvataḥ sarva śabdānām na asti dūṣaṇam aṅgīkṛte api na eva asti doṣaḥ  vākya samanvaye tad artha tvena karma ādeḥ sambhavāt alpabuddhaye kaḥ chandasām yogam iti śruteḥ yoga artha tattva vid  brahmā ekaḥ  na eva ca anyaḥ  asti ka iti asyara ubhaya arthataḥ tasya api pūrva siddhasya jñānam eva iti niścayāt  nitya yogaḥ  api śabdānām arthaiḥ na eva niṣiddhayate strī śabdāḥ ca niṣedha arthāḥ sarve api brahma vācakāḥ virodhi sarva bāhulya kāraṇa strī niṣedhinām pṛthak  samanvaya arthāni sthānāni etāni sarvaśas  sarva mānaiḥ virodhaḥ ca vyutpatteḥ api aśakyatā paraspara virodhaḥ ca virodhaḥ kārya tadvatoḥ strī liṅga tvam niṣedhaḥ ca pūrva pakṣeṣu hetavaḥ doṣāti aspṛṣṭi niyamaḥ śabda artha aneka tā tathā bahu rūpa tvam īśasya vyaktaya vyakti viśeṣi tā utpādanam sva dehāt ca durjana avyakta tā tathā itayā ādyā yuktayaḥ sākṣāt  siddhānta sthāpakā iha anvayaḥ sarva śabdānām aśakyaḥ  jñātum añjasā iti yad loka vaimukhyam jaiminī ādi matam vadan vidyā adhināthaḥ bhagavān apācakre svayam prabhuḥ sva śiṣyāṇām prasiddhayartham matam ātmīyam aṃśataḥ vijñātam taiḥ jagāda atra tāratamyam nṛṇām vadan teṣu teṣu padārtheṣu rūḍhiḥ aṅgīkṛtā yatas  prayojana bahutvena tasya tasya avirodhataḥ upadeśa ādi sāmarthyāt  viṣṇau śaktiḥ ca gṛhyate tathā api etad virodhe tu tad vāci tvam apodyate avirodhe tu bahu arthā etad mūla tayā matāḥ itas  hi rūḍha tā anyeṣām upajīvya tvam atra hi tad siddhiḥ tad apekṣā ca sa apekṣā ca hari icchayā tasmāt  parama mukhya tvam viṣṇau  anyatra mukhya tā upalakṣaṇā ca gauṇī ca tisraḥ śabdasya vṛttayaḥ pravṛtti hetoḥ bāhulyam jñeyam parama mukhya tā tatra prayoga bāhulyam yadi tatpara tā kim u ubhayam dṛśyate viṣṇau śabdānām api sarvaśas  prayoga mātra bāhulyam rūḍhiḥ iti abhidhīyate prayoga yukta sādṛśyam sambandhaḥ  vāpi amukhyataḥ vṛtti hetuḥ iti jñeyaḥ pūrva ayoge para grahaḥ etam eva tathā santam śataṛcī iti ādi nāmabhiḥ ācakṣata iti hi atra santam iti avadhāraṇā yogasya rūḍheḥ prābalyam vidvat rūḍhim ca tatragām bahuśas  darśayati añjaḥ tāt paryāt  sa niruktikam iti brahma kathitam tadvaya ākhyānāt matā tathā śabdānām api sarveṣām nāma vid kṛta kṛtya tā viṣṇu nāma artha rūpa tvam saṃhitā ādeḥ athā bravīt ṇakāram ca ṣakāram ca bala ceṣṭā ātmakam vadan tad jñāna pūrvaka tvena saṃhitā adhyayanam tathā upasarga tvataḥ  vestu tāt śīlya arthādunaḥ tathā ṇakāraḥ ca ṣakāraḥ ca nāma rūpa tayā matau tasmāt  samanvayaḥ  viṣṇau svara varṇa pada ātmanaḥ api vedasya kim uta vākya rūpeṇa saṅgatiḥ ghoṣāḥ sarve api vedāḥ ca sarve vedāḥ ca yad  padam indram mitram yam indram ca prathamaḥ saṅkṛtiḥ tathā nāmadhāḥ sarva devānām eka iti ādikā śrutiḥ pramāṇa mukta viṣaye tad eva uktam upakramāt  iti svayam bhagavatā bruvata aśeṣam anvayam na śabda vācya taiva atra pradhanasya niṣiddhayate sarva veda itihāseṣu purāṇeṣu ca saṅgrahāt  sattvam rajaḥ tama iti guṇāḥ prakṛti sambhavāḥ nibadhnanti mahā bāhaḥ dehe dehinam avyayam ityādi vākya rūpeṇa yatra arthaḥ  na anya iṣyate tejaḥ  abanna ātmakam vā api yadi upādānam iṣyate anādi eva aparādhaḥ kaḥ pradhānam iti codite ajām ekām iti prāha śrutiḥ etām yadā tadā kaḥ  doṣaḥ sarvathā eva asti pariṇāmi jaḍam yadi asmākam parama mukhya arthaḥ  bhagavān eka eva tu mukhya mātra tayā rūḍham sarvam abhyupagamyate sarveṣām api śabdānām gauṇya ādyam tad ayogataḥ artha dvayam abhipretya pravṛtte hariḥ uktavān kāryāṇām kāraṇam pūrvam vacasām vācyam uttamam yogānām paramām siddhim paramam te padam viduḥ iti buddhau samārohāt ubhayoḥ yoga rūḍhayoḥ tyāge ca kāraṇa abhāvāt ubhaya artha tvam iṣyate viparīta pramābhāve pūrva ārohaḥ tu kāraṇam sā bhavet  yatra sa vyarthaḥ pūrva ārohaḥ  bhramaḥ  yathā atas  jagat upādānam pradhānam vakti sā śrutiḥ yad tad triguṇam avyaktam nityam sat asat ātmakam pradhānam prakṛtim prāhuḥ aviśeṣam viśeṣavat  pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ brahma caturbhiḥ daśabhiḥ tathā etad caturviṃśatikam gaṇam prādhānikam viduḥ iti bhāgavate prāha vidyā adhīśaḥ svayam prabhuḥ na ca prakṛti śabdena brahma upādānam ucyate avikāraḥ sadā śuddhaḥ  nitya ātmā sadā hariḥ sadā eka rūpa vijñāna bala ānanda rūpakaḥ nirvikāraḥ  akṣaraḥ śuddhaḥ  nirātaṅkaḥ  ajaraḥ  amaraḥ aviśvaḥ viśvakartā ajaḥ  yaḥ paraḥ saḥ  abhidhīyate nirvikāram anaupamyam sadā ekarasam akṣayam brahma iti paramātmā iti yam viduḥ vaidikā janāḥ iti śruti purāṇa uktayā na vikārī janārdanaḥ para adhīna viśeṣa āptiḥ anivartyā anyathā bhavaḥ kṣīra ādivat  vikāraḥ syāt na eva sa syāt hareḥ kvacid  apādāna tvam eva asya yadi upādānatā iṣyate aṅgīkṛtam tad  pitṛvat natu viśva ātmanā bhavaḥ na ca ūrṇa nābhi janitṛ mātṛṇām ca vikāritā cetana tvāt  tad annam hi kārya rūpa tayā bhavet  apādāna tayā viśvakartṛ tvam buddhi pūrvakam uktam bhālla viśākhāyām brahmatarke ca sādaram icchā mātrāt prabhoḥ sṛṣṭiḥ avikārasya sarvadā svabhāvaḥ  ayam anantasya rajaḥ  yena abhavat jagat  sva dehāt icchayā viśvam bhukta pūrvam janārdanaḥ sasarja mātā pitṛvat ūrṇa nābhivat eva vā pradhānam pariṇāmyeśaḥ  nirvikāraḥ svayam sadā na cetana vikāraḥ syāt  yatra kvāpi hi acetanam na acetana vikāraḥ  api cetanaḥ syāt  kadācana na ca anyasya anya rūpa tvam vikṛta tve api dṛśyate na kṣīrāt anya tā dadhnaḥ kenacid  dṛśyate kvacid  sarva jñād brahmaṇaḥ  anya tvam jagataḥ  hi anubhūyate abhedaḥ sattva mātreṇa syāt  kharva svaṇayoḥ api bhāgena pariṇāmaḥ ced  bhāgayoḥ bheda eva hi yaḥ  bhāgaḥ  na vikārī syāt  sa eva asmākam īśvaraḥ bhinnānām samudāyasya nāma brahma iti ced  bhavet  brahma upādāna tā na syāt  tadā viśvasya hi kvacid  śṛṅgāt śaraḥ avilom abhyaḥ  dūrvā gomayataḥ tathā vṛścikaḥ ca iti evamādyeṣu apādāna tvam iṣyate upādāna eka deśa tvam yadi api atra pradṛśyate api apādāna tā eva atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  bhavet  na hi  upādāna tā eva atra bāhya avayava gauravāt na ca acetanatas tatra cetanasya samudbhavaḥ upādāna tayā kintarhi apādānam hi acetanam kārya deha gatasya asya cetanasya pradṛśyate sat ca tyat ca abhavat iti na asya viśva tvam ucyate tad  sṛṣṭvā iti girā eva asya pūrvam viśvasya siddhitaḥ sattvāt  tateḥ vaidika tvāt  samyak  vaktum aśakyatas  āśraya tvāt  sva āśraya tvāt jñāna tvāt  durvida tvataḥ sat tateḥ yātanāt ca eva hi aprāpta tvāt ca durjanaiḥ nitya asādhu guṇa vyāpti yantṛ rūpa tvataḥ sadā jagat gatena rūpeṇa brahmā eva hi tathā ucyate vyaktiḥ ukta guṇānām hi puruṣa apekṣayā nṛṇām bhavet abhavat ityādyaḥ prayogaḥ ca atra yujyate tasmāt aśeṣa kartā ekaḥ  nirvikāraḥ  ramāpatiḥ śabdaiḥ prakṛtiḥ ityādyaiḥ strī liṅgaiḥ abhidhīyate bahu syām iti tasya eva hi ukta mārgeṇa yujyate tad tad gatena rūpeṇa tad artham hi asṛjat jagat  yad ca avikṛtam eva etad  brahma viśva ātmanā mṛṣā dṛśyate manda dṛṣṭayā eva sa sarga iti kathyate sā manda dṛṣṭiḥ tasya eva brahmaṇaḥ kim tatas  anya gā brahmaṇaḥ ced  kva sārvajñyam anya gā ced  svatas  anya tā na adeha yoginaḥ  dṛṣṭiḥ iti tad  kāraṇam svatas  dehinaḥ kāraṇa yutā dehāḥ ca yadi na bhramāt  kim bhrānti kalpitam tatra bhedaḥ  api bhrama jaḥ  yadi bhrānteḥ ajñāna mūla tvāt tasya bheda vyapekṣayā na ajñāna kalpakam kiñcid anyonya āśraya tā yatas  bhrama tve tu iyamuktiḥ ca tad antar patanāt na hi vyāvahārika tā ca asya syāt abādhyatva eva hi bādhyam na artha kriyā kāri na ca svapnaḥ  api naḥ mṛṣā vāsanā janita tvena tasya api aṅgīkṛta tvataḥ sa hi kartā iti vākyāt ca jāgrat tvam iti hi bhramaḥ sarpa bhrama ādau  api hi jñānam asti eva tādṛśam tad eva artha kriyā kāri tad  sa deva artha kārakam brahma tu artha kriyā kāri paratas  svata eva vā aṅgīkṛtam hi tena eva paratas tve na ca pramā amukhya satya mānasya sādhaka tve sadā avayoḥ na hi sampratipattiḥ syāt atas tiṣṭhatu sā pramā na hi vipratipannena śakyam sādhayitum kvacid  sādhaka tvam tu satyasya sākṣiṇaḥ  hi āvayoḥ dvayoḥ samyak  sampratipannam tad na vivatarma matam bhavet  yadi na aṅgīkṛtam kiñcid anaṅgīkṛta tā api hi na aṅgīkṛtā iti mūkaḥ syāt iti na asmad vivādi tā viśvam satyam yad ciketa praghānvasya yathārthataḥ ityādi śrutayaḥ sarvā viśvasatyatva vācakāḥ satya tvam gagana ādeḥ ca sākṣi pratyakṣa sādhitam sākṣi siddhasya na kvāpi bādhya tvam tad adoṣataḥ sa varkāleṣu abādhya tvam sākṣiṇā eva pratīyate kālaḥ  hi sākṣi pratyakṣaḥ suṣuptau ca pratītitaḥ atīta anāgatau kālau  api nāsā akṣi gocarau pakṣīkartum aśakyatvāt na anumā tatra vartate tad etad iti sarvam ca dṛśyam vā smṛti gocaram sākṣi siddhena kālena kha citam hi eva vartate tasmāt na tam vinā kiñcid  smartum draṣṭum atha api vā śakyam tad nitya siddheḥ hi na anumāvasaraḥ  bhavet  atas  adoṣa pratītasya satya tvam sākṣiṇā matam parīkṣā ādeḥ ca satya tvam tena hi eva matam bhavet  anyathā śruti yuktayā ādi pramāṇaiḥ ca saha eva tu akasmāt  vinivṛttiḥ ca kim viśvasya na śaṅkayate itas  pūrvam tathā abhāvāt  yadi naḥ saṃsṛteḥ gatiḥ vākyānumāditaḥ ced  syāt  tad prāmāṇyam ca sākṣitaḥ tad prāmāṇyam yathā sākṣī sthāpayati evam eva hi sarva kāleṣu api sthairyāt  vyabhicāram apohya ca evam akṣajamānatva siddhām viśvasya satya tām kim iti sthāpayet na ayam nirdoṣa jñāna śaktitaḥ eka jñāna kṛtam viśvam iti yad ca uṣyate mṛṣā bahu jñāna kṛtam viśvam iti tasya uttaram bhavet  parasya satyatām jānan  api yaḥ sva ātma taskaraḥ paraḥ  na asti iti vadati kim iti unmattavat  vadet  parābhāve hi vāc  vyarthā yadi na eva ucyate tadā kaśā vetra ādikam tasya taskarasya uttaram vadet  prapañcaḥ  yadi vidyeta nivarteta na saṃśayaḥ māyā mātram idam dvaitam advaitam paramārthataḥ vikalpaḥ  vinivarteta kalpitaḥ  yadi kenacid  upadeśa ādayam vādaḥ  ajñāte dvaitam na vidyate iti atra yadi śabdau ca nivarteta iti ca dvayam viśvasya satya tām āhuḥ vidyeta utpattim eva ca vidā utpattau  iti hi asmāt  dhātoḥ utpattiḥ eva hi nivṛtti vyāpti yuj  prāyas  prapañcaḥ  bheda pañcakaḥ jīveśvara bhidā ca eva jaḍa īśvara bhidā tathā jīva bhedaḥ  mithas ca eva jaḍa jīva bhidā tathā mithas ca jaḍa bhedaḥ  yaḥ prapañcaḥ  bheda pañcakaḥ saḥ  ayam satyaḥ  hi anādiḥ ca sādiḥ ced nāśam āpnuyāt dvaitam na vidyata iti tasmāt ajñāninām matam iti śruteḥ mitam trātam māyā ākhya hari vidyayā uttamaḥ  arthaḥ  hariḥ tu ekaḥ tad anyat madhyama adhyamam vācā ārabdham tu sa aṅketyam nāma syāt  vikṛtam bahu nityam tu nāmadheyam yad mṛttikā ityādi vaidikam prādhānyāt  tad parijñānāt  prākṛta ājñaḥ  api pūruṣaḥ vidvān iti ucyate sadbhiḥ evam nitya para ātma vid  sadātanam satyam iti nityam eva ucyate budhaiḥ prayogaḥ ca uttaratra asti jarā yadi enam āpnuyāt  dehaḥ pradhvaṃsate vāyam kim tatas  asya atiśiṣyate hanyate na vadhena ayam jarayā ca na jīryati etad  satyam brahma puram iti nityatva eva hi vācā ārambhaṇam iti ukte mithyā iti aśruta kalpanam punaruktiḥ nāmadheyam iti iti asya nirarthatā ekaḥ piṇḍaḥ  maṇiḥ ca iti pada vaiyathyarmā iva ca vikāratva vivakṣāyām naca eka nakha kṛntanam sarva kārṣṇāyasam ca syāt atas  sādṛśya eva ca vivakṣā atra tu nitya tve prādhānye ca ukta vartmanā prādhānya pratipatti artham sṛṣṭayā ādeḥ ca eva vistaraḥ tasmāt  kena api mārgeṇa na vivartamatam bhavet  tad asaṅkhayāta doṣetam heyam eva śubha arthibhiḥ asaṅkhayatvena doṣāṇām grantha ādhikya bhayāt api uparamyate tatas  viṣṇuḥ icchā pūrva kam aśramaḥ karoti pitṛvat  viśvam pūrṇa śeṣa guṇa ātmakaḥ uktaḥ samanvayaḥ sākṣāt avirodhaḥ  atra sādhyate caturvidhasya tasya ādau yauktaḥ tatra api ca smṛteḥ tasyāḥ catur svarūpa tvāt pratyekam catur ātmakāḥ pādāḥ sarve tad aṃśāḥ ca mūrtīnām varṇam āagamāt  āpta tā samatā dṛṣṭi śruti sāmya balāt bhavāḥ sarva anusāraḥ  laghu tā viśeṣa adarśana aphale iṣṭa siddhiḥ ca niyamaḥ pūrva pakṣeṣu yuktayaḥ etā eva tu atibalā siddhāntasya niyāmakāḥ āptaiḥ pratyakṣataḥ dṛṣṭvā proktam artham katham śratiḥ pipīlikā lipi nibhā vārayeta sarvagā hi te iti ced  yadi aśeṣa jñā rudra ādyā hari pūrvakāḥ kim na aśeṣa vidaḥ  mānam hi  ubhayatra samam bhavet  na ca āpti niścayaḥ tatra śakyate vyabhicārataḥ naca asyā vyabhicāre api hīyate mānatā kvacid  veda uktasya adhikārasya durnirūpa tvatas  sadā niyamaḥ  vyabhicāraḥ  vā na eva jñātum hi śakyate adhikāraḥ  hi sulabhaḥ kathitaḥ  anya āgameṣu alam veda uktaḥ  hi  adhikāraḥ tu durlabhaḥ sarva mānuṣaiḥ anya āgameṣu vipra tvam api caṇḍāla janmanām maṇḍala antar praveśena kramaśas  pratipādyate adhikāram durāpādya m ukta vāti sulabham punar  aśakyam sādhanam ca uktavā suśakam tad phala āptaye ucyate atas tad uktam hi vyabhicāri phale api tu katham pramāṇa tām gacchet nitya tvāt puruṣa udbhavaiḥ ujkhitam sarva doṣaiḥ ca katham naḥ mānatām vrajet  virūpa nityayā vācā nityayā anityayā sadā iti ādi śrutibhiḥ vedaḥ  nitya iti avagamyate pipīlikā lipiḥ ca api pramāṇam avirodhataḥ yathā drauṇeḥ ulūkena kṛtam api āsa bodhakam aviruddham viruddham tu virodhāt eva bādhitam virodha adarśanāt  tasmāt  veda prāmāṇyam iṣyate tad mūla tvāt smṛtīnām ca virodhaḥ  yatra na kvacid  virodhaḥ  api sa eva uktaḥ pratyakṣeṇa āgamena vā āgamena āgamasya eva virodhe yuktiḥ iṣyate upajīvya virodhe tu vedasya anya artha kalpanā pratyakṣam upajīvyam syāt  prāyaḥ yuktiḥ api kvacid  āgama eka pramāṇeṣu tasya eva hi upajīvyatā yuktaḥ  ayuktaḥ ca yadi artha āgamasya pratīyate syāt  tatra yukta eva arthaḥ  yuktiḥ ca trividhā matā vyāptiḥ pratyakṣatā yasyāḥ  yukti gā agama gā tathā pratyakṣa āgama mūlā tu yuktiḥ tatra balīyasī yāthārthyam eva māna tvam tad mukhyam jñāna śabdayoḥ arthatva marya tā eva syāt na kriyā artheṣu sā matā jñāna arthe jñeya tā mukhyā śabda arthe tad anantaram yathā artha jñāna janakā yathārthā yuktayaḥ smṛtāḥ anupramāṇam etāni hi akṣa yukti vacāṃsi atas  prāmāṇyam na anuvādasya smṛteḥ api vihīyate yāthārthyam eva prāmāṇya śabda arthaḥ  yad  vivakṣitaḥ aṅgīkṛtam ced  prāmāṇyam smṛti ādeḥ kā virodhatā nacā phala tvam vaktavyam sarva smṛti anuvādayoḥ phalavat tvam naca asmābhiḥ prāmāṇyam hi vivakṣitam tṛṇa ādi darśane kim ca phalavat tvam nigadyate sukha duḥkha ādikam kiñcid  smṛtau  api hi dṛśyate na pariccheda kāri eva pramāṇam iti ca pramā nirdoṣa akṣa udbhavam hi atra pratyakṣam iti gīyate prākṛtam śuddha caitanyam akṣam tu dvividham matam śuddham īśaramāmukteṣu anyatra prākṛtaiḥ yutam nirdoṣam eva caitanyam anyatra ubhayam iṣyate sukha duḥkha ādi viṣayam śuddham saṃsāra geṣu api nirdoṣatva ati niyamāt  tad  baliṣṭhatamam matam pañca indriya manaḥ bhedāt  prākṛtam ṣaḍvidham smṛtam anumā yuktiḥ eva uktā vyāptiḥ eva tu sā smṛtā pratijñāta artha siddhayartham vyāptiḥ eva yadā uditā avaśiṣṭam kim atra asti liṅgam tatra vijānataḥ yadi liṅgam asiddham syāt  kuta eva asya mānatā yadi smāraka mātram syāt  smartuḥ na atra prayojanam na pañca avayā uktau ca vivādau  asitiḥ bhavet  dṛṣṭānta ādiṣu ca evam syāt  sādhanam punar eva hi liṅga uktau  api ca evam syāt anumāva sitiḥ dhruvā virodhaḥ  asaṅgatiḥ ca eva sākṣāt  yukteḥ tu dūṣaṇam pratijñāyāmasambandhaḥ yukteḥ uktā hi asaṅgatiḥ virodhaḥ  api tridhā eva syāt  pratijñā artha viruddha tā liṅga rāhityam avyāptiḥ nyūna ādhikye tu vācike sādhya vyāpaka vailomyam avyāptiḥ sādhanasya ca durbalena virodhe api na pramāṇam asādhakam sva vākyena virodhe api na eva sādhaka tām vrajet  saṃvāda anukti saṃyuktā eta eva ca nigrahāḥ vādaḥ  jalpaḥ  vitaṇḍa iti kathāḥ tisraḥ  vijānatām sva artham para artham api vā tattva nirṇaya sādhanī kevalam tu kathā vādaḥ  jalpaḥ  artha ādi vyapekṣayā satām eva kathā jñeyā vitaṇḍā tu asatām satām aprakāśya sva siddhāntam asatām pakṣa dūṣaṇam ukte taiḥ prathamam māne vaktavyam tasya dūṣaṇam vidyā parīkṣā pūrvā eva vitaṇḍā jalpa eva ca ucca nīcatva nirṇītiḥ yatas  jaya parājayau vinā eva tattva nirṇītim na hi jalpa ādinā kvacid  ucca nīcatva vijñānam iti vidyā parīkṣaṇam vādena ca ucca nīcatva vijñānam bhavati sphuṭam iti vādasya pūrva tvam tad siddhau vyarthatā anyayoḥ bahu vidyatva siddhau tu na eva vādaḥ  api kāraṇam sa bhāsa bhāpa prāśnīka pūrvaḥ tu spardhinām api vāda eva ubhaya arthaḥ syāt nirṇīti jaya kārakaḥ tattva aprakāśa eva ekaḥ  vitaṇḍā jalpayoḥ phalam vinā vādena vidyāyā yadi śakyam parīkṣaṇam syāt jalpa ādiḥ api kvāpi vāda eva anyathā bhavet  jalpa iti api nāma syāt  vādasya etādṛśasya tu pratijñā mātra sādhya tvam api syāt  yājñavalkyavat  sabhā sabhā patiḥ ca eva prāśnikāḥ ca eva vaiṣṇavāḥ rāga dveṣa vihīnāḥ ca syuḥ sabhyāḥ sarva vedinaḥ prāśnikāḥ ca etad ajñāne sabhyāḥ ca eṣām ca dūra gāḥ pramāṇam nirṇayāya syuḥ pakṣapāta vivarjitāḥ ubhābhyām sādhanam ca eva dūṣaṇam vāda jalpayoḥ sadbhiḥ āgama eva ekaḥ prayojyaḥ  abhīṣya sādhakaḥ sva siddhānta anusāreṇa hi asadbhiḥ anumā ucyate pratyakṣa āgama vairūpyam āśritya anyārtha tā eva tu āgame daśarnīyātra doṣaḥ  liṅga viloma tā liṅga ānukūlyam sva arthasya śruti ādīnām anugrahaḥ tri pañca avayavām eva yugma avayavinīm api niyamāt  yaḥ  anumām brūyāt  tam brūyāt  yadi tādṛśī na anumā iti tadā kena sādhya avayava kalpanā niyata avayava asiddhau vyāpti mātreṇa sādhanam kartavyam eva tena syāt  tasmāt  sā eva anumā matā anubhūtiḥ pramāṇam ced  kena smṛtiḥ apa udyate pūrva anubhūte kim mānam iti ukte syāt  kim uttaram mānasam tad hi vijñānam tad ca sākṣi pramāṇakam atīta anāgatam yadvat  yogibhiḥ dṛśyate añjasā evam pūrva anubhūtam ca manasā eva avagamyate vijñātam manasā pūrvam mayā etad  kṛtam iti api sākṣāt anubhavāt  siddham katham eva hi apodyate evam lakṣaṇake māna traye brahma ādi vastuṣu pramāṇam veda eva ekas tad prāmāṇyam ca sādhitam tathā api mṛd jala ādīnām buddhi vāc ādi vācakaḥ dṛṣṭa vyāpti viruddha tvāt  tatra mānam katham bhavet  tatas tad nāmakaḥ kaścid  pumān anyaḥ bhavet iti yuktayā āgama avirodhena prāptam atra abhidhīyate bāla rūḍhim vinā eva api vidvat rūḍhi samāśrayāt tad tad nāmāna eva ete tad tad vastu abhimāninaḥ santi teṣām viśeṣeṇa śaktiḥ anyebhyaḥ  ucyate vyāptiḥ ca ukta anusāreṇa dṛśyante ca ādhikāribhiḥ śāstra ukta vastunaḥ ca eva vyutpattiḥ śāstra liṅgataḥ vyutpattiḥ sā balavatī mūrkha vyutpatti tā hi yad  dṛḍha yukti virodhe tu sarvatra nyāya īdṛśaḥ alpa vākya yutā yuktiḥ bahulā eva virodhinī yatra tatra katham vastu nirṇayaḥ sya ādi ti īrite virodhi yukti bāhulyāt iti nyāyaḥ  viniścitaḥ yukteḥ tu yukti bāhulyam āgamāt āgamasya ca katham na nirṇayam kuryāt iti asat kāraṇam na hi śruti arthaḥ  bhavati kvāpi śruti prāya upapattibhiḥ avirodhaḥ caturthe tu pāte samyak  samarthyate asat  kāryam yathā dṛṣṭam vastu tvāt  kāraṇam tathā iti ced na niṣedha eka svarūpasya na kartṛ tā buddhi pūrva pravṛttiḥ hi kartṛ tvam iha niścitam pratiṣedha ātmaka tvam tu bhāvasya abhāva dharmataḥ dharma dharma aikyataḥ ca eva na tu tanmātra tā bhavet  abhāvasya ca bhāvaḥ api dharmaḥ  atha api hi dharmiṇaḥ tādṛktavam mātratā iha uktā buddhiḥ āhityam eva tad  viśeṣyatā eva dharmi tvam prathama pratipattiṣu niṣedha vidhi rūpa tvam bhāva abhāva tvam atra hi sarva nāśeṣu api sadā śiṣṭa tvāt  yasya kasya nuḥ na āśaḥ ayam vimataḥ  api syāt nāśa tvāt kartṛ śeṣavān naca aśeṣa nṛnāśaḥ tu dṛṣṭaḥ  dṛśyaḥ  asti vā kvacid  dharma adharma āśraya tvena svīkāryaḥ  api naraḥ  laye anādi tvam vinā dṛṣṭam katham syāt  kāraṇam kvacid  pūrva adṛṣṭāt  parādṛṣṭam yadi na eva uttaram kutas  adṛṣṭam kāraṇam naḥ cellaye mānam ca kim bhavet  utpatti nāśa kārī hi buddhimān dṛśyate kvacid  tad dṛṣṭāntena sarvatra kartā kim na anumīyate āgama anugṛhītā tu mānam eṣān umāpitu āgama anugraha abhāve na tarkaḥ syāt  pratiṣṭhitaḥ akṣaja āgama mūlasya syāt eva asya pratiṣṭhitiḥ anyathā asya apratiṣṭhā ca sva vācā vyāhata eva hi na ca śiṣyā gṛhīta tvam nirīśāt īśa vādinaḥ atas  avaśiṣṭa jīva ādi kartṛ tā atra niṣiddhayate tad manaḥ  akuruta iti ādeḥ asataḥ  manasaḥ  janiḥ nivāritā tu pūrvatra hi akasmāt iti tad vinā asataḥ  viśva jananam āśaṅkayātra niṣiddhayate prāpakam vākya mātram tu parihāraḥ  viśeṣitaḥ kvacid jīva akṛtam dṛṣṭvā cetanāt eva ca akṛtam tadvat eva anumāni atra vastu tvāt  kriyate śruteḥ na anyat anya tvam āpannam kvacid  dṛṣṭam kathañcana atas  jīvasya na brahma bhāvaḥ syāt hi kadācana kvacid  bhinna tayā dṛṣṭam tad abhinnatayā katham dṛśyet na u dṛṣṭa pūrvam hi tādṛśam na ca dṛśyate bhoktṛ tvā āpattita iti yad matam tad  kutaḥ hariḥ bhoktrāpatteḥ iti prāha katham ca tad ananyatā jagataḥ tu avikāratva ukta nyāyena sādhite svatantra kāraṇa anya tvam tena hi atra niṣiddhayate dravyam karma ca kālaḥ ca svabhāvaḥ cetanā dhṛtiḥ yad prasādāt ime santi na santi yad upekṣayā iti śruteḥ tad vaśasya bhāvaḥ na para iti atas  śaktaḥ  api hi anyathākartum sva icchā niyamataḥ  hariḥ kāraṇaiḥ niyataiḥ eva karoti idam jagat  sadā nitya bhedaḥ  nimittena hi upādānena tu dvayam asad yad  kārya rūpeṇa kāraṇa ātmatayā asti hi anavasthā anyathā hi syāt  sarvatra utpatti nāśayoḥ śaktaḥ  api bhagavān viṣṇuḥ akartum kartum anyathā sva bhinnam kāraṇa abhinna bhinnam viśvam karoti ajaḥ iti śruteḥ avasita ukta arthaḥ  ayam aśeṣatas  anaṃśasya api jīvasya kiñcid  sāmarthya yojanām kāryeṣu yaḥ karoti addhā namaḥ tasmai svayambhuve yadi bhāgena kāryeṣu jīva śaktim na yojayet  hariḥ tadā hi sarvatra kṛtsnayatnoṃ aśitā api vā aṃśinaḥ hi paṭa ādyā ye bhinnaiḥ eva parasparam aṃśaiḥ aṃśina ucyante na evam eva hi cetanāḥ atas  anaṃśina iti eva śrutiḥ eteṣu vartate api aneka svarūpeṣu viśeṣāt eva kevalam bahu svarūpa tā ākhyā tu teṣu asti eva hi sa aṃśatā bahu tvena avinābhāvāt  bhinna tā niyamāt  bhavet  yadi na evam niyama kṛt  bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ tasya tu aśeṣa śakti tvāt  yujyate sa varmā iva ca virodhaḥ sarva vaiśiṣṭaye yaḥ  dvitīye nirasyate nārāyaṇasya tu adhyāye tad anye tatra tatra gāḥ sṛṣṭi saṃhāra vākyānām jīva rūpa abhidhāyinām api anyonya avirodhaḥ tu dvitīya adhyāya gocaraḥ māna meya viśeṣeṇa punaruktiḥ na jāyate sadā pravṛttiḥ īśasya svabhāvāt eva kevalam aṅga ceṣyā yathā puṃsaḥ kāścid uddeśa varjitāḥ devasya eṣa svabhāvaḥ  ayam iti āha śrutiḥ añjasā krīḍām prayojanam kṛtvā sṛṣṭiḥ śruti virodhinī iti kevala līlā eva nirṇītā prabhuṇā svayam ātma prayojana arthāya spṛhām śrutiḥ avārayat  na prayojanavat tvena iti ata āha jagadguruḥ icchā mātram prabhoḥ sṛṣṭiḥ iti sṛṣṭau viniścitāḥ iti praśaṃsayā kāmaśrutibhyaḥ ca eva yuktitaḥ mahātātparya yukteḥ ca na icchā mātram niṣiddhayate mokṣa arthāḥ śrutayaḥ yasmāt  sa ca tasya prasādataḥ unninīṣati vākyāt ca loka dṛṣṭa anusārataḥ icchāṃnimitta kaḥ yasmāt  tad abhāve kutas  śrutiḥ mahātātparya rahitā pramāṇa tvam gamiṣyati yāthārthyam eva māna tvam api vākyam prayojakam māna tvam eti tatra api yad  sampūrṇa prayojanam vaiṣamyam ca eva nairghṛṇyam veda aprāmāṇya kāraṇam na aṅgīkāryam atas  anyat tu na vaiṣamya ādi nāmakam yad adhīnā guṇāḥ ca eva doṣā api hi sarvaśas  guṇāḥ tasya katham na syuḥ syuḥ deṣāḥ ca katham punar  sarva dharma āpapatteḥ tad  vākyaiḥ api hi tādṛśaiḥ nirdoṣa aśeṣa guṇa kaḥ  nirṇītaḥ  bhagavān hariḥ smṛti yukti śruti guṇa yuktayaḥ bahu yuktayaḥ evam caturvidhā na eva viruddhayante anvayam prati iti prathama pādena nirṇīte api abhiyogataḥ darśanānām pravṛtta tvāt manda āśaṅkate punar  anādi kālataḥ  vṛttāḥ samayā hi pravāhataḥ naca ucchedaḥ  asti kasya api samayasya iti atas  vibhuḥ bhrānti mūla tvam eteṣām pṛthak  darśayati sphuṭam tarkaiḥ dṛḍhatamaiḥ eva vākyaiḥ ca āgama vādinām daurlabhyāt śuddha buddhīnām bāhulyāt alpa vedinām tāmasa tvāt ca lokasya mithyājñāna prasaktitaḥ vidveṣāt  parame tattve tattva vediṣu ca aniśam anādi vāsanā yogāt asurāṇām bahutvataḥ durāgraha gṛhīta tvāt  vartante samayāḥ sadā tathā api śuddha buddhīnām īśa anugraha yoginām yuyuktayaḥ tamaḥ  hanyuḥ āgamānugatāḥ sadā iti vidyā patiḥ samyak  samayānām nirākṛtim cakāra nija bhaktānām buddhi śāṇatva siddhaye cetana acetanam tattva dvayam eva nirīśvarāḥ āhuḥ tad  pañca pañcatva vibhāga stham acetanam cetanam tad asaṅkha yātam bhinnam anyat  layam bhavet  acetanasya kartṛ tvam svātantryeṇa nigadyate paraspara vibhedaḥ ca kāryāṇām ālayam bhavet  bhoktṛṇām cetanasya āhuḥ kecid  tām api na apare sva rūpa caitanya balāt sva prakāśāt ca bhogitām prakṛteḥ ca svarūpasya viveka agraham eva tu abhoga vādinaḥ  bhogam āhuḥ bheda grahāt tayoḥ bhoginām muktiḥ uddiṣṭā sa eva ābhoga vādinām īśasya asaṅgrahāt eva na yuktau tau  ubhau  api cetana icchā anusāreṇa yadā dṛṣṭaḥ paṭa udbhavaḥ etādṛśa tvam anyasya vastu tvāt  kena vāryate na ca kācid  pramokta arthe śrutiḥ eva pramā hi naḥ āpta tvam ukta mārgeṇa vaktuḥ na eva upapadyate aprāmāṇi asvataḥ tu asya svīkārāt api māyivat  sva ukta akhila niṣedhī syāt na ca kiñcid  prasiddhayati idam na acetana vaśam vastu tvāt  pratipannavat  iti eva pratiṣiddhasya kena mūla anumā bhavet  svatantra vṛttī racanā sā ca eva acetane kutas  acetana tvam svātantryam iti ca ātma pramāhatam sva icchā anusāritām eva svātantryam hi vidaḥ  viduḥ kuta icchā acetanasya seccham ced  kim acetanam icchāmi aham iti hi eva nija anubhava rodhataḥ acetana icśāpa gatā yadi bheda āgrahaḥ atra ca katham na sa ghaṭasya syāt manaḥ  ma iti bhedataḥ manasaḥ  api gṛhīta tvāt ubhaya ātmaka tā yatas  kāmasya tu manaḥ kāmaḥ priya apriya vibhedataḥ dvaividhyam dṛśyate ca asya tasmāt  bheda āgrahaḥ kutas  racanā anupapatteḥ tad na sarvajñānum āgatam acetanam jagatkartṛ payaḥ  ambu ādi ca na upamā etad praśāsti vacanāt cetanā acetanasya ca dvaividhye api tu kāma ādeḥ kutas  svāmi tvam ātmanaḥ sākṣāt anubhava ārūḍham śakyate apoditum kvacid  icchā svāmi tvam eva uktam icchāvat tvam naca aparam kiñcid  tad vaśa ga tve api svāmi tvam lokavat  bhavet  sarva ātma tantra kāma ādeḥ kim uta eva pareśituḥ na ca anubhava gam kāma svāmi tvam veda vāc api śakta apavaditum tasmāt  sā tad anya abhidhāyinī mokṣa kāmaḥ  bhavet anyaḥ  yadi muktāt  bhaviṣyataḥ mokṣa kāmasya kim tena sva nāśa artham ca kaḥ  yatet  kartṛ tvam yasya tasya eva bhoktṛ tvam upalabhyate vibhāge ca tayoḥ mānam na eva kiñcid  kvacid  bhavet  sarva māna virodha eka durdīkṣā dīkṣitaḥ tu ayam māyā vādi upamām yāyāt  tad caśabdāt nirākṛtaḥ sāṅkhayaḥ tu sa īśvaraḥ  brūte kṣetra anugraha śaktimān asti īśvaraḥ svayambhātaḥ kleśa karma ādi varjitaḥ kṣetra śaktimatī sā eva prakṛtiḥ bīja śaktimān jīvaḥ parjanyavat  daiva śaktimān īśvaraḥ smṛtaḥ pṛthivīvat  pradhānam tad jīvaḥ sannidhi mātrataḥ bīja avapana kartā iva iti atra prāha prabhuḥ svayam anyatra kā api śaktiḥ na svātantryeṇa īśa eva hi śaktīḥ tāḥ prerayati añjaḥ tad adhīnāḥ ca sarvadā sattā pradhāna puruṣa śaktīnām ca pratītayaḥ pravṛttayaḥ ca tāḥ sarvā nityam nitya ātmanā yatas  yathā nitya tayā nityam nitya śaktayā svayā īśvaraḥ niyāmayati nityam ca na ṛte tvad iti śruteḥ svabhāva jīva karmāṇi dravyam kālaḥ śrutiḥ kriyāḥ yad prasādāt ime santi na santi yad upekṣayā iti śruteḥ na sattā ādyā api nārāyaṇam vinā tad patañjali vindhya ādi matam na puruṣa artha dam cārvākaiḥ ucyate mānam akṣa jam na aparam kvacid  deha ātmā pum arthaḥ ca kāma arthābhyām vinā na hi yad evam darśanena asya kaḥ  arthaḥ pratyakṣa gocaraḥ labdhaḥ tena eva hi naraiḥ śāstrāt  kim mohanam vinā sva para artha vihīna tvāt  sva matena eva niṣphalam kim iti unmattavat śāstram vṛthā pralapati svayam dehāt anyaḥ  anubhavata ātmā bhāti śarīriṇām mama deha iti vyaktam mama artha itivat  sadā pratyakṣasya eva māna tvam iti kena avasīyate yadi tad sādhakam veda prāmāṇye na katham bhavet  na ca anyāmāna tā kvāpi pramāṇena avasīyate sva matena artha rahita upekṣyaḥ pakṣa īdṛśaḥ sannidhānāt cetanasya vartate yadi acetanam tathā api abuddhi pūrva tvāt ukta doṣaḥ samaḥ  bhavet  aṅgi tvam puruṣasya eva sarvaiḥ api anubhūyate tad aṅgatva uktitaḥ ca eva syāt  sarvasya apalāpakaḥ kim u sarva īśvarasya asya hi apalāṣāt  yatas  akhilam aṅgi tvam yadi tasya eva svātantryam ced na ca akhilam tad preraṇe api aśakta tvāt  svatantraḥ  anyaḥ  hi apekṣitaḥ na ca svātantryam asya eva pratyakṣa ādi virodhataḥ hita ākṛtya ādi doṣāt ca bhadram nānīśvaram matam saṃsāriṇaḥ  anyam sarva īśam sarva śaktim anaupamam cetana acetanasya asya sattva ādeḥ tad adhīna tām na aṅgīkurvanti ye teṣām sarveṣām ca samā ime tasmāt śruti pramāṇena yuktibhiḥ ca paraḥ  hariḥ aṅgī kāyartamaḥ  nityaḥ sarvaiḥ api su niścitam nitya jñāna prayatna iccham saṅkhayadyaiḥ api pañcabhiḥ yuktam īśam vadanti anye tad icchā dṛṣṭa coditāḥ paramāṇavaḥ caturvargāḥ saṃyujyante dviśaḥ akhilāḥ paramāṇu dvayena eva dvayaṇukam nāma jāyate dvayaṇukatrayeṇa tṛyaṇukam taiḥ caturbhiḥ tad ātmakam tatas tu aniyamena eva khaṇḍa avayavinām bhavaḥ tatas ca aniyamena eva sarva avayavi sambhavaḥ kāraṇam samavāyi ākhyam paramāṇu ādi tatra hi īśa icchā dṛṣṭa kālāḥ tu nimittam kāraṇam matam sāmānya antya viśeṣau ca samavāyaḥ ca tad trayam nityam kriyā anityāḥ tu guṇa dravye dvi rūpake kārye guṇa kriyāṇām tu samavāyi anya kāraṇam kāraṇa sthā guṇa ādyāḥ tu saṃyogaḥ  dravya kāraṇam evam sthite api siddhānte viśeṣaḥ tatra kalpitaḥ dvayaṇuke paramāṇau ca hrasva tvam parimaṇḍalam na kāraṇam kārya guṇe vairūpyam tatra kāraṇam iti āhuḥ tān athā uvāca vidyā adhīśaḥ svayam prabhuḥ mahat tvam ca eva dīrgha tvam tṛyaṇuka ādyeṣu kalpitam tasmāt ca sadṛśam kāryam tad kāryeṣu upajāyate yathā tathā eva hrasva tvāt  pārimāṇḍalyataḥ  api hi jāyeta sadṛśam kārye parimāṇam samatvataḥ na ced mahat tvataḥ ca eva dīghaṛtvāt api naḥ bhavet  sadṛśasya hi kāryasya na eva yogaḥ kathañcana apratyakṣa tvam evam syāt  yatas  kāryeṣu aṇutvataḥ iti ced na mahat tvam ca paramāṇauvaṇau  api katham tṛyaṇuka pūrveṣu na aṇu tvam api kathyate pratyakṣatva tad anya tve puruṣa apekṣayā akhile aṇu tvam ca mahat tvam ca yatas  vastu vyapekṣayā tāratamya sthitā yasmāt  padārthāḥ sarva eva ca yathā mahattva viśrāntiḥ tathā aṇu tvasya ca iṣyate parimāṇa tvataḥ ced na mahat tvasya api viśramaḥ dṛśyate ananta iti eva tathā ānanti amaṇau  api na mahat tatva guṇata etāvān iti hi īśvaraḥ paricchinnaḥ tathā aṇoḥ ca na etāvat bhāga tā kvacid  viśrāntaḥ  yadi ananta aṃśaḥ kaścid asti iti gamyate na avasāyayitum śakyaḥ  virodhāt eva kevalam kevalam sākṣi mānena kālaḥ  deśaḥ  api na antavān aparyavasitiḥ ca aṇoḥ dṛśyate sakṣiṇā dvayoḥ yadi naḥ sa akṣi gamyam tad mahat tvam kena gamyate viśrāntiḥ tāratamyena dṛśyate hi anumānataḥ yadi āgamāt anantam tad mahat tvam avagamyate anantam eva ca aṇu tvam kutaḥ na eva avasīyate mahattva aṇu tvayoḥ na eva viśrāntiḥ upalabhyate anyat eva hi ananta tvam mahattva aṇu tvayoḥ samam bahutva alpa tvayoḥ yadvat  sāṅkhayāyām upalabhyate ānantyam eka bhāgānām tāvat tvam hi eva gaṇyate aṇīyān  ca mahīyān  ca bhagavān āgama uditaḥ ānantya vācakaḥ śabdaḥ  dvidhā ānantye api mānatām yāti na eva guṇa alpa tvam kālāt patvam ca māna gam sarva kāla gatasya alpa kāle api syāt avasthitiḥ mahā guṇasya ca alpaḥ  api guṇaḥ syāt iti ced  bhavet  tāvat tvam eva na eva syāt  deśe api etad na naḥ matam mahataḥ  alpa tvam api hi vyomavat  prāha veda vid  yadi alpa deśa saṃsthānam na sarvatra api naḥ bhavet  sthitasya hi alpa deśeṣu sarvaga tvam bhavet  dhruvam ekatra api anavasthasya kuta eva akhila stha tā śūnya tvam eva tasya syāt  yasya ekatra api na sthitiḥ atas  na aṇutva viśrāntiḥ na mahattvasya ca kvacid  ubhaya ānantya yuj  tasmāt  yadi mukhya mahat  bhavet  tad ca brahma param sākṣāt  sarva ānantya yutam sadā yadi sākṣī svayambhātaḥ  na mānam kena gamyate akṣa ja ādeḥ ca māna tvam anavasthā athavā bhavet  atas  sarva padārthānām bhāgāḥ santi eva sarvadā sarva dikṣu api sambandhāt avibhāgaḥ parāṇu tā tad saṃyogāt aniyatāt padārthānām janiḥ bhavet  dvayoḥ eva tu saṃyoga iti kena avasīyate kāraṇasya guṇāḥ tena bhaveyuḥ kārya gā api tāratamyena sarve api mahāntaḥ ca aṇavaḥ  yatas  na ca tad prokta sṛṣṭau tu mānam kevala kalpanā katham sākṣi mitasya asya śaknuyād vāraṇe kvacid  yadi sākṣi mitam na etad na anumā tatra vartate pakṣīkartum aśakyatvāt  kuta eva anumā bhavet  yatra na asti padanyāsaḥ kaḥ tam viṣayam āpnuyāt  deśa antara ādi śabdaḥ ca śaśaśṛṅga ādi śabdavat sadṛśam ca sajātīyam na asmad pakṣe kim eva hi yena eva ca prakāreṇa atyasiddham anumīyate tena eva śaśṛṅga ādeḥ śakyam astitva kalpanam pratyakṣam āgamaḥ  vā api bhavet  yatra niyāmakaḥ sā eva vyāptiḥ bhavet mānam na anyā sandigdha mūlataḥ saha darśana mātreṇa na vyāptiḥ avasīyate yadā eva avyatirekasya hi akṣa jam vā āgamaḥ  bhavet  tad nirdhārita yuktiḥ vā vyāptiḥ sā eva aparā na hi anyathā saptama rasa bhavaḥ  api anumayā apatet aniṣṭāni ca sarvāṇi hi anumā kāma cāriṇī kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca eva guṇa ādeḥ pañcakasya ca bhinnasya eva tu sambandhaḥ samavāyaḥ  anya īryate bhinnatva sāmyataḥ tasya tābhyām yogaḥ  bhavet  dhruvam sa sva nirvāhakaḥ ced  syāt  dravyam eva tathā na kim viśeṣaḥ tad gatatva ādiḥ yadya bhinne avasīyate guṇa kriyā ādi rūpasya niṣedhaḥ kena hetunā dravyam eva tatas  ananta viśeṣa ātma tayā sadā nānā vyavahṛteḥ hetuḥ ananta tvam viśeṣataḥ viśeṣaḥ ca viśeṣī saḥ svena eva samavāyavat  kalpanā guru tā doṣāt padārtha antara tā na hi kalpayitvā ṣaḍ  padārthān sa abhāvān api kevalam ekasmin sa viśeṣaḥ ced  kim pūrvam tasya vismṛtiḥ yena pratyakṣa siddhena vyavahāraḥ  akhilaḥ  bhavet  bhāva abhāva vibhāgena yam vinā na kathañcana abhedena pratītiḥ ca kārya kāraṇa pūrvake abhāva ante padārthe asmin sa viśeṣa avasīyate sāmānya ādi padārtheṣu tad niṣṭha tvāt ayaḥ  akhilāḥ katham dharmā nivāryante vastu aikye api hi vādibhiḥ kāryasya tad tad niṣṭha tvam guṇa ādeḥ vyāpita ādikaḥ katham viśeṣaḥ  na eva asti sa ca dharmaḥ  aparaḥ  yadi ṣaṣ padārtha atirekaḥ syāt  padārtha aniyame api hi dharmasya dharma santānāt anavasthā karaḥ  bhavet  sāmānyasya api sāmānyam guṇasya api guṇa u hi atas  na aṅgīkṛtaḥ sa ca yadi na anavasthā kvacid  bhavet  asmad pakṣe guṇa ādyāḥ ca tad vantaḥ  hi viśeṣataḥ ananya tvāt na anavasthā bhedaḥ  nāśe bhavet  tathā viśeṣam eva saṃśritya viśeṣaḥ  balavān yatas  dṛṣṭi pramāṇataḥ ca eva virodhaḥ  darśane katham virodhaḥ  hi avirodhaḥ ca yatas  darśanam ānagau tatas  dṛṣṭe virodhaḥ tu sadbhiḥ āpādyate katham abhinnaḥ bhagavān svena tad anyena vibhedavān nityā dharmāḥ tadīyāḥ tu sarve asmān na eva bhedinaḥ sāmastya ucchedinaḥ  anyatra dharmā ubhaya rūpakāḥ bhāve ta eva ca ucchedāt  tad anye ca samastaśas  aṃśāṃśinā uḥ abhedena tu aṃśa saṃyoga eva hi aṃśinaḥ na anavasthātaḥ  yadi api aṃśeṣu aviśramaḥ ekasmin jāta eva anyaḥ saṃyogaḥ  jāyate yadi anavasthā tadā eva syāt  saṃyoga aikye bhavet  kva sā aṃśe saṃyoga dṛṣṭeḥ ca dṛṣṭe kā sa anavasthitiḥ yadi aṃśa gaḥ na saṃyogaḥ kāryeṣu prathimā katham paramāṇoḥ aṇoḥ na asti mahattā iti adbhutam vacaḥ aṇūnām prathimā apekṣām vinā eva tṛyaṇuke api saḥ paramāṇoḥ mahat tvam ca vinā iti etad  vacaḥ katham aṃśinaḥ aṃśaiḥ abhedaḥ  ayam aṃśena tu bhidā abhidā sarva pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ katham eva hi apohyate saṃyogaḥ ca vibhāgaḥ ca bhedaḥ ca eva pṛthak  pṛthak  anyonya pratiyogena hi ubhayoḥ api dṛśyate bhinnā iti tu bhedānām samudāyaḥ  hi dṛśyate yathā eva ca padārthānām anayoḥ bheda iti api itas  amuṣya amutas  api asya bhedaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ  dvi dharmikaḥ tatra eka vacanam yad tad  viprāṇām bhojanam yathā naratva ādikam api evam tad tad dharmatayeyate na sarva dharma ekaḥ  asti samudāyaḥ tu bhinna gaḥ etādṛśam ca sādṛśyam padārtheṣu pṛthak  pṛthak  ekasmin sa vinaṣṭe api yatas  anyatra eva dṛśyate kutaḥ bhasma tvam āptasya nara tvam punar iṣyate ekatve na asti mānam ca śrutiḥ api āha sādaram bhinnāḥ ca bhinna dharmāḥ ca padārthā akhilā api svaiḥ svaiḥ dharmaiḥ abhinnāḥ ca svarūpaiḥ api sarvaśas  anivṛtta vināśāḥ tu dharmā ubhaya rūpakāḥ na kenacid abhinnaḥ atas  bhagavān sva guṇaiḥ vinā iti vyutpattiḥ api hi sādṛśyena eva gamyate sarveṣu yugapad śabdaḥ sadṛśeṣu pravartate tathā api prāptitaḥ tu eka vacanāt ca viśeṣataḥ abhīṣya avagatiḥ ca syāt śaktiḥ sādṛśya gā yatas  tādṛśaḥ  ayam ca tad śabda iti jñāpayati sphuṭam jātitaḥ ced  katham tāsu tatra ced anavasthitiḥ tathā eva vyakti vijñānam vyaktitva abhāva dūṣitam yadi tad ca asti tasya api viśeṣeṣu anavasthitiḥ katham svarūpa tvam api jñāyate anugatam yadi eka vyutpatti paryantam anavasthā ādi dūṣitam kalpanā gauravāt tena yuktā na anuga kalpanā aupādhika viśiṣṭa ādyam api tad vastu kim tatas  anyat  tad eva ced agnimat tvam kim tatra bhaṇyate agni saṃyoga mātram ced  bhavet  tad  siddha sādhanam bhūdharasya agni saṃyogaḥ  yadi ṣaṣṭhayartha eva kaḥ samavāyaḥ  yadi hi  asya ca eka tvāt  siddha sādhanam yadi asya aupādhikaḥ  bhedaḥ kuta eka tvam iṣyate na anirvācyam hi tena iṣyam ata aupādhika anyayoḥ satya tvāt  kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ syāt māyāvādi anyathā bhavet  upādhi janyam tad gamyam iti vaupādhikam bhavet  ubhayatra api anantāḥ syuḥ samavāyā itas tatas  bhinna tvam ca eva teṣu asti kaḥ  viśeṣa upādhi ge avidyamāna eva anyaḥ samavāyaḥ  adhigamyate upādhinā tad gamakam anumānam na mā bhavet  evam eva asataḥ satta samavāyaḥ  janirmatā tatra api hi ukta doṣāṇām na eva kiñcid nivārakam asmad pakṣe viśeṣasya sarvatra aṅgīkṛta tvataḥ na asti doṣaḥ kvacid  bhāvaḥ hi abhāvaḥ ca sa eva hi abhāvasya ca dharmāḥ syuḥ bhāvāḥ teṣām ca te akhilāḥ pratyakṣa mānataḥ sarvam etad naḥ vāraṇa kṣamam sarve bhāvā abhāvāḥ ca padārthāḥ tena sarvadā tathā api prathamam buddheḥ yaḥ  niṣedhasya gocaraḥ saḥ  abhāvaḥ  vidhi buddheḥ tu gocaraḥ prathamam paraḥ tasmāt  pradhvasta bheda ādi sat iti eva avagamyate asti abhāvaḥ  asti ca dhvaṃsaḥ deha abhāvaḥ ca bhasma tā ityādi yujyate sarvam pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇataḥ anyonya abhāva bhedau ca pṛthaktavam ca pṛthak  pṛthak  yad  kalpayanti tad ca eva kalpanā gauravāt  gatam paryāya tvena te śabdā jñāyante sarva eva hi bhedasya tu svarūpa tve ye vadanti ca śūnyatām adbhuta tā āḥ te yatas  anyasya pratiyogi tvam iṣyate pratiyoginaḥ  hi bhedaḥ  ayam na tu svasmāt  kathañcana vibhāgena alpa tā eva syāt  kuta eva ca śūnyatā na śūnyānām hi saṃyogāt  bhāvaḥ vastuna iṣyate vidāraṇa arthaḥ  dhātuḥ ca vibhāga guṇa vācakaḥ avidāraṇe api hi āsyasya bhinnau  oṣṭhau tu tasya ca ata unmatta vākya tvāt māyā vādaḥ  abhyupekṣitaḥ na ca amanda sat ānanda syandī ananta guṇa arṇavaḥ īśvaraḥ  aṣṭaguṇa tvena prameyaḥ  apramita tvataḥ mayi ananta guṇe anante guṇataḥ  ananta vigrahe ananta guṇa māhātmya śakti jñāna mahā arṇavaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ  aśeṣa cetanebhyaḥ param padam ityādi veda tad vākyaiḥ anantaiḥ ca avasīyate ananta guṇa tā viṣṇoḥ katham eva hi apodyate yadi ananta viśeṣāḥ ca tad jñāna ādeḥ nivāritāḥ katham tad tad viṣaya tā sārvajñya artham vidhīyate aupādhika viśeṣaḥ tu pūrvam eva nirākṛtaḥ sva prakāśa tvam api tu yaiḥ jñānasya nivāritam katham sarvajña tā tasya sva jñāna adhigamam vinā jñānam viśva adhigam tu ekam tad jñāna viṣayam param iti jñāna dvayena eva sarva vid  parameśvaraḥ iti ced eṣa eva arthaḥ tad jñāna  asitaḥ  yadi sva prakāśa tvam eva syāt jñānam hi etad  viśeṣaṇam jñāna antareṇa ced atra bhavet eva anavasthitiḥ sva prakāśa tvam etasmāt  durnivāryam samāpatet  sukhavān duḥkhavān  ca syāt iti vyāptiḥ ca naḥ bhavet  nirduḥkha tvam mahānandaḥ śrutyā eva īśasya bhaṇyate yaḥ  aśanāyā pipāse ca śoka ādīn  ca ativartate ānandam brahmaṇaḥ  vidvān vipāpmā iti ādikā ca sā īśvarasya tathā iṣṭa tvam duḥkhitvā upādhiḥ iti api ukte kim uttaram brūyāt śruti anādara tatparaḥ naca ātma duḥkhita icchā syādata etad nivāryate saha darśana mātreṇa śrutī nām apalāpakaḥ yajña ādeḥ  api pāpasya hetu tvam hiṃsayā yuteḥ na anumāti katham tatra yadi upādhiḥ niṣiddha tā aduḥkhi tvena ca anuktiḥ katham na upādhitām vrajet  aduḥkham itarat  sarvam jīvā eva tu duḥkhinaḥ teṣām duḥkha prahāṇāya śrutiḥ eṣā pravartate iti śrutiḥ hi paramā śruti uktiḥ  yadi kāraṇam kim kāryam anumānena gaḷa stana samena hi anumānena yadi arthaḥ śruti dṛṣṭaḥ  vyapodyate pūrva uktena prakāreṇa na īśvaraḥ  dharma eva ca syāt  tad phalam ca tena atra śrutiḥ eva pramā bhavet  īśasya anumayā siddheḥ śrutiḥ dhamiḥ pramā bhavet  tayā sarva guṇaiḥ pūrṇa ukta īśaḥ  yatas tatas  anānanda anumā tasya dharmi grāhi virodhataḥ na pramāṇam bhavet  tasmāt na anumātra upayoginī nitya icchatvāt  pareśasya paramāṇu sadātvataḥ adṛṣṭa kālayoḥ ca eva bhāvāt  kāryam sadā bhavet  na hi kāla vibhedaḥ  asti tad pakṣe asmad mate hareḥ viśeṣa kāla eva etad sṛṣṭayā ādi icchā sadātanā viśeṣāḥ ca eva kālasya hareḥ icchā vaśāḥ sadā sarve nimeṣā iti hi śrutiḥ eva āha sādaram udīrayati kāla ākhya śaktim iti asya vāc api kālasya kāla ga tvena na virodhaḥ  api kaścana asaṅkha yāta viśeṣa tvāt icchāyā api sarvadā īśaḥ  deśaḥ  ca kālaḥ  ca sva gatā eva sarvadā īśa adhīnau ca tau nityam tad ādhārau ca tad gatau iti śrutiḥ api prāha kāle sva uddiṣṭa eva tu tad kāla sṛṣṭim eva atas  vāñchati īśaḥ sadā eva hi syāt  kālaḥ sa tadā eva iti kālasya sva gata tvataḥ svabhāvāt eva hi icśā eṣā devasya eva iti śruteḥ svabhāvaḥ  api pareśa icchā vaśa iti uditaḥ purā nityā anityāḥ ca tatas tad adhīnā iti śrutiḥ rūpa sparśa ādi hetubhyaḥ paramāṇoḥ anitya tā anumeyā śrutīnām ca viruddha tvāt na tad matam upādeyam atas ca ayam aviruddhaḥ samanvayaḥ vaibhāṣikāḥ ca sautra antāḥ svara sakṣaṇikam jagat  aṇūnām samudāyam ca kāla karma nimittatas utpatti kāle yuktānām ātmānam ca kṣaṇa sthitim nityam santānam eteṣām pañca skandha ātmanā sthitam saṃskāra rūpa vijñāna sañjñā duḥkha ātmanā sthitiḥ duḥkha abhāvam sukham ca āhuḥ arūpa jñāna santatim mokṣam sa samudāyaḥ  hi na ekasmāt eva yujyate na ubhayoḥ ca ubhaya tvam yad  samudāya vyapekṣayā atas  anyonya āśraya tvena samudāyaḥ  na yujyate anyonya apekṣayā puṃsaḥ samudāyatva vedanam syāt  tad sadātana tve api tad ca sāmīpya hetukam iti ced  kārya sambhūti mātra vyāpṛti kāraṇam na tu kārya viśeṣeṣu vyāpṛtam kāraṇam bhavet  atas  artha indriya saṃyogi rūpa kāraṇa tā ātmanaḥ saṃyogi rūpa rāhityāt na eva tad jñāna tā api hi viśaṣaṣa kārya janakam yadi kāraṇam iṣyate kutas  samāna rūpa tvam kāryāṇām api sarvaśas  atas  aniyatyā yad kiñcid yasya kasya api kāraṇam adṛṣṭasya api tasya eva viśeṣa āpādakam kutas  yasya kasya api yad kiñcid viśeṣam upapādayet  kāryam ca kāraṇam ca eva yad kiñcid yasya kasyacid  bhavet niyāmaka abhāva ādi damasya eva kāraṇam iti nitya vināśi tve kena mānena gamyate idam na jāyate amuṣma āditi atra api na kāraṇam vināśa utpattayaḥ ca eva na dṛśyante sadātanāḥ dṛśyate pratyabhijñātaḥ sthira tvam sarva vastuṣu phala ādīnām viśeṣeṇa sarvatra api anumīyate sattvena kṣaṇika tvam ced ākāśasya aviśeṣatas  aviśeṣaḥ  akhilasya api sattvāt  kim na anumīyate yadi ākāśasya sattvam na kuta eva nara ādiṣu sa dharmi pratiyogi tvam ākāśasya avagamyate tau vinā na hi  abhāvaḥ  ca kvacid dṛṣṭaḥ kadācana adharmi pratiyogi tvam ākāśasya avagamyate svīkāra tyāgataḥ  adṛṣṭa dṛṣṭayoḥ sarva vastuṣu guṇān unmatta eva asau vidadhāti adhikam punar  uttara utpatti mātreṇa vināśāt  pūvarvastunaḥ na saṃskāra arpaka tvam ca yujyate kasyacid  kvacid  atas  jñātam mayā ityādi na jñeyam anumā kutas  eka tvam anubhūti stham tyaktavā nirmānakā bhidā kuta ātma ādikeṣu syāt  balyā iva anubhavaḥ  yatas  kārya kāraṇayoḥ ca eka kālīna tvam vinā katham pūrva saṃskāra yogī syāt uttaraḥ  niyamena ca sambaddha  eva saṃskāram anyatra ādattate akhilāḥ asambaddhaḥ katham pūrva uttare vāsanākaraḥ eka kāla tayā yogam vinā saṃskārataḥ katham kṣaṇa mātram avasthānam svīkṛtam sarva vastuṣu pūrva madhya apara kalā ra hitaḥ kṣaṇa iṣyate pūrva bhāva bhavam kāryam uta tad nāśa sambhavam yaugapadyam sati bhavet utpādyānām aśeṣatas  vināśe ced na tad kāryam kārya utpattau ca kā pramā abhedena viśeṣeṇa deha dīpa phala ādiṣu viśeṣa darśanam yuktam asmākam anubhūtitaḥ viśeṣa darśanam mānam yadi na sthairya dṛś  kutas  diś sukhe ca kha dṛṣṭānta āt  bhāvau sat ced  kvacid  bhavet  viśvam pratyakṣa gaṃ tyaktavā tayoḥ yaḥ  anumitam vadet  māyāvādivat eva asau  upekṣyaḥ  bhūtim icchatā sarva pramāṇa siddham yad  buddheḥ bhedena sarvadā katham nu tasya buddhi tvam viśvam anyat ca kimpramam sarva lokaḥ  bibheti añjaḥ  yasmāt anubhavāt  sadā tasya apalāpinaḥ kim na niṣpramāṇaka vādinaḥ saḥ  aham tad idam eva aham sukhī sat  gaganam diśaḥ satyā ityādi anubhavāḥ sadā tad pratipakṣa gāḥ atas  nirmānam akhila pramāṇa pratipakṣa gam durmatam kaḥ  nu gṛhṇīyāt  vināsuratatim kvacid  aparaḥ śūnyam akhilam manaḥ vācām agocaram nirviśeṣam svayambhātam nirlepam ajara amaram aśeṣa doṣa rahitam anantam deśa kālataḥ vastutas ca tad asmi iti nitya upāsā para ukṣitam rāga ādi doṣa rahitam tad bhāvam yoginam nayet  tasya eva anādi saṃvṛttyā nānābheda ātmakam jagat  sat ivābhāti satya tvam sāṃvṛtam tasya ca iṣyate pāramārthika sattvam tu śūnyāt anyasya na kvacid  sāṃvṛtena eva satyena vyavahāraḥ  akhilaḥ  bhavet  śūnyāt  saṃvṛti yogena viśvam etad  pravartate sṛṣṭi kāle punar ca ante stimitam śūnyatām vrajet  iti brūte tam uddiśya jagāda jagatām guruḥ na asataḥ  jagataḥ  bhāvaḥ na hi dṛṣṭa asataḥ  janiḥ sataḥ kvacid  pramāṇam ca dṛṣṭiḥ eva akhilāt  varam yadi evam saptama rasān madhurāt iva pīnatā bhavet janasya mārjārṛṅgam goḥ iva ghātakam kārya arthī kāraṇam sat ca na upādadyāt kathañcana na pravarteta ca iṣyāya śūnyādeveṣya sambhavāt  deśa kāla ādi niyamaḥ  niṃha śūnyāt  sataḥ  bhavet  puruṣa icchā anusāreṇa yadi kiñcid  prajāyate kim na anumīyate tadvat  vastu tvāt  puruṣāt  bhavaḥ sarvasya api naca abhāvaḥ  viśvam sat iti gamyate yatas  anubhava rodhe tu vacanam vādinaḥ kutas  svapna bhrāntivat eva idam saṃvṛttyā eva upalabhyate yadi sattvena kiñca atra bhramaḥ  na eva nivartate anādeḥ asya viśvasya nivṛttiḥ yadi ca iṣyate nivṛttiḥ ca nivarteta tasyāḥ  bhrāntitva sambhavāt  dṛṣṭasya bhrānti tā ced  syāt adṛṣṭe na bhramaḥ kutas  gavāma śṛṅgi bhāvena na hi syāt śaśaśṛṅgitā asmākam tu pramāṇena prasādāt īśvarasya ca ukta bhaṅgayā agamānām ca prāmāṇyāt  yujyate akhilam dṛśya tvāt  vimaṃta mithyā svapnavat ced iyam ca mā mithyā ced  sādhya siddhiḥ na vyabhicāraḥ  na ced  bhavet  sādhaka tvam asatyasya sādhyam vipratipattitaḥ tasya ca iti anavasthā syāt  sattvam ca asya anubhūtitaḥ anubhūti virodhena mithyātve mā na kācana atīta anāgatau kālau  api naḥ sākṣi gocarau tad sambandhi tayā sattvam api dṛṣṭasya sākṣi gam dṛḍha dṛṣṭam tu yad  dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭa ābhāsaḥ tatas  aparam bhrānteḥ saṃvṛti satyasya viśeṣaḥ  avyabhicāravān tena api aṅgīkṛtaḥ samyak  sa naḥ satya tvam eva hi vijñānāt  vyabhicāraḥ  asya kadācid  syāt iti pramā na eva dṛṣṭā pramā sā ca na bhavet  sva virodhataḥ bhedaḥ  viśeṣya dharmyādi grahaṇa apekṣayā yadi anyonya āśraya tā hetoḥ durgāhya iti yad na tad  svarūpam vastunaḥ  bhedaḥ  yad na tasya grahe grahaḥ anyathā asya amunā bheda iti vaktum na yujyate agṛhītaḥ  yadā bhedaḥ tadā svasmāt iti grahaḥ syāt  pratīti virodhāt ca na hi kaścid  tathā vadet  dharmitva pratiyogitva tad bhedā yugapad  yadi viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyam ca tad bhāvaḥ ca eva gṛhyate kaḥ  virodhaḥ sva rūpeṇa gṛhītaḥ  bheda eva tu asya amuṣmāt iti punar viśeṣeṇa eva gṛhyate kiñca bhedaḥ katham grāhya iti yaḥ paripṛcchati dharmya ādi bheda grahaṇāt tena uktaḥ  anyonya saṃśrayaḥ anyatva agrahaṇe proktaḥ katham anyonya saṃśrayaḥ anya tvam yadi siddham syāt  katham anyonya saṃśrayaḥ etādṛśasya vaktārau  ubhau jāti uttara ākarau māyī mādhyamikaḥ ca eva tad upekṣyau bubhūṣubhiḥ yad śūnya vādinaḥ śūnyam tad eva brahma māyinaḥ na hi lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ  asti nirviśeṣa tvataḥ tayoḥ anṛta ādi virodhi tvam ubhayoḥ ca sva lakṣaṇam sva vākya abhāva saṃvādāt na kṛtyam prativādinaḥ tad pakṣa iti vaidharmyāt na svapna ādi vadityajaḥ aprayatnāt nirācakre ca iti dṛṣṭi viruddha tām niṣpramāṇa tvam api asya sūcayāmāsa viśvakṛt  jñānam eva ekam akhila jñeya ākāram prabhāsate tatra santati bhedaḥ ca sva bhedaḥ  bheda eva ca kalpitāḥ pratibhāsante nānā saṃvṛti bhūmiṣu iti etad api naḥ yuktam na hi jñāna tayā jagat  bhāsate anubhavasya eva viruddha tvāt apeśalam tad matam kṣaṇika tvāt ca jñānasya sthira rūpataḥ jñeyasya ukta prakāreṇa sarva śruti virodhataḥ anubhūti viruddha tvāt api pakṣā ime aśivāḥ āha kṣapaṇakaḥ  viśvam sat asat  dvayam advayam dvayāt vayam atat sarvam sapta bhaṅgi sadātanam na etad  padārtha ekasmin yuktam dṛṣṭi virodhataḥ bhāva abhāva tayā viśvam yena rūpeṇa mīyate tad rūpam eva tad iti niyamaḥ kena vāryate tad tad doṣa nivṛtti artham svīkṛtā tad tad ātmanā yadi taiḥ akhilaiḥ deṣaiḥ lipyate cala darśanaḥ atihāya pramāṇa āptam niyamam sat asat tayā aśeṣam āviruddham ca nirmānam vyāhatam sadā sarva prakāram vadataḥ  dṛṣṭa hāniḥ ama grahaḥ sva vyāhata tvam iti ādyā doṣāḥ sarve bhavanti hi vakti sva prabham ātmānam deha mānam tad api alam duṣyam nānā śarīreṣu praveśāt anyathā abhavāt  anyathā bhāvi yad  vastu tad anityam iti sthitiḥ tad mate tad anitya tvam pudgalasya anivāritam na anitya tā asmad pakṣe tu caitanya ādeḥ viśeṣiṇaḥ lakṣaṇasya nivṛttau tu syāt na tad cetane kvacid  ota prota ātmaka tvam tu paṭe dehe aṅga saṃsthitiḥ ityādi lakṣaṇasya eva nivṛttau syāt anitya tā bhautikam tu eva rūpa ādi vyāptam nāśena naḥ mate na evam tasya anyathā bhāva u yasya anitya tvam īritam rūpa ādi yuktasya tathā jagat nāśitva siddhaye vyāptyā tayā anyathā bhāvāt ātmanaḥ  anitya tā bhavet  nitya ūrdhva gatiḥ api eṣā yā muktiḥ iti kathyate aloka ākāśam āptasya katham na vikṛtiḥ ca sā kīdṛśaḥ ca anyathā abhāvaḥ  nāśa hetutayā iṣyate saṃsthāna apagamaḥ ced  sa na hi bhū sāgara ādiṣu yaḥ kaścid anyathā bhāvaḥ  yadi muktiḥ ca tādṛśī deha māne vikāraḥ syāt iti sthāsnūnana ātmanaḥ āha hasti ādi deheṣu hi api syāt anyathā bhāvaḥ aṇu dehasya jīvasya gaja tve vikṛtiḥ hi yā deha vyāptyai viśeṣaḥ kaḥ tasyāḥ sthāsnu tanau ca nuḥ gītāt  puṣpa phala avāptiḥ sparśāt  kārśyam rasāt  sthitiḥ api vṛkṣasya dṛśyanta iti nānā ātma tā bhavet  evañca ātmākārtsnyam iti tatas  eva āha veda vid  sarvajñatva ādikaiḥ sarvaiḥ guṇaiḥ yuktam sadāśivam jagat vicitra racanā kartāram doṣa varjitam āhuḥ pāśupatāḥ tad ca bahu śruti virodhataḥ na upādeyam matam hi asya devasya stuhi garta gam utpipeṣa śiraḥ tasya gṛṇīṣe sat patim padam yad
