viṣṇoḥ upamam hantum rudram ākṛṣṭate mayā dhanuryam kāmaye tam tam ugram mā śiśna devatāḥ ghnan śiśna deva anekaḥ  asau  āsīt nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ tasmāt  rudraḥ samprasādaḥ ca abhūtām vaiṣṇavam makham yajñena yajña maya janta abadhnan puruṣam paśum yaḥ  bhūtānām adhipatī rudraḥ tanti caraḥ  vṛṣā ityādi śruti sāmarthyāt  pāratantryam janiḥ mṛtiḥ para adhīna para prāptiḥ ajña tvam praḷaye abhavaḥ pratīyante sa doṣa tvāt na īśaḥ paśupatiḥ tatas  aśarīra tvataḥ tasya sambandhaḥ  jagatā kvacid  kartṛ tvena na yujyeta dehinaḥ  jñāna dṛṣṭitaḥ na ca deha ādivat  viśvam asya syāt  bhoga sambhavāt  adhiṣṭhāne sthitaḥ kartā kāryam kurvan pratīyate na asya adhiṣṭhāna yogaḥ  asti bhūtānām praḷaye tadā adehaḥ ced asārvajñaḥ śilā kāṣṭha ādivat  sadā dehī ced antavān eva yajñadatta nidarśanāt  naca etad akhilam viṣṇau śruti prāmāṇya gauravāt  manaḥ buddhayaṅgitām viṣṇoḥ lakṣayāmaḥ  ya eva saḥ sa eva dehaḥ  vijñānam aiśvaryam śaktiḥ ūrjitā dehaḥ  viṣṇoḥ na te viṣṇaḥ vāsudevaḥ  agratas  abhavat  ekaḥ  nārāyaṇaḥ tu āsīt na brahmā na ca śaṅkaraḥ ajasya nābhau  adhi ekam arpitam mātrayā paraḥ sat dehaḥ sukha gandhaḥ ca jñāna bhāḥ sat parākramaḥ jñāna jñānaḥ sukha sukhaḥ sa viṣṇuḥ parama akṣaraḥ ānanda eka eva agra āsīt nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ priyam tasya śire moda pramodau ca bhujau hareḥ ānandaḥ  madhyataḥ  brahma puccham na anyat abhūt  kvacid  manasaḥ  asya abhavat  brahmā lalāṭāt api śaṅkaraḥ pakṣayoḥ garuḍaḥ śeṣaḥ  mukha āt āsa sarasvatī sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapād  ityādi śruti sandarbha balāt nitya guṇa ātmanaḥ viṣṇoḥ dehāt jagat  sarvam āvirāsīt itīyate mānavat tvāt  virodhaḥ kaḥ  nāmānam kvacid iṣyate avirodhaḥ  virodhaḥ ca mānena eva hi gamyate ata uktam samastam ca vāsudevasya yujyate śiva ādi nāma yuktāḥ ca śrutayaḥ viṣṇu vācakāḥ nāmāni sarvāṇi ca yam ekaḥ  yaḥ  deva nāmadhāḥ viṣṇu nāmāni na anyasya sarva nāmā hariḥ svayam na nārāyaṇa nāmāni tad anyeṣu apare harau iti ādi śrutayaḥ tatra mānam ca uktaḥ samanvayaḥ purāṇāni purāṇa ādyaiḥ viruddha tvāt na tad  pramā tad viruddheṣu naḥ mānam pūrva apara virodhataḥ sama brāhma virodhāt ca niyamāt  vaiṣṇaveṣu api moha artha m uktitaḥ ca eva viṣṇuḥ ekaḥ  guṇa arṇavaḥ skanda sūrya gaṇa īśa ādi matāni nyāyataḥ  amutas  nirākṛtāni aśeṣeṇa siddhāntasya aviśeṣataḥ nirākṛtau viśeṣasya bhāvāt śakti matam pṛthak  dūṣyate mahatī devī hrīṅkarī sarva kāraṇam tripurābhairavi iti ādi nāmabhiḥ sā abhidhīyate tasyāḥ sadāśiva ādyāḥ ca jāyante deva mānuṣāḥ bhūta bhautikam api etad iti tad na upapadyate dṛṣṭā pumbhyaḥ sadā sṛṣṭiḥ strī pumbhyaḥ  vā viśeṣataḥ kevala abhyaḥ  na hi strībhyaḥ tata utpatti asambhavāt  na arcyam mahā vāma matam vāmaiḥ anyat udīryate śiva upasarjanā śaktiḥ sasarja idam samantatas iti tad ca upapannam na śivasya akaraṇa tvataḥ adeha tvāt api hi anye brūyuḥ sarvajñam īśvaram aṇuvāmā na tad yuktam īśavāda praveśanāt  sārvajñi ādi guṇaiḥ yuktam guru kalpanayā dvayam na yujyate hi atas tu īśa eka eva prayojakaḥ ukta doṣaḥ ca tad pakṣa iti na eva atra dūṣyate śruti smṛti itihāsānām sāmastyena virodhataḥ satām jugupsita tvāt ca na aṅgīkāryam hi tad matam pañca rātra niṣedha artham etāni ācakṣate yadi sūtrāṇi ati viruddham tad  yata āha sa bhārate pañca rātrasya kṛtsnasya vaktā nārāyaṇaḥ svayam jñāneṣu eteṣu rāja indra sarveṣu etad  viśiṣṭate pañca rātra vidaḥ  ye tu yathā krama parā nṛpa ekānta bhāva upagatā vāsudevam viśanti te iti gītā ca tad śāstra saṅkṣepa iti hīritam vedena pañca rātreṇa bhaktayā yajñena ca eva hi dṛśyaḥ  aham na anyathā dṛśyaḥ  varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api iti vārāha vacanam ślokā iti vacaḥ śrutau vedaiḥ ca pañca rātraiḥ ca dhyeyaḥ  nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ pañca rātram ca vedāḥ ca vidyā ekā eva dvidheyate iti ādi veda vacanaiḥ pañca rātram apodyate katham eva atra doṣaḥ ka utpattiḥ jñaḥ  ata iti api iha eva uktā nacābhūta bhāvaḥ tatra api kathyate anādi karmaṇā baddhaḥ  jīvaḥ saṃsāra maṇḍale vāsudeva icchayā nityam bhramati iti hi tad vacaḥ na hi saṃsāra sādi tvam pañca rātra uditam kvacid  jīva abhimāni śeṣasya nāmnā saṅkarṣaṇasya tu vāsudevāt janiḥ proktā pradyumnasya tatas tathā manaḥ  abhimāninaḥ kāmasya evam sākṣāt hareḥ kvacid  saṅkarṣaṇa ādi nām nā eva nitya acintya uru śaktitaḥ vyūha uktaḥ  anyathā anūdya katham duṣṭa tvam ucyate yadi vidyāt catur vedān itivat  veda pūraṇam pañca rātrāt iti kutaḥ dveṣaḥ śāṇḍilya vartane atas  parama śāstrorudveṣāt uditam āsuraiḥ dūṣaṇam pañca rātrasya vīkṣāyām api na kṣamam atas  aśeṣa jagat dhātā nirdoṣa uru guṇa arṇavaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ śruti gaṇa tātparyāt avasīyate andham tamaḥ praviśanti ye tu avidyām upāsate tatas  bhūya iva āpsyanti ye tasyāḥ  na eva nindakāḥ tatas  vidyām avidyām ca yaḥ  jānāti ubhayam saha doṣa jñānāt atītya etān vidyayā amṛtam aśnute atha aśeṣa samāmnāya virodha apākṛtim prabhuḥ kariṣyan  adhidaiva adhibhūta jīva para ātmanām svarūpa nirṇayāya eva vacanānām parasparam pādena anena avirodham darśayati amita dyutiḥ anubhūti yukti bahu vāc vailomyam ca tatas  adhikam etad  sarvam sataḥ sāmyam dvāra vaiyarthyam eva ca dṛṣṭa yuktayanu sāritva muktā anyārtha avirodhataḥ prasiddha nāma svīkāre bahu vākya anuvatiḥ tā loka dṛṣṭa anusāri tvam jīva sāmyam anāditā tatra tatra parijñānam guṇa sāmya śrutī tathā utpattimat tvam sva guṇān anubhūti alpa kalpane nānā śrutiḥ ca vaicitṛyam yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣa gāḥ vyavasthā anupapattiḥ ca svātantryam anusāritā mukhya tā śaktimat tvam ca vairūpyam sarva saṅgrahaḥ gati ādiḥ īśa śaktiḥ ca sarva māna virodhitā abhīṣya asiddhi su vyaktī śāstra siddhi virparyayaḥ viśeṣa kāraṇam ca iti siddhāntasya eva sādhakāḥ prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kālaḥ  devāḥ tad abhimāninaḥ mahat ādyāḥ ca jāyante para adhīna viśeṣitā idam sarvam sasarja iti janimat tvam iha uditam avakāśa mātram ākāśaḥ katham utpadyate anyathā yadi anākāśa tā pūrvam kim mūrta nibiḍam jagat  mūtarsampūrṇa tā ca eva yadi anākāśa tā bhavet  mūrta dravyāṇi ca ākāśe sthitāni eva hi sarvadā ata ākāśa śabda uktaḥ tad devaḥ  atra vināyakaḥ deha utpattyā samutpanna iti śrutyā abhidhīyate bhūtam api asitam divya dṛṣṭi gocaram eva tu utpadyate avyākṛtam hi gaganam sākṣi gocaram pradeśa iti vijñeyam nityam na utpadyate hi tad  tathā api pūrva sambandha paratantra viśeṣa yuj  kham eva utpattimat nāma śruti śabda vivakṣitam prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kāla iti ete ca samastaśas  īśa adhīna viśeṣeṇa janyā iti eva kīrtitāḥ kāla pravāha eva ekaḥ  nityaḥ  na tu viśeṣavān puruṣa avyakta kālānām rama eva eka abhimāninī sisṛkṣutva viśeṣam tad  sākṣāt  bhagavat icchayā prāptā eva sṛṣṭā iti uditā pradhānam vikṛteḥ api pumāṃsaḥ  deha sambandhāt  sṛṣṭimanta iti īritāḥ evam praḷaya kāle api pratibhāta parāvaraḥ mukhyau  āyuḥ nitya samaḥ śarīra utpatti kāraṇāt para adhīna viśeṣeṇa janimān eva śabditaḥ na eva kiñcid  tatas  janma varjitam paramāt ṛte para adhīna viśeṣa tve janmanaḥ sthūla tā bhavaḥ pūrva śabda vilopaḥ ca yadi janma iti kīrtyate ramāyā na eva janma asti caitanyasya api kevalam pradhanasya ca vedasya vedasya api īśvara icchayā vyaktiḥ nāma viśeṣaḥ  asti tasmāt  tad vaśatā eva hi utpattiḥ atra kathitā svatantra tvāt para ātmanaḥ na eva utpattiḥ katham api na svatantram tatas  aparam acchedyasya api jīvasya vibhāgam bahudhā hariḥ kṛtvā bhogān pradāya eva ca aikyam āpādayet  punar  ata īśa vaśam sarvam cetana acetanam jagat  avibhāgam vibhāgāya yadā nayati keśavaḥ kim aśakyam pareśasya tadā iti hi abhidhīyate evam sthite api jīva aikyam kecid āhuḥ para ātmanā tad  yaḥ  aham iti pūrvābhiḥ śrutibhiḥ ca anumābalāt na tad  yuktam yatas  viṣṇuḥ pṛthak eva abhidhīyate prajñā netraḥ aloke  iti muktau bhedaḥ  abhidhīyate etam ānandam iti anyā paramam sāmyam iti api idam jñānam apāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ sarge api na upajāyante praḷaye na vyathanti ca upasampadya tad jyotiḥ sva rūpeṇa abhipadyate tatra paryeti jakṣan  ca krīḍan  api sadā sukhī ācakṣva me mokṣam dhīrā yam pravadanti tam iti akta āha vāgdevī param mokṣam prajāpateḥ śākhām śākhām mahānadyaḥ saṃyānti paritas sravāḥ dhānā pūpā māṃsa kāmāḥ sadā pāyasa kardamāḥ yasmin  agnimukhā devāḥ sa indrāḥ saha marut gaṇāḥ ījire kratubhiḥ śreṣṭhaiḥ tad akṣaram upāsate praviśanti param devam muktāḥ tatra eva bhoginaḥ nirgacchanti yathākāmam pareśena eva coditāḥ bheda dṛṣṭayā abhimānena niḥsaṅgena api kamarṇā kartṛ tvāt sa guṇam brahma puruṣam puruṣa ṛṣabham sa saṅgatya punar  kāle kālena īśvara mūrtitā jāte aguṇa vyatikare yathāpūrvam prajāyate ṛcām tvaḥ poṣam āste ca pareṇa preritāḥ sadā yad kāmaḥ tad  sṛjati addhaiṣā ātmanā tad  sṛjati api saha eva brahmaṇā kāmān bhuṅkate nistīrṇa tad guṇaḥ duḥkha ādīn  ca parityajya jagat vaya āpāra varjitaḥ bhuṅkte bhogān saha eva uccān itya ādi āgama mānataḥ muktasya bheda avagateḥ katham eva hi abhinnatā jīveśayoḥ na anumā ca tad abhedam pramāpayet  mithyā eva bhedaḥ  vimataḥ  bheda tvāt candrabhedavat  iti ced  sādhya dharmaḥ  ayam san  asan vā nava ubhayam yadi san  apa siddhāntaḥ sa eva āsanniti īrite na ubhayam ced na siddham tad iti mānasya dūṣaṇam na ca māna antareṇa etad śakyam sādhayitum kvacid  anumānena ced  sā eva hi anavasthā bhaviṣyati naca āgamaḥ tad arthaḥ  asti na asat āsīt na tad  vadet  pariśeṣāt anirvācyam yadi siddhayet  para ātmanaḥ anirvācya tvam eva syāt  pariśiṣṭaḥ  hi asau tadā naca anya āgamaḥ tatra sat asat pratiyogini na ca pratyakṣa mātrā asti naca artha āpattiḥ iṣyate bādhā yogāt  sata iti bādhā bhāvata eva hi viṣayasya kutaḥ bādhaḥ  vidyamānam hi bādhyate na hi vandhyā sutaḥ  vadhyaḥ  yajñadattaḥ  hi vadhyate bādhā yogaḥ sata iti vyāptiḥ eṣā kva dṛśyate kaḥ ca ayam bādha uddiṣṭaḥ  na hi na āśaḥ asataḥ  bhavet  nivṛttiḥ ca apravṛttasya katham eva upapadyate na āsīt asti bhaviṣyat ca tad iti jñānam eya tā yadi bādhaḥ tadā asattvam tena eva aṅgīkṛtam punar  pratītiḥ na āsata iti vadan  aṅgīkaroti tām niṣedhaḥ  hi apratītasya kathañcid nā upapadyate na ca upamā bhavet atra pratyakṣāt  sattvam eva ca śāstra gamya para īśānāt  bhedaḥ sva ātmana īyate anubhūti virodhena katham ekatvam ucyate kiñcitkartā ca duḥkhī iti sarvaiḥ eva anubhūyate sarvajñaḥ  bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarva śaktiḥ iti śrutaḥ anubhūtāt hi bhedena śrutiḥ eṣā vadati amum upajīvya viruddham tu katham aikyam śrutiḥ vadet  aprāmāṇyam yadā bheda vācakasya bhaviṣyati sa eva dharmiṇaḥ  grāhī tad abhedaḥ katham bhavet  yad  svarūpa grahe mānam tad dharme na katham bhavet  eka vijñāna vijñaptyā dvayam mānam bhaviṣyati na ced ekam amānam tad  dvayam api atra naḥ bhavet  dharmi grāhi virodhaḥ tu tasmāt mānasya dūṣaṇam na upajīvyaḥ hi abhedaḥ  atra kvacid  bheda śruteḥ balāt  na ca māna antara upeyam brahma tad  bhavati kvacid  yena mānena cāpeyam bhedaḥ tena avagamyate sarva jñānamaya eva īśaḥ  yadi upeyaḥ kathañcana sarvajñathva guṇena eva tayā bhedaḥ  avagamyate na duḥkha anubhavaḥ kvāpi mithyā anubhavatām vrajet  na hi bādhaḥ kvacid  dṛṣṭaḥ  duḥkha ādi anubhavasya tu yadi duḥkha anubhūtiḥ ca bhrāntiḥ iti avasīyate aduḥkhita aśrutiḥ kena na bhrāntiḥ iti gamyate śruti svarūpam arthaḥ ca mānena eva avasīyate tad ced mānam gṛhītam te kim duḥkha anubhave bhramaḥ na ca bādha viśeṣaḥ  asti yad abādhitam eva tad  bādhaḥ  yadi anubhūte arthe katham nirṇaya īyate kaḥ  api hi  arthaḥ  na niścetum śakyate bhrama vādinā bhrama tvam abhram atvam ca yadā eva anubhava upagam ekasya bhramatā tatra parasya abhrama tā kutas  bhrama tvam abhram atvam ca sarvam vedyam hi sākṣiṇā sa ced  sākṣī kvacid  duṣyaḥ katham nirṇaya īyate viśeṣā sarva eva ete sākṣi pratyaya gocarāḥ ūrīkṛtya ca tān sarvān vyavahāraḥ pravartate sākṣiṇaḥ  vyavasāyī tu vyavahāraḥ  abhidhīyate tasmāt  sarva prasiddhasya vyavahārasya siddhaye sākṣī nirdoṣa eva ekaḥ sadā aṅgī kārya eva naḥ śuddhaḥ sākṣī yadā siddhaḥ  duḥkhi tvam vāryate katham upajīvya pramāṇam tad  bheda grāhakam eva hi atas  jīveśayoḥ bhedaḥ śruti sāmarthya su sthiraḥ tathā api tu cit ānanda pūrvāḥ tad sadṛśā guṇāḥ sāra sva rūpam asya api muktau  api avaśiṣyate atas  abhedavat eva etāḥ śrutayaḥ pravadanti hi paurāṇāni ca vākyāni sādṛśya abheda saṃśrayāt  sādṛśyāt ca pradhāna tvāt  svātantryāt apicā abhidām āhuḥ īśena jīvasya na svarūpa abhidām kvacid  sthāna aikyam aikamatyam ca muktasya tu viśiṣṭate sādṛśyam ca viśeṣeṇa jaḍānām dvayam eva tu bhavet  sādṛśyam ati alpam tṛtīyam parama ātmanā īśa rūpa kriyāṇām ca guṇānām api sarvaśas  tathā eva avayavānām tad svarūpa aikyam tu mukhyatas  yathā udakam durge vṛṣṭam parvateṣu vidhāvati evam dharmān pṛthak  paśyan  tān eva anuvidhāvati iti śruteḥ na ubhayam ca bheda abheda ākhyam iṣyate ekam eva advitīyam na iha nānā asti kiñcana mṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyum āpnoti ya iha na anā iva paśyati iti śrutau  iva iti asmāt  bheda abheda nirākṛtiḥ iva ubhaye ca sādṛśya iti vāc  śabda nirṇaye bhedasya muktau vacanāt api tad pakṣa nigrahaḥ cetanatva ādi sādṛśyam yadi abheda iti iṣyate aṅgīkṛtam tad asmābhiḥ na svarūpa eka tā kvacid  na kenacid abhedaḥ  asti bheda abhedaḥ  api vā kvacid  samudāya mṛte viṣṇoḥ sva guṇa ādīn vinā api vā iti śruteḥ na tasya asti bheda abhedaḥ  api kenacid  abheda śrutayaḥ ṃśa tvāt  sādṛśyam ca aṃśatā asya tu aṃśaḥ tu dvividhaḥ  jñeyaḥ svarūpa aṃśaḥ  anya eva ca vibhinna aṃśaḥ  alpa śaktiḥ syāt  kiñcid sādṛśya mātra yuj  aṃśinaḥ yad tu sāmarthyam yad  svarūpam yathā sthitiḥ sa eva ced  svarūpa aṃśaḥ prādurbhāvā hareḥ yathā sūrya maṇḍala māni ekaḥ tad prakāśa abhimānavān sūryaḥ  atha saptama abdheḥ ca bāhyodasya ca vāripaḥ kaṭhina tvena meru ādeḥ pṛthivyāḥ  api devatā dharā devī evam eva ekaḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ nānā avatāra rūpeṇa sthitaḥ pūrṇa guṇaḥ sadā viṣ mūtra akṣi ādi māninyaḥ yathā apabhraṣṭa devatāḥ sūrya ādibhyaḥ tathā eva ayam saṃsārī paramāt  pṛthak  deha doṣaiḥ ca duṣṭa tvāt apabhraṣṭa ākhya devatāḥ anyāḥ sūrya ādidevebhyaḥ  hi anugrāhyāḥ ca taiḥ sadā evam eva parād viṣṇoḥ pṛthak  saṃsāriṇaḥ  matāḥ anugrāhyāḥ ca tena eva tad prasādāt ca mokṣiṇaḥ na tu matsya ādi rūpāṇām anugrāhya tvam iṣyate guṇaiḥ aśeṣaiḥ pūrṇa tvāt mukhyā bhedaḥ  aparaiḥ naca aṃśa ābhāsāḥ ca sarve api parasya aṃśā na mukhyatas  yathā eṣā puruṣe cchāyā etasmin  etad ātatam na tu pumpādavat  pādā jīvā ete para ātmanaḥ pūrṇāḥ tasya guṇā eva prādurbhāvatayā sthitāḥ evam jagāda parama śrutiḥ nārāyaṇam param akṣayaḥ  bhagavān viṣṇuḥ lakṣmī āvāsaḥ  laye sthitaḥ muktaiḥ sadā cintyamānaḥ  brahma ādyaiḥ tāratamya gaiḥ prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ kālaḥ  vedāḥ ca iti catuṣyayam nityam svarūpataḥ  viṣṇoḥ viśeṣa avāpti mātrataḥ utpattimāt iti proktam lakṣmīḥ tad abhimāninī tatas  jātaḥ pumān nāma brahma āsyām vāsudevataḥ sūtra ātmā prāṇa nāmā ca devyau prakṛti māninī tatas  rūpam mahān nāma brahmaṇaḥ  ahaṅkṛtiḥ śivaḥ brahmaṇaḥ  buddhi nāmnomā tatas  indraḥ  manaḥ  abhidhaḥ skandaḥ ca tatas  eva anye sarve devāḥ prajajñire tatra pūrvatanaḥ śreyān guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ samastaśas  tebhyaḥ ca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ tad adhīnā ime sadā janma sthiti laya ajñāna niyati jñāna saṃsṛtiḥ mokṣaḥ ca tad adhīna tvam eteṣām na eva hīyate muktau  api sa eva ekaḥ svatantraḥ pūrṇa sat guṇaḥ iti śruti upapattibhyām pāde asmin prabhuṇā uditam śruti arthaḥ śruti yuktibhyām viruddha iva dṛśyate yatra tad nirṇayam devaḥ su viśiṣṭa upapattibhiḥ karoti anena pādena tatra spaṣṭa arthavat śrutiḥ viśeṣa śruti vairūpyam māhātmyam vyakta sat guṇāḥ dṛṣṭa ayuktiḥ samāna tvam kartṛ śaktiḥ vimiśratā yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣeṣu su nirṇīta asatu tādṛśāḥ yuktayaḥ nirṇayasya eva svayam bhagavatā uditāḥ svābhāvikānyathānām sahābhāvāni athoktayaḥ aviśeṣaḥ  viśeṣau ca sahabhāvaḥ  vimiśratā viruddha uktiḥ saha sthānam vaiyarthyam ca anyathāgatiḥ yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣasya guṇa ādhikya arthatobhavau upapattiḥ dvi rūpa tvam ādhikyam anurūpa tā yogya tā prabala tvam ca vibhāgaḥ kāraṇa abhavaḥ kḷptiḥ anyā gatiḥ ca eva siddhāntasya eva sādhakāḥ bījā pūruṣa yonīnām saṅga ati niyama ujkhitim atha śabdena bhagavān āha kāraṇataḥ ca tām paścāt adṛṣṭayavijñāna kāla duḥkha pṛthak bhavāḥ sthāna bhedaḥ  viruddha tvam nyāya sāmyam svatobhavaḥ guṇa sāmyam ayogaḥ ca tarka bādhaḥ viloma tā nānābhāvaḥ pralobhaḥ ca pūrva pakṣa gāḥ aśakya kartṛ tā śaktiḥ svatas  abodhaḥ tad eva ca amāna kḷpti sanmāna vyavasthā ati alpatā bhavāḥ viśeṣa dṛṣṭi vākye ca puṃśaktiḥ su nidarśanam alaukika tvam ādhikyam svātantryam nirṇaya pramāḥ vāsanāḥ sarva vastūnām anādi anubhava āgatāḥ santi eva aśeṣa jīvānām anādi manasi sthitāḥ triguṇa ātmakam manaḥ  asti eva yāvat muktiḥ sadātanam tatra eva aśeṣa saṃskārāḥ sañcīyante sadā eva ca sūkṣma tvena laye sat ca prākṛtaiḥ upacīyate sṛṣṭi kāle yadā tad na kutas  saṃsāra saṃsthitiḥ saṃskāraiḥ bhagavān eva sṛṣṭvā nānāvidham jagat  svapna kāle darśayati bhrāntiḥ jāgrat tvam eva hi adṛṣṭe ca aśrute bhāve na bhāva upajāyate adṛṣṭāt aśrutād bhāvān na bhāva upajāyate iti śruti purāṇa uktiḥ anādi tvāt tu yujyate kadācid  darśana ayogyam yad  tatra api vibhāgataḥ dṛṣṭam samāna adhikaraṇam dṛśyate ca sa ca bhramaḥ vāsanā mātra mūla tvāt jāgradvat spaṣṭa tā na ca bhedaḥ  abhedaḥ  athavā dvandvam iti praśnaḥ  na yujyate draṣṭuḥ svapnasya dṛṣṭa tvāt  bhedasya eva akhilaiḥ janaiḥ praśna doṣā hi catvāraḥ sva vyāhatiḥ asaṅgatiḥ siddhārtha tā ca vaiphalyam na taiḥ syāt  tattva nirṇayaḥ tattva nirṇaya vailomyam syāt  vāde api hi nigrahaḥ udbhāvanīyam eva syāt na kathā avasitiḥ bhavet vijigīṣu kathāyām tu kathā avasiti kāraṇam parihāre api siddha tvam dūṣaṇam prativādinaḥ pratijñāyām tad anyasya siddha tā eva hi sādhakā āśraya vyāśraya asiddhī sādhya siddhiḥ ca dūṣaṇam keṣāñcin na ca te doṣā vyāptau satyām kathañcana doṣaḥ  vyāhatiḥ eva asti nṛśṛṅga astitva sādhane yatra vyāhata tā na asti kaḥ  atisaṅgaḥ  asya sādhane pratyakṣa āgama mūlāḥ tu nyāyāḥ sarve bhavanti hi nyāya ābhāsā amūlāḥ syuḥ nyāyasya anyasya tau punar  adṛṣṭe vyabhicāre tu sādhakam tad iti sphuṭam jñāyate sākṣiṇā eva advā māna bādhe na tad  bhavet  yad  sākṣiṇā eva māna tvam mānānām avasīyate amānasya tu māna tvam mānasa tvāt calam bhavet  utsargataḥ  api yad  prāptam apavāda vivarjitam vyabhicārya pavādena mānam eva bhaviṣyati atas  hi bhojana ādīnām iṣṭa sādhana tā anumā mānam vyavahṛtau nityam vyabhicāraḥ  hi tatra ca vyāpta tve vyāśraya tvam tu katham eva hi dūṣaṇam rohiṇī udaya āsannaḥ kṛttikā abhyuditā yatas  iti ukte sādhanam naḥ kim na hi ājñā eva atra sādhakā anyat  sat asatoḥ viśvam iti ca vyāhateramā asiddha sādhane doṣaḥ kaḥ  vyāptiḥ yadi vidyate vyāptiḥ ca vyatirekeṇa tatra taiḥ ca eva gamyate aprasiddhasya sādhyasya sādhaka tvam yad ā iṣyate liṅgasya uktau viśeṣaḥ  ayam kena mānena gamyate sādhanam paramāṇu ādeḥ yadā siddhasya ca iṣyate yathā anubhavam eva etad na aṅgīkāryam kutas tadā yatra na ati prasaṅgaḥ  asti mānam na ca viparyate kliṣṭa kalpanayā eva atra sādhyam iti ati durvacaḥ pariśeṣaḥ  mithas siddhiḥ cakraka sva āśraya ādayaḥ asiddha sādhaka tvena pañca avayava tām vinā aṅgīkāryāḥ samastaiḥ tad niyamaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ sidda sa adhana tāyām ca na kathā avasitiḥ bhavet vyabhicāraḥ  hetu asiddhiḥ eka pakṣe api dūṣaṇam sādhya sādhana vaikalyam dṛṣṭāntasya viśeṣaṇe vaiyathyarmeka asiddhau ca viśiṣṭa asiddhiḥ eva hi aprayojaka tā tatra prathama praśna dūṣaṇam siddha praśna ādikam yad  tad ādhikya anta gartam bhavet  artha āpatti upama abhāvā anumā antargatāḥ kvacid  pratyakṣa antargataḥ  abhāvaḥ sukha ādeḥ niyamena ca anyatra khaḍiti prāptaḥ prārambha ādyāḥ ca yuktayaḥ āgama artha  asiti arthā niyata vyāptayaḥ akhilāḥ vākyam prakaraṇam sthānam samākhyā ca tathāvidhāḥ kuru pāṇḍavavat  teṣām upapatteḥ pṛthak  vacaḥ sva nyāyaiḥ sādhanam kāryam para nyāyaiḥ tu dūṣaṇam sva nyāyaiḥ dūṣaṇam ca syāt  sādhitaiḥ prativādinaḥ prasaṅga artha tayā proktā na siddhāntasya dūṣakāḥ chalam jātiḥ iti dvedhā vyāhati antaram iṣyate jātiḥ sva vyāhatiḥ jñeyā chalam artha antara uttaram evam saṃśodhita nyāya sat āgama virodhataḥ na anirvācyam iha proktam māyā mātra padena hi vilakṣaṇam sat asatoḥ iti hi vyāhatam svatas  pratiyogi tvam api asya brahmaṇaḥ  aṅgīkṛtam bhavet  mithyā ced  pratiyogi tvam vailakṣaṇyam tatas  na hi avilakṣaṇa tvam satyam syāt mithyātvam brahmaṇaḥ tatas  anirvācyasya sattvam vā yadi dharmā na kecana brahmaṇaḥ  na eva jijñāsyam jijñāsā dharma nirṇayaḥ idam ittham iti jñānam jijñāsāyāḥ prayojanam ittham bhāvaḥ  hi dharmaḥ  asya na ced na pratiyogitā itthambhāva ātmakān dharmān āhuḥ ca śrutayaḥ akhilāḥ adṛśya tvāt ayaḥ  api asya guṇā hi prabhuṇā uditāḥ yadi syuḥ tādṛśā dharmāḥ sarvajña tvāt ayaḥ  na kim anya apekṣā yadi syuṣṭe sattā evam deśa kāla gā deśa kāla anapekṣā hi na sattā kvāpi dṛśyate sarva dharma ujjñitasya asya kim śāstreṇa adhigamyate mithyā dharma vidhātuḥ ca vedasya eva apramāṇa tā aprāptām bhrāntim āpādya kim vedaḥ  mānatām vrajet  na hi vedam vinā brahma vedyam dharmāḥ ca tad gatāḥ veda vedyasya mithyātvam yadi naikyasya tad  katham dharma āropaḥ  api sāmānya dharma ādīnām hi daśarne idantat ādi dharmi tve dharmaḥ  anyaḥ kalpyate atra hi sarva dharma vihīnasya dharma āropaḥ kva dṛśyate tad artham yadi dharmāṇām āropaḥ sa anavasthitiḥ īśa tad jñāna veda akṣa ja anumā mātṛ pūrviṇaḥ bhrāntiḥ viśvasya yena eva māna ābhāsena kalpyate atra hi tanmātrasya anyathā bhāvāt  kim na syāt  viśva satyatā yena idam kalpyate bhrāntam bhrāntiḥ tasya eva kim na sā bhrānta tve tasya viśva ādeḥ īśādya bhrāntam eva hi bhaveyuḥ bhrāntayaḥ nṛṇām na eva īśa ādeḥ kathañcana satya tvam akṣaja prāptam yadi bhrāntam iti iṣyate prāmāṇyam āgamasya api pratyakṣāt anyatas  kutas  sākṣi pratyakṣataḥ hi eva mānānām mānateyate sākṣiṇaḥ sva prakāśa tvam anavasthā tatas  na hi tātkālikam pramāṇa tvam akṣajasya yadā bhavet  aikya āgamasya kim na syāt  tasya api etādṛśam yadi aikya prāmāṇya mithyā tvam yadā viśvasya satyatā aikya āgamasya māna tvam yadi abādhyam iti iṣyate akṣa jasya api māna tvam na abādhyam kim iti iṣyate advaita hāni sāmānyāt na viśeṣaḥ ca kaścana yadi svatas tvam prāmāṇye viśvasattā katham na te prāmāṇyasya ca maryādā kālataḥ  vyāhatā bhavet  kāla antare apyamānam ced idānīm mānatā kutas  mithyātva mānam mokṣe api mānam kim na iti bhaṇya tām māna tve advaita hāniḥ syādamāna tve api amokṣa tā viśvasya punar āpattiḥ mithyāmānam yadā na mā asti ced mukta yavasthā ca dvaita āpattiḥ atas  anyathā amukta tvam tathā kāle kāla adhīnā hi mukta tā kāla eva āgamaḥ  api āha muktim kāla nivartane mukteḥ api nivṛttiḥ syāt  saṃsāri tvam atas  bhavet  kva ca pratyakṣataḥ prāptam anumāgama bādhitam deha ātma tvam yadi na tad  prāptam pratyakṣataḥ kvacid  mama deha iti hi eva na dehaḥ  aham iti pramā upacāraḥ ca kṛṣṇaḥ  aham iti kardama lepane vastrasya yadvat evam syāt  yadi upādhi kṛtam tadā svatas  śukla tvavat  kārṣṇyam na mama iti pratīyate katham ca bhedaḥ  deha ādeḥ ātmanaḥ  na pramīyate jāta mātrā mṛgā gāvaḥ  hastinaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ  khaṣāḥ bhaya abhaya sva bhoga ādau kāraṇāni vijānate asmṛtau pūrva dehasya vijñānam tad  katham bhavet  anvaya vyatireka ādeḥ anusandhāna vismṛtau yadā deha antara jñānam deha aikyau  asitiḥ kutas  vyāpta tvāt ātmanaḥ  dehe vyavahāreṣu apāṭavāt  bheda jñāne api ca aṅgāra vahnivat  svāviviktavat  bhavanti vyavahārāḥ ca na hi pratyakṣa gān api arthān yathā anubhavataḥ pratipādayitum kṣamāḥ lokāḥ tatas  hi pratyakṣa siddham na anyena kenacid  śakyam vārayitum kvāpi tad ced na uttara gocaram katham eva uttaraḥ kālaḥ tad gaḥ mokṣaḥ ca gamyate āgamaḥ  api hi sāmānye siddhe pratyakṣataḥ punar  viśeṣam gamayet eva katham śakti grahaḥ  anyathā atīta anāgata artheṣu jāte śakti grahe akhilam viśeṣam jñāpayet  vākyam na tad ajñāta śaktike śaktiḥ ced  vartamāne syāt na atīta anāgatam vadet  yadi śakti grahaḥ  anyatra katham sa syāt  tad agrahe sāmānyam dṛṣṭam eva asau  anyatra gamayet  yadi sāmānya varjitam vastu svarūpam gamayet  katham na svarūpatva sāmānyam kena api aṅgīkṛtam kvacid  svarūpam ced anugatam vyāvṛttam tatra kim bhavet  sarva anugata dharmāṇām ante hi sva tvam iṣyate kim vyāvṛttam iti praśne svarūpam iti kevalam syāt uttaram tatas  anyat ced  tad eva svayam eva naḥ evam vyāvṛtta rūpe api yadā śakti grahaḥ  bhavet  tasya sāmānyatas  jñānam vinā sa ca bhavet  kutas  atas  viśeṣa sāmānya rūpam sarvam api iṣyate vyāvṛttam yad ca sāmānyam tad eva syāt  viśeṣataḥ naca eka dharma tā tena padārthānām parasparam dharmāṇām bheda dṛṣṭayā eva tad sādṛśyasya darśanāt  atas  sarva padārthāḥ ca sāmānyāt  sākṣi gocarāḥ sarvam iti eva vijñānam sarveṣām katham anyathā kiñcid sādṛśya vijñānāt akhilasya api vastunaḥ śabda śakti grahaḥ ca syāt  tad tad sādṛśya mānataḥ pratyakṣam mānasam ca eva yadā atīta artha gocaram tadā smṛti pramāṇa tvam atītatva viśeṣitam ādhikyam anubhūtāt tu yadā atīta tvam iṣyate mānatā ca katham na syāt  smṛteḥ bādhaḥ ca na atra hi māna tvam pratyabhijñāyā api sarva anubhūti gam atīta vartamānatva dharmiṇī sā ca dṛśyate na ca sā smṛti mātra ardhā tad idantu agraha ekatas  atas  na vatarmāna eka niyamaḥ syāt  grahe akṣaje na ca pramāṇataḥ  anyā syāt  pramitiḥ nāma kutracid  māna abhāvāt  gauravāt ca kalpanāyāḥ kim etayā mayā etad jñātam iti tu sākṣi gam jñāna gocaram jñānam eva tatas  anyā na pramitiḥ nāma dṛśyate māna amātṛ prameyāṇām tad ucchittiḥ na hi kvacid  svapnānām api ca eteṣām na bādhaḥ  dṛśyate kvacid  jāgrattva mātram atra ekam anyathā dṛśyate sphuṭam atas  mithyā na ca svapnaḥ  jāgratvat ja agradeva ca ātmavat  kvacid ātmā ca syāt eva bhrama gocaraḥ etāvatā na mithyā asau svapne jāgarite tathā yadi ātmani anyathā dṛśyam bhrāntam atra api tad  bhavet  abādhita anuvṛtteḥ tu svapna ādeḥ bhrānta tā kutas  na ca kācid  pramā viśva bhrānta tve sarvam eva ca abhra anta tve pramāṇam tu katham tad bhrānti tā bhavet  kiñca bhrāntatva vādī sa bhrānta tvam sva matasya ca aṅgīkaroti niyatam tatra sampratipanna tā vādinoḥ tena ca abhrāntam viśvam eva bhaviṣyati bhrāntitva bhrānta tā ced  syāt  katham na abhrānti satya tā aśeṣa doṣa duṣyam tad matam heyam bubhūṣibhiḥ yena sva mata heya tvam svayam aṅgīkṛtam sadā bhrānti tvāt  durghaṭa tvasya bhūṣaṇa tvāt ca kevalam unmattaḥ  api katham tasya matam svīkartum icchati īśa śakteḥ acintya tvāt mahā unmattaiḥ pravartitam atas  prajñā atra māyā uktā jaivī upādānam eva sā nimittam aiśvarī mukhyam nirmitam trātam eva ca tābhyām saha pṛthak  ca eva māyā mātram iti īryate ubhābhyām mātam aiśvaryā trātam saha pṛthak  tatas  prajñā ātmakam manaḥ  yena manaḥ rūpāḥ ca vāsanāḥ dhīrbhīḥ iti manaḥ tu eva iti āha ca śrutiḥ añjasā cit acit miśram eva etad manaḥ  yāvat ca saṃsṛtiḥ tena avasthā imāḥ sarvā jīvaḥ paśyati sarvadā manaḥ vikārā viṣayāḥ svāpnā yad  bahyavat na te sthūlā bhavanti atas teṣām spaṣṭa tā na tathā kvacid  kvacid  spaṣṭā api syuṣye vāsanā mānasī ca sā īśa icchayā antardadhāti vyajyate ca punar tayā sṛṣṭvā eva vāsānabhiḥ ca prapañcam svāpnam īśvaraḥ vāsanā mātra tām tasya nītvā antardhāpayati ajaḥ suṣupti moha bodhān  ca svavaśaḥ tad vaśam sadā jīvam nayati deveśaḥ  na anyaḥ kartā asya kaścana na sthāna bhedataḥ  api asya bhedaḥ kaścid  pareśituḥ sarvatra aśeṣa doṣa ujkha pūrṇa kalyāṇa cidguṇaḥ tad viruddham tu yad  tatra mānam na eva bhavet  kvacid  mahātātparya rodhena katham tad mānam atra tu duḥkha apyaya sukha  āpti hetu tvena eva veda vāc  bhavet mānam tad īśānāt prasannāt eva na anyathā prasanna tā guṇa utkarṣa jñānāt eva hi kevalam nirdoṣa tā parijñānāt api na anyena kenacid  yaḥ  mām aśeṣa doṣa ujkham guṇa sarva sva bṛṃhitam jānāti asmai prasannaḥ  aham dadyām muktim naca anyathā yaḥ  mām aśeṣa abhyadhikam vijānāti sa eva mām vijānāti akhilān  tasya dadyām kāmān param padam yaḥ  mām evam asammūḍhaḥ kim mā nindanti śatravaḥ ityādi veda smṛti gavākyaiḥ eva avasīyate lokataḥ ca prasādena muktiḥ sa guṇa vedanāt  mahātātparya mukhyasya virodhādata eva hi doṣitva nirguṇatva alpa guṇatva ādi kathañcana na arthaḥ śruti purāṇa ādeḥ tad viruddhaḥ  akhilasya ca arthaḥ svayam vinirṇītaḥ  vāsudevena sādaram iti guhyatamam śāstram idam uktam mayā anagha etad  buddhvā buddhimān syāt  kṛtakṛtyaḥ ca bhārata iti atas  akhila sat śāstra viruddha tvena na anumā vartate tatra tena īśaḥ  nirṇītaḥ  akhila sat guṇaḥ na ca cit tvāt abhinna tvam jīvasya īśavat āpyate yata ābhāsatām eva śrutiḥ asya vadati alam yathā eṣā puruṣe cchāyā etasmin  etad ātatam chāyā yathā puṃsadṛśā pumā adhīnā ca dṛśyate evam eva ātmakāḥ sarve brahma ādyāḥ paramātmanaḥ sattā pratīti kāryeṣu pum adhīnaḥ  yatheyate ābhāsa eva puruṣā muktāḥ ca paramātmanaḥ chāyā viṣṇaḥ ramā tasyāḥ chāyā dhātā viśeṣakau tasya indra kāmau ca tayoḥ tayoḥ anye akhilā api hareḥ brahma asya gīḥ tasyāḥ  viśeṣau  indra etayoḥ māraḥ ca ābhāsakāḥ sarva etayoḥ tad adhīnataḥ sarve alpa śaktayaḥ ca eva pūrṇa śaktiḥ paraḥ  hariḥ cetana tve api bhinnāḥ te tasmāt etena sarvadā ityādi śruti vākyebhyaḥ  jñāyate bheda eva hi ābhāsa tvam hi nirṇītam jīvasya paramātmanaḥ tad na yuktam yadābhāsa upādhyāyatta īyate upādhi āyatta tā bhāvāt ābhāsatva virodhataḥ cetana tvena ca aṃśa tvāt  samudāya aikyam āpatet  atas  pṛthaktavam uditam samudāya aṃśayoḥ bhavet  īśā ākhyā samudāye syāt īśa rūpeṣu iva uditā atas  deha ādi upādhīnām apāye sama tā bhavet  īśa rūpaiḥ atha ābhāsā mukhyatas  sūryaka ādivat  yadā tadā upādhi āyatta rūpāṇām nāśitā bhavet  iti āśaṅkā nivṛtti artham āha veda adhipaḥ prabhuḥ ata eva upamā iti eva ca anya ābhāsa viśeṣitām yad uktam tad adhīna tvam sarva avasthāsu aśeṣataḥ jīvasya sadṛśa tvam ca cittva mātram naca aparam tāvat mātreṇa ca ābhāsaḥ  rūpam eṣām cit ātmanām na upādhi adhīnata ādyaiḥ ca na ati sāmyam nidarśane kiñcid sukha ādi sādṛśyam api īśenesura anṛte tatas  ābhāsate nityam tadvat ābhāsate api ca bhānam asti tvam apica eva asamantād yatas tatas  jīva ābhāsa uddiṣṭaḥ sadā eva paramātmanaḥ na jala āyatta sūrya ādi pratibimba upama tvataḥ tad adhīna tvam eva iti kiñcid  sādṛśyam eva ca samprakāśayataḥ sūtra gatau  akhila mānataḥ jīveśa bheda dṛṣṭayā eva samudāya eka tā kutas  aśeṣa doṣa rāhityam sarva śakti tvataḥ  hareḥ sarva upeta iti kathitam ata aikyam kva doṣiṇā aśeṣa śakti yuktaḥ ced  svātantryāt  doṣavān katham anusandhāna rahitam aikyam ced ekatā na tad  cetana aikye anusandhānam pramāṇam na eva ca aparam anusandhāna rahita samudāya aikyam eva ced  cetaneṣu astu tad nāma mātram eva yatas tatas  muktau syāt anusandhānam ced mithyā jñānitā bhavet  sarvajña ekatām na anusandhatte na eva sā yatas  paścāt  syāt anusandhānam ced mithyā jñānitā bhavet  vidyamāna anusandhānam na ced ajña tvam āpatet asat aikyam bhavet  paścāt  yadi syāt  saptamaḥ  rasaḥ samudāya aikyam etasmāt  dūratas  apākṛtam sadā atas  aśeṣa guṇa unnaddham nirdoṣam yāvat eva hi tāvat eva īśvaraḥ  nāma tatra bhedaḥ  api na kvacid  na iha nānā asti kim api harayaḥ  ayam ayam hi saḥ ityādi śruti mānena jīva aṃśāḥ sarva eva ca niyamena anusandhānavantaḥ  yadi eka tā svatas  aṃśinaḥ aśeṣa sandhānam ati alpasya api vidyate bhuvi jātena ca aṃśena sukha duḥkha ādi tad gatam anubhūyate viśeṣaḥ tu kaścid īśa kṛtaḥ  bhavet  īśasya acintya śakti tvāt na aśakyam kvāpi vidyate sa īśata anupapannā eva yadi jīva eka tā asya hi anīśasya īśata iti eva viruddham sarva mānataḥ īśa tvena eva vijñātam anīśa tvena ced śrutiḥ anīśa tvena vijñātam īśa tvena athavā diśet  upajīvya virodhena na eva māna tvam eṣyati ata eva īśata asiddheḥ na kiñcid śakyam asya ca īśa tve anīśa bhedena śrutyā samyak  prakāśite ayuktam api ca anyatra yuktam bhavati tad balāt  atas  anyatra api yad  dṛṣṭam tad īśena eva kalpyate śruti ābhāsa āptam api na hi īśatva paripanthi yad  īśaḥ  anīśaḥ  jagat mithyā duḥkhī muktaḥ  bhidā na hi iti pratijñā vyāghātaḥ sarva doṣa adhika adhikaḥ iti hi brahma tarka uktiḥ ati heyam atas  akhilaiḥ bubhūṣubhiḥ matam idam jīveśa abheda vādinaḥ na ayuktam īśituḥ kiñcid īśa tvasya avirodhi yad  yadi īśitva virodhi syāt  tad eva ayuktam añjasā īśitvasya avirodhena yojayitvā akhilāḥ pramāḥ siddha īśi tvena ca ayuktam api hi īśe na yojayet  mānataḥ prāptam akhilam nāmānam yojayet  kvacid  iti hi brahma tarka uktiḥ atas  yuktam iha uditam sa ca aprākṛta rūpa tvāt arūpaḥ sva guṇa śatmakam rūpam asya śiraḥ pāṇi pāda ādi ātmakam iṣyate atas  na anitya tā na eva śruti dvaya virodhitā yathā hi taijasasya eva prakāśasya ujkhitau  api ātmā eva jyotiḥ iti āha jīvasya īśam śrutiḥ tathā tad bhakti tāratamyena tāratamyam vimukti gam brahma ādīnām ca sarveṣām ānanda ādeḥ yathākramam pratibimbavat api eṣām ānandaḥ  anya guṇā yathā nārāyaṇa guṇa adhīnaḥ ca ati alpaḥ tad apekṣayā tasmāt  bhinnaḥ ca satatam anyat jñānam parasya ca anyat jñānam tu jīvānām anya ānanda īśatā mukhyeśatā pareśasya gauṇī jīvasya sā yatas  iti śruteḥ sṛṣṭi nāśau tad adhīna aviti īrite svabhāva tvāt  sthiteḥ na etad apekṣā iti na yujyate yatas  svabhāvaḥ  akhila īśa āyattaḥ  akhilasya ca avyaktaḥ  api svaktayā eva bhaktānām dṛśyate hariḥ tad abhinnā guṇā nityam api sarve viśeṣataḥ guṇa tvena guṇi tvena bhoktṛ bhogya tayā sthitāḥ viśeṣa ātma tayā teṣām nitya śaktayā ātmanā tathā nitya sthiteḥ na dharmāṇām kriyā ādīnām anitya tā na viśeṣa ātma tā ca iyam anityā śakti rūpa tā sā eva yad  sa viśeṣā syāt  viśeṣaḥ  anyaḥ  naca api ayam sva nirvāha ka tā hetoḥ tathā api syāt  viśeṣataḥ viśeṣa tvena vijñāteḥ pramāṇaiḥ akhilaiḥ api sasarja sañjahāra iti viśeṣaḥ  hi avagamyate śrutyā eva sa sa eva iti tad abhedaḥ ca gamyate bhedaḥ  yadi viśeṣasya sa bhedaḥ  bhedinā katham bhinnaḥ ced anavasthā syāt abhinnaḥ ced  purā na kim viśeṣaḥ  abhinna eva iti tena na abhyupagamyate abhinnaḥ nivirśeṣaḥ ced  bhedaḥ tad bheda tā kutas  anena anena bhinnaḥ ayam iti yad  sa viśeṣataḥ bheda eva eṣa bahudhā dṛśyate tad  kim uttaram abheda bhedayoḥ ca eva svarūpa tvam hi bhedinā tayoḥ api aviśeṣa tve paryāya tvam hi śabdayoḥ abheda bheda śabdau ca paryāyau  iti kaḥ  vadet  bhedaḥ  anyonyam abhedaḥ ca bhedinā ced  viśeṣa tā nirviśeṣe katham bhedaḥ  bhedina ekaḥ tathā abhidā punar tayoḥ vibhedaḥ ca bhedi mātra tvataḥ  bhavet  bhedinaḥ ca eva bhedasya viśeṣaḥ  yadi gamyate abheda abhedinoḥ ca eva kim bhedaḥ  abheda bhedayoḥ viśeṣeṇa eva sarvatra yadi vyavahṛtiḥ bhavet  kalpanā gauravāya eva kim bhedaḥ kalpyate tadā aikya pratīti abhāvena bheda eva gavaśvayoḥ sa eva iti pratītau hi viśeṣaḥ  nāma bhaṇyate saccit ādera paryāya siddhayartham māyinā api hi aṅgīkāryaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  ayam yadi asati aviśeṣaṇam pṛthak  pṛthak  vārayitum śabda antaram iti iṣyate māyā viśeṣa rāhitya viśeṣeṇa viśeṣitā satyasya api bhavet  sā ca tathā ced anavasthitiḥ yadi satye viśeṣaḥ  na na tad uktiḥ bhavet tadā lakṣyate ced  tena lakṣyam iti api syāt  viśeṣitā punar punar lakṣaṇāyām api syāt anavasthitiḥ yadi abhāva viśeṣi tvam syāt aṅgīkṛtam eva te asārvajñyādirāhityam api evam te bhaviṣyati tadā sārvajñyam eva syāt  bhāva artha tvāt nañoḥ dvayoḥ yadi na etādṛśam grāhyam asukhatva anivartanāt asattva jñāna tā ādeḥ ca syāt asattva ādikam tadā anṛta ādi virodhi tvam yadi asya abhyupagamyate anaiśvarya virodhi tvam api evam kim nivāryate akhaṇḍa khaṇḍanāt evam viśeṣaḥ akhaṇḍa vādinā khaṇḍitena api manasā svīkāryaḥ ananyathāgateḥ akhaṇḍa khaṇḍa vādibhyām khaṇḍākhaṇḍena ca eva tad  mahā ādareṇa śirasi viśeṣaḥ  dhārya eva hi nidarśana trayeṇa atas  bhagavān atyabhinna tām guṇānām ādareṇa āha tad ca na abhihita anvayaḥ yadā aśeṣa viśeṣāṇa muktiḥ sāmānyatas  bhavet  pada ekena api uttareṇa viśeṣa avagatiḥ bhavet  yatas  aśeṣa viśeṣāṇām vastunā asti eva ca ekatā atas  sāmānyatas  jñātaḥ pada antara balāt punar  bhavet  viśeṣataḥ  jñānaḥ tena syāt anvita uktitā sva artha eva anvitaḥ yasmāt  kenacid  tad viśeṣataḥ anena iti tad uktayā eva jñāyate anubhavena hi yadi ananvitam eva etad  padam sva artham vadet iha tathā anyāni api sarvāṇi kaḥ kuryāt anvayam punar  vyāpāraḥ  na hi śabdasya paraḥ sva artha prakāśanāt  pumān api eka vāra uktayā kṛtakṛtyaḥ  yadā bhavet  anvayasya katham jñānam śabda artha tvam yadā asya na yadā eva ananvita arthasya vacanam taiḥ padaibharvet  ananvitaḥ syāt śabda arthaḥ  na tad arthaḥ  hi saḥ  anvayaḥ nirākāṅkṣa padāni eva vākyam iti ucyate budhaiḥ tad tad artha abhidhānena syāt nirākāṅkṣatā ca sā apūrteḥ tāvat arthānām ākāṅkṣā pūrvam iṣyate karma kartṛ kriyāṇām tu pūrtau kaḥ  anyaḥ  anvayaḥ  bhavet  apūrtiḥ ced  padaiḥ uktaiḥ kim nṛ śṛṅgeṇa pūryate vyāpāraḥ ced  punar teṣām anuktau  api kim na saḥ ukte buddhi sthatā hetoḥ yadi vyāpāra iṣyate buddhi stha tvāya yatnam na katham kuryuḥ purā eva ca puruṣa adhīna tā teṣām yadi paścāt ca sā samā pumān eva anvayāya eṣām paścāt  yadi viceṣyate ananvita abhidhānānām sa eva artha antara uktiṣu yatatām śabda śaktiḥ ced  tatra na eva anvaye katham tad kalpanā gurutva ādi doṣetaḥ  abhihita anvayaḥ anubhūti viruddhaḥ ca tyājya eva manīṣibhiḥ kartṛ śabde hi abhihite dharma sāmānya vedanāt viśeṣa dharmam anvicchan kim iti eva hi pṛcchati guṇa kriyā ādi dharmāṇām viśeṣe kathite punar  nirākāṅkṣaḥ  bhavet  yasmāt śabdā anvita vācakāḥ atas  ananta guṇa ātmā ekaḥ  bhagavān eka eva tu ucyate sarva vedaiḥ ca te ca akhila vilakṣaṇāḥ sarve sarva guṇa ātmānaḥ sarva kartāra eva ca tathā api sa viśeṣāḥ ca vidvadi vutpattitaḥ  apica taiḥ taiḥ śabdaiḥ ca bhaṇyante yujyate ca upadeśataḥ anya ānanda ādi sādṛśyam ānu kūlya ādinā param pūrṇatva ādi mahat  teṣām vailakṣaṇyam śrutau śrutam pūrṇe aśeṣa niyantā ca sukha at utam eka kalaḥ guṇa uru samudāyaḥ  ayam vāsudevaḥ sa niṣkaḷaḥ vāsudeva śrutiḥ sā eṣā guṇān vakti hareḥ parān sa eva aśeṣa jīva stha nissaṅkha yāna ādi kālikān dharma adharmān sadā paśyan sva icchayā bodhayati ajaḥ kāṃścid  teṣām phalam ca eva dadāti svayam acyutaḥ na te viśeṣam kam api preraṇa ādikam ucyate kuryuḥ kadāpi tena ayam svatantraḥ  anupacārataḥ karmāṇi tāni ca pṛthak  cetanāni eva sarvaśas  acetana śarīrāṇi sva karma phala bhāñci ca pratyekam teṣu ca ananta karmāṇi evaṃvidhāni ca tāni ca evam iti īśasya nissīmā śaktiḥ uttamā ekā eva brahmahatyā hi varāha hariṇā uditā brahmapāra stavena eva niṣkrāntā rāja dehataḥ stotrasya tasya māhātmyāt  vyādha tvam gamitā punar  prāpya jñānam param ca apa tathā anyāni api sarvadā anantāni uditāni evam prabhuṇā kapilena hi saṃsāre pacyamānāni karmāṇi api pṛthak  pṛthak  tasmāt ananta māhātmya guṇa pūgaḥ  janārdanaḥ bhaktyā paramayā arādhya iti pādārtha  īryate vairāgyataḥ  bhakti dārḍhyam tena upāsā yadā bhavet  āparokṣyam bhavet  viṣṇoḥ iti pāda kramaḥ  bhavet  yuktitaḥ  jñāta veda arthaḥ  nirasya samayān parān paraspara virodham ca praṇudya aśeṣa vākya gam adhyātma praṇavaḥ  bhūtvā tasya sannihita tvataḥ bahu yukti virodhānām bhānāt  tad sahita śruteḥ virodham ca nirākṛtya śrutīnām prāṇataḥ tvagān parihṛtya virodhān  ca tad prasāda anurañjitaḥ deha kartṛ tvam īśasya jñātvā tad pitṛtā smṛteḥ viśeṣa sneham āpādya sarva kartṛ tvatas  adhikam niṣpādya bahu mānam ca tad anyatra ati duḥkhataḥ utpādya adhika vairāgyam tad guṇa ādhikya vedanāt sarvasya tad vaśa tvāt ca dārḍhyam bhakteḥ avāpya ca yateta upāsanāya eva viśiṣṭa ācārya sampadā kartavyā brahma jijñāsā iti ukte kim iti saṃśaye ata iti udite api asya viśeṣa anuktitaḥ punar  sṛṣṭi bandhana mokṣa ādi kartṛ tvasya śrutatvataḥ yatas  mokṣa ādi dātāsāvataḥ  jijñāsya eva vaḥ iti āha tad  param brahma vyāsa ākhyam jñāna raśmimat  yena eva bandha mokṣaḥ syāt  sa ca jijñāsayā gataḥ su prasannaḥ  bhavet īśaḥ  jijñāsātaḥ  asya mukti dā mokṣāt idatvam īśasya katham eva avagamyate iti ced śāstra yoni tvāt śāstra gamyaḥ  hi mokṣa daḥ pratyakṣa avasitebhyaḥ syāt  yadi mokṣaḥ kathañcana kim iti anādi saṃsāra magnāḥ sarvā imāḥ prajāḥ yasmāt niyamataḥ  duḥkha hāniḥ pratyakṣataḥ bhavet  dhāvanti eva tam uddiśya rāja ādyam akhilāḥ prajāḥ anumāna gamyataḥ  mokṣaḥ  yadi tasya anumā eva hi dṛṣṭa pūruṣavat mokṣa dātṛ tām vinivārayet  tad śāstra gamya eva ekaḥ  mokṣa daḥ  bhavati dhruvam śāstra gamyaḥ ca na anyaḥ  asti mokṣa da tvena keśavāt  mokṣa daḥ  hi svatantraḥ syāt  paratantraḥ svayam sṛtau vartamānaḥ katham śaktaḥ para mokṣāya kevalam anya āśrayeṇa yadi eṣa dadyāt mokṣam sa eva hi tena ananusṛtaḥ  mokṣam na dadyāt anya vākyataḥ atas tad artham api sa jñeyaḥ  viṣṇuḥ mumukṣibhiḥ yam eva eṣa iti śrutyā tam eva iti ca sādaram śāstra yoni tvam asya eva jñāyate veda vādibhiḥ ya enam viduḥ amṛtā iti uktaḥ tu samudra gaḥ tad eva brahma paramam iti śrutyā avadhāritaḥ yatas  prasūtā iti tatas  sṛṣṭim āha tatas  hariḥ śāstra yoniḥ naca anyaḥ  asti mukhyatas tu iti gamyate śāstra yoni tvam etasya jñāyate hi samanvayāt  samiti hi upasargeṇa para mukhyāthaṛtā ucyate evam parama mukhya arthaḥ  nārāyaṇa iti śruteḥ nirdhāraṇāya na aśabdam iti veda patiḥ jagau katham samanvayaḥ  jñeyaḥ su alpa śākhā vidām nṛṇām vedā hi anantā iti hi śrutiḥ āha api anantatām ananta veda nirṇītiḥ mahā praḷaya vāridheḥ uttāraṇa upamā iti asmān na jñeyaḥ  atra samanvayaḥ iti śaṅkā apanoda artham sa āha karuṇā karaḥ aśakya uttaraṇa tve api hi āgama apāra vāridheḥ nirṇīyate mayā eva ayam romakūpalayodinā yadi api aśeṣa veda arthaḥ  durgamaḥ  akhila mānavaiḥ mad jñāna avyākṛta ākāśe prāpnoti parama aṇu tām iti prakāśayan viśvapatiḥ āha prameya tām nikhilasya api vedasya gati sāmānyam añjasā kaḥ  nāma gati sāmānyam ananta āgama sampadaḥ jñāna sūryam ṛte brūyāt  tam ekam bādarāyaṇam anyaḥ  api alpa matiḥ śākhā catuṣpañca gatam vasu jānanna anumita tvena brūyāt  tasya prasādataḥ iti mukhya tayā aśeṣa gati sāmānya vid  prabhuḥ pratijajñe dṛḍham yasmāt  devānām api pūryate atas  nikhila vedānām siddha evam samanvayaḥ iti su jñāpita arthaḥ  api pṛthak  ca āha samanvayam tatra prathamatas  anyatra prasiddhānām samanvayaḥ śabdānām vācya eva atra mahā malleśa bhaṅgavat  itas  ati abhyadhika tve api turya pāda uditasya tu mahā samanvaye tasmin na adhikāraḥ  akhilasya hi brahma eva adhikṛtaḥ tatra mukhyataḥ anye yathākramam durgama tvāt ca na eva atra prāthamyena uditaḥ  añjasā atas  anyatra prasiddhānām śabdānām nirṇayāya tu pravṛttaḥ prathamam devaḥ tatra ānanda ādayaḥ  guṇāḥ īśasya eva iti nirṇītāḥ śruti yukti samāśrayāt devatā antara gāḥ sarve śabda vṛtti nimittatas viṣṇum eva vadanti addhā tad saṅgāt upacārataḥ anya devān vadanti iha viśeṣa guṇa vaktṛtaḥ viṣṇum eva param brūyuḥ evam anye api aśeṣatas  iti anyatra prasiddha ūru śabda rāśeḥ aśeṣatas  jñāte samanvaye viṣṇau liṅgaiḥ hi eṣa samanvayaḥ teṣām anya gata tve tu na syāt  samyak  samanvayaḥ iti eva aśeṣa liṅgānām brahmaṇi eva samanvayam āha ubhaya gata tvam ca syāt atas  liṅga śabdayoḥ iti saṃśaya nutti artham ubhayatra pratītitaḥ śabdānām vartamānānām sa liṅgānām viśeṣataḥ samanvayaḥ  harau  eva yad na eva anyatra mukhyatas  śabdā liṅgāni ca yatas  na eva anyatra svatantra tā asvatantreṣu śabdasya vṛtti hetuḥ na mukhyatas  yatas  atas  yad adhīnāḥ te śabda artha tvam upāgatāḥ ati alpena eva śabdasya vṛtti hetu guṇena tu ayaḥ  yathā dāhaka tvam sa eva īśaḥ svatantrataḥ mukhya śabda artha iti hi svīkartavyaḥ  manīṣibhiḥ iti āha evañca śabdānām nārāyaṇa samanvaye siddhe api aśeṣa śabdānām na kathañcana yujyate virodhau  avaratva ādeḥ api prāptiḥ yatas  bhavet  iti ced avaratva ādi dvividham hi upalabhyate parasya āvarata ahetuḥ yaḥ svayam para eva san saḥ  api hi avara śabda arthaḥ  yathā rājā jayī bhavet  anyaḥ  avara tvā anubhavī tayoḥ pūrvaḥ asti keśave dvitīyaḥ  jīva eva asti svātantrān na ca dūṣaṇam hareḥ evam aśeṣeṇa sarva śabda samanvaye ukte virodha hīnasya syāt  samanvayatā yatas  atas  aśeṣa virodhānām kṛta īśena nirākṛtiḥ samanvaya avirodhābhyām san jāte vastu nirṇaye kim mayā kāryam iti eva syāt  buddhiḥ adhikāriṇaḥ tatra bhakti vidhāna artham abhakta anartha santatau uktāyām bhakti dārḍhyāya prokte aśeṣa guṇa uccaye vaktavya upāsanā nityam kartavyā iti ādareṇa hi sa upāsanā ca dvividhā śāstra abhyāsa svarūpiṇī dhyāna rūpā parā ca eva tad aṅgam dhāraṇa ādikam tathā ubhaya ātmakam ca eva pāde asmin bādarāyaṇaḥ āha upāsana m addhava vistarāt śruti pūrvakam pṛthak dṛṣṭiḥ aśakya tvam anirṇītiḥ samuccayaḥ viśeṣa darśanam kārya lopaḥ  nānā uktiḥ āśu tā vibhramaḥ  apākṛtiḥ liṅgam anavasthā viśeṣitā aprayojana tā ca atiprasaṅgaḥ  adūra saṃśrayaḥ viśiṣṭa kāraṇam ceṣyā dṛṣṭa vairūpyam unnatiḥ anuktiḥ aprayatna tvam dṛḍha bandha parābhavau puṃsāmyam prāpta santyāgaḥ kāraṇa anirṇayaḥ  bhramaḥ viśeṣa darśitā alāpaḥ  guṇa sāmyam pṛthak dṛśiḥ agamyavartma sandhānam iṣṭam phalam akalpanā śuddha vairūpyam aṅga tvam aviśeṣa dṛśiḥ kriyā yuktayaḥ pūrva pakṣa sthāḥ su jñeya tvam vidhi kriyā māhātmyam alpa śakti tvam yathāyogya phalam bhavaḥ phala sāmyam viśeṣaḥ ca guṇa ādhikyam pradhāna tā yathāśakti kriyā sandhiḥ pramāṇa balam ānatiḥ kāraṇam kārya vaiśeṣyam svabhāvaḥ  vastu dūṣaṇam pratikriyā virodhaḥ ca pratisandhiḥ anūna tā saṃskāra pāṭavam sva icchā niyatiḥ vastu vaibhavam viśeṣa uktiramāna tvam prādhānyam prītiḥ āgamaḥ su sthira tvam kṛta prāptiḥ anādi guṇa vistaraḥ sādhana uttama tā nānā dṛṣṭiḥ śiṣṭiḥ anūna tā avighnatva virodhau ca guṇa vaiśeṣyam āgamaḥ siddhānta nirṇaye hi etā yuktayaḥ avyāhatāḥ sadā yathāśaktayakhilān vedān vijñāya upāsanam bhavet  tatra akhilasya vijñaptiḥ samyak  brahmaṇa eva hi tad anyeṣām yathāyogyam akhila jñaptiḥ iṣyate tāvatā upāsane yogyaḥ  bhavet eva akhilaḥ pumān mahattvasya param pāram viditvā eva janārdanaḥ stoṣya tām eti tuṣṭa tvam iti na asti eva nārada kintu niścalayā bhaktayā hi ātma jñāna anurūpataḥ yaḥ stoṣyati sadā bhaktaḥ tuṣyaḥ tasya sadā hariḥ ityādi vākya sandarbhāt  yathāyogya akhila jña tā ātma jñāna anurūpa tvam yathāśakti vicāraṇāt  vedaḥ kṛtsnaḥ  adhigantavyaḥ svādhyāya adhyayanam bhavet  ityādi vākya vaiyarthyam anyathā na nivāryate adya api tena deva ādyāḥ śṛṇvate manvate sadā dhyāyanti ca yathāyogam tathā āpyā vastu nirṇayāt  śravaṇam mananam ca eva kartavyam sarvathā eva hi mati śruti dhyāna kāla viśeṣam guruḥ uttamaḥ vetti tasya ukti mārgeṇa kurvataḥ syāt hi darśanam śravaṇam dṛṣṭa tattvasya mananam dhyānam eva ca viśeṣa ānanda samprāptyā anyasya etāni dṛṣṭaye yadi tādṛś  guruḥ na asti nirṇīta śravaṇa ādikam tad siddhānta anusāreṇa nirṇaya jñāt  samācaret  śravaṇa ādi vinā na eva kṣaṇam tiṣṭhet api kvacid  atyaśakye tu nidrā ādau punar eva samārabhet  abhāve nirṇaya jñasya sat śāstrāṇi eva sarvadā śṛṇuyāt  yadi sat jñāna prācuryam upalabhyate mahat bhayaḥ  viṣṇu bhaktebhyaḥ  yathāśakti ca saṃśayān chindyāt  svatas  adhika abhāve svayam eva samabhyaset  aśeṣa guṇa pūrṇa tvam sarva doṣa samujkhitiḥ viṣṇoḥ anyat ca tad tantram iti samyak  vinirṇayaḥ svatantra tvam sadā tasya tasya bhedaḥ ca sarvatas  adoṣa tvasya siddhayartham yad abhede tad anvayaḥ tad tantra tvam ca muktānām api tad guṇa pūrtaye muktānām api bhedaḥ ca na hi bhinnam abhinnatām gacchat  dṛṣṭam kvacid  tasya api abhāvaḥ  anubhava upagaḥ pūrva abhede doṣavat tvam īśasya iti ati bhinna tā nārāyaṇena muktānām api samyak iti sthitiḥ bheda abhede api abhedena doṣāṇām api sambhavaḥ nirdoṣa tvam ramāyāḥ ca tad anantara tā tathā brahmā sarasvatī vīndra śeṣa rudrāḥ ca tad sriyaḥ śakra kāmau tad anye ca kramāt muktau  api iti ca sat siddhānta iti jñeyaḥ  nirṇītaḥ  hariṇā svayam etad virodhi yad  sarvam tamase andhāya kevalam andham tamaḥ  viśanti iti prāha śrutiḥ ati sphuṭam iti eva śrutayaḥ aśeṣāḥ pañca rātram atha akhilam mūla rāmāyaṇam ca eva bhāratam smṛtayaḥ akhilāḥ vaiṣṇavāni purāṇāni sāṅkhaya yogau parau  api brahmatarkaḥ ca mīmāṃsā iti anantaḥ śabda sāgaraḥ anantara yuktayaḥ ca eva pratyakṣa āgama mūlakāḥ pratyakṣam aiśvaram ca eva rama ādīnām aśeṣatas  muktānām api amuktānām etam eva artham uttamam anya avakāśa rahitam prakāśayati sādaram etad eva ca sat śāstram duḥśāstram tu tatas  param sat śāstram abhyaset nityam duḥśāstram ca parityajet  asaṃśayena tattvasya nirṇaye brahma darśanam samyak viṣama vijñāna tāratamya anusārataḥ phalam bhavet  tāratamyāt  sukha duḥkha ātmakam nṛṇām samyak  ca adhika vijñānāt sukha ādhikyam bhavet nṛṇām atas  yathā ātma śaktayā eva śravaṇam mananam tathā viṣayeṣu ca saṃsargāt śāśvatasya ca saṃśayāt  manasā ca anyat ākāṅkṣāt  param na pratipādyate iti bhārata vākyam hi tena etad doṣa varjitaḥ sadā upāsanayā yuktaḥ  vāsudevam prapaśyati doṣā anādi sambaddhāḥ te mukti paripanthinaḥ santi eva prāyaśas  puṃsu tena mokṣaḥ  na jāyate sarve ta ete jīveṣu dṛśyante tāratamyataḥ ṛjūnām eka eva asti parama utsāha varjanam sa guṇa alpatva mātra tvāt narja tvena viruddhayate atas  viṣṇau parā bhaktiḥ tad bhakteṣu rama ādiṣu tāratamyena kartavyā puruṣa artham abhīpsitā svādaraḥ sarva jantūnām saṃsiddhaḥ  hi svabhāvataḥ tatas  adhikaḥ sva uttameṣu tad ādhikya anusārataḥ kartavyaḥ  vāsudeva antam sarvathā śubham icchatā na kadācid  tyajet  tam ca krameṇa enam vivardhayet  sameṣu sva ātmavat  snehaḥ satsu anyatra tatas  dayā kāryā evam āparokṣyeṇa dṛśyate kṣipram īśvaraḥ tad  tamaḥ  andham vrajet  viṣṇu sama tvam yaḥ  anupaśyati ramā brahma śiva ādīnām api muktau kathañcana kim uta ādhikya dṛṣṭeḥ tad  guṇa abhāva mateḥ api doṣa vettuḥ abhedasya draṣṭuḥ draṣṭuḥ tathā ubhayoḥ iti āha sat śrutiḥ tena samprokta guṇa saṃyutam upāsīta harim dṛṣṭvā muktiḥ tena eva jāyate dveṣāt  yad mukti kathanam śruti vākya virodhi yad  ripavaḥ  ye tu rāmasya vimukha tvāt nirāmiṇaḥ abhidroha pade nityam andhe tamasi te sthitāḥ haridviṣaḥ tamaḥ  yānti ye ca eva tad abhedinaḥ tad nirguṇatva vettāraḥ tasya doṣa vidaḥ  api ca ityādi śruti sandarbhāt  dveṣiṇaḥ tama īyate hiraṇyakaśipuḥ ca api bhagavat nindayā tamaḥ vidhi kṣuḥ ati agāt sūnaḥ prahlādasya anubhāvataḥ yad anindat pitā mahyam tvad bhakte mayi ca aghavān tasmāt  pitā me pūyeta durantāt  dustarāt aghāt nindām bhagavataḥ śṛṇvan  tatparasya janasya vā tatas  na apaiti yaḥ saḥ  api yāti aghaḥ sukṛtāt cyutaḥ avajānanti mām mūḍhā mānuṣīm tanum āśritam param bhāvam ajānantaḥ  mama bhūta maheśvaram mogha āśā mogha karmāṇaḥ  mogha jñānā vicetasaḥ rākṣasīm āsurīm ca eva prakṛtim mohanīm śritāḥ mām ātma para deheṣu pradviṣantaḥ  abhyasūyakāḥ tān aham dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu nara adhamān kṣipāmi ajasram aśubhān āsurīṣu eva yoniṣu āsurīm yonim āpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani mām aprāpya eva kaunteya tatas  yānti adhamām gatim yaḥ  dviṣṭāt  vibudha śreṣṭham devam nārāyaṇam prabhum katham sa na bhavet  dveṣya āloka antasya kasyacid  yaḥ  dviṣṭāt  vibudha śreṣṭham devam nārāyaṇam prabhum majjanti pitaraḥ tasya narake śāśvatīḥ samāḥ ityādi vākya sandohāt  dveṣiṇaḥ tama eva tu na eva mokṣa iti prāhuḥ lokāyata mate sthitāḥ bhogaḥ śarīra paryantam bhasmībhāvaḥ tatas  bhavet  iti tad  kena mānena dṛṣṭam pratyakṣa vādinā na hi pratyakṣamānena mokṣa abhāvaḥ  avasīyate ghaṭate mukti dṛṣṭiḥ tu puruṣeṇa mahīyasā na iti vaktuḥ mahat tvam tu kathañcana na vidyate sādhayan sarva sāmānyam katham eva viśeṣavān dṛśyante puruṣā loke parāvara vidaḥ  apica aparokṣa dṛśaḥ  yoga niṣṭhāḥ ca amala cakṣuṣaḥ pratyakṣam devatām dṛṣṭvā tad prasāda āpta bhūtayaḥ jñāna vijñāna pāra jñā niṣiddhayante katham nṛbhiḥ dṛśyate ca ati māhātmyam teṣām ati mahā ojasām yadi te api niṣiddhayante kim na uktiḥ te niṣiddhayate yad ukta vākya prāmāṇyam pratyakṣeṇa upalabhyate varādayaḥ  api tad dattāḥ sadā satyā bhavanti hi aprāmāṇyam tad ukteḥ ca vṛthā vācā avasīyate na hi prayojanam kiñcid  para loka nivāraṇāt vṛthā vācam vṛthā hanyāt  yadi tasya kim uttaram sva jīvana virodhāya vadan kim nāma buddhimān prāmāṇye saṃśayaḥ kim syāt  tayoḥ puruṣayoḥ api sva jīvana viruddha ukti rajñaḥ  dṛṣṭasya ca api saḥ yaḥ ca atīndriya deva ukti śrotā dṛṣṭa parāvaraḥ atīta anāgatam sarvam loka anubhavam āpayan atas  pratyakṣa gamya tvāt  vedamātvasya ca sphuṭam yadi āgamasya naḥ mātvam akṣajasya tathā bhavet  yadi akṣa jasya mātvam syāt āgamasya katham na tad  loka vākyāt  viśeṣaḥ ca avyabhicāreṇa siddhayati asti mokṣaḥ  api dharmeṇa yathā artha jñānataḥ api ca prāmāṇyam anumāyāḥ ca jinasya āptatva sādhane tad vākyāt  dharma sat jñāna vijñaptiḥ bhavati iti ca dharmaḥ  ahiṃsā paraḥ  na anyaḥ  jñānam pudgala darśanam iti jaināḥ katham tad  syāt  pramāṇam anumānataḥ viṣayān prati sthitam hi akṣam pratyakṣam iti gīyate pratyakṣa śabda anusārāt anumā iti prakītiḥ tā ā samantāt  gamayati dharma adharmau param padam yad ca api atīndriyam tu anyat  tena asau  āgamaḥ smṛtaḥ etena kāreṇena eva tad tad māna tvam iṣyate svarūpam hi tad eteṣām anyathā siddhi mānataḥ atas  anumā katham dharmam pudgalam ca api darśayet  svarūpam pudgalasya uktā doṣā ānandam eva ca na manyate pudgalam sa duḥkha abhāvaḥ sukham tu iti mātrā bhoga atirekeṇa sukha ādhikyasya darśanāt  sukhasya abhāva tā kena na ca syāt  kim viparyayaḥ yadi bhāvaḥ api kaścid  syāt  tasya eva abhāva tā kutas  yadi sarve api abhāvāḥ syuḥ anyonyam iti bhāvatā abhāva abhāva tā yad  syāt  kim naḥ chinnam tadā bhavet  bhāva tvam vidhi rūpa tvam niṣedha tvam abhāvatā niṣedhasya niṣedhaḥ  api bhāva eva balāt  bhavet  prathama pratipattiḥ tu bhāva bhāva niyāmikā na ca pudgala vijñānam mokṣa dam bhavati kvacid  asvātantryāt  pudgalasya jñātaḥ  api sukha daḥ  na hi na hi duḥkhi parijñānāt  duḥkhi tvam vinivartate yadi pudgala vijñānāt aduḥkhī syāt  kathañcana dehavān api na āduḥkhī kim jñānāt uttaram sadā īśa kḷpti anusāreṇa syāt  kālādi īśa vādinaḥ karma hetu tvam api tu niścaitanyāt na hi kvacid  aśeṣa duḥkha vilaye na idānīm kāraṇam yathā tathā uttaram ca na eva syāt  dṛṣṭi pūrva anumā yatas  śaktasya anyasya vijñānam tad prīti janakam yadi tayā eva bandha hāniḥ syāt iti kim nāma dūṣaṇam sva jñānāt  bandha hāniḥ tu dṛśyate kasya kutracid  ahiṃsāyāḥ ca dharma tvam kena mānena gamyate hiṃsāyāḥ  eva dharma tvam iti ukte syāt  kim uttaram dharmasya sukha hetu tvam api kena avagamyate hatyayā mokṣa hetu tvam kutaḥ mānāt nivāryate na ca śūnya parijñānāt śūnya bhāvanayā api ca mokṣaḥ kathañcana bhavet  yadi idānīm katham na saḥ para prasādana icchoḥ tu viḷambaḥ  nāma yujyate pum it chā adhīna tā naḥ ced  viḷambaḥ kiṅkṛtaḥ  bhavet  anyatra api viḷambāḥ tu syuḥ īśa icchā nimittatas anyathā kāraṇam ced  syāt  kim kāryam na upajāyate kāraṇe sati kāryasya bhāvaḥ su niyataḥ  asya hi vijñāna vādinaḥ ca eva vijñāna advaita vedanāt  vijñāna bhāvanāt ca eva mokṣaḥ  na ghaṭate kvacid  antar jñānasya bāhye ca kṣaṇika tvasya vedanāt  bhāvanāt ca ukta mārgeṇa māna abhāvāt na mucyate prakṛteḥ puruṣasya api vivekaḥ  mukti sādhanam iti śaṅkayā na ca etasmin mānam īśa aprasādataḥ śrutayaḥ smṛtayaḥ ca eva yadi īśasya prasādataḥ vadanti niyamāt muktim tam ṛte atas  kutaḥ bhavet  kaṇāda yoga akṣapādā api īśasya prasādataḥ muktim bruvāṇā api āhuḥ bhogāt eva ca karmaṇām kṣayam prāhuḥ kutas ca etad  prasanne jagat īśvare bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi dṛṣṭa eva ātmani īśvare iti śruti purāṇa ādi vacanebhyaḥ  anyathāgateḥ na ca pāśupatādyukta śiva ādīnām anugrahāt  na anyaḥ panthā iti hi uktam puruṣa jñānataḥ śrutau sarve nimeṣā jajñire vidyutaḥ puruṣādataḥ evam puruṣa śabdaḥ ca prayuktaḥ  abdhiśaye harau na tasya īśe kaścana tasya nāma mahat  yaśaḥ iti ca adhipatiḥ tasya pratiṣiddhaḥ svayam śrutau viśvatas  paramām nityam viśvam nārāyaṇam harim iti sarva adhikatva uktayā samaḥ  api vinivāritaḥ samādhikasya rāhityāt na upacāra pumānasau puruṣa eva idam sarvam yad  bhūtam yad ca bhavyam uta amṛta tvasya īśānaḥ  yad annena atirohati muktā mukta para īśa tvam iti tasya āha sā śrutiḥ amṛta īśāna vacanāt  sarvasya īśāna toditā yadi sarva tvam uditam uta īśa iti tad  vṛthā uta śabdaḥ  vadet eṣa hi īśa tvasya samuccayam puruṣeṇa idam vyāptam iti brāhmaṇam ca āha tam prati etāvān asya mahimā iti mahimnaḥ  vacaḥ  hi tad  saḥ  amṛtasya abhayasya īśaḥ  martyam annam yad atyagāt  iti amukta ādhipatyam tu pūrva ardha uktam anūdya ca uta amṛtasya īśa iti vidhatte mukti geśa tām atas  viṣṇu parijñānāt eva muktiḥ naca anyatas  tad  yathā iti śruteḥ ca eva tatas  karma kṣayaḥ  bhavet  yathā edhāṃsi samidhaḥ  agniḥ bhasmasāt  kurute arjuna jñāna agniḥ sarva karmāṇi bhasmasāt  kurute tathā sarva dharmān parityajya mām ekam śaraṇam vraja aham tvā sarva pāpebhyaḥ  mokṣayiṣyāmi mā śucaḥ ityādi bhagavat vākyaiḥ ukta arthaḥ ca avasīyate nitya naimittikam karma kurvan  anyat  parityajan mucyate saṃsṛteḥ ca etad api etena nirākṛtam vidyā eva iti imam eva artham svayam eva āha veda rāj  vinā karma na mokṣaḥ syāt jñānena iti api sā śrutiḥ na anyaḥ panthā iti hi eva nivārayati sādaram anyathā upāsanam api tam evam iti vādinī nivārayati ādareṇa na pratīka iti prabhuḥ andham tamaḥ praviśanti ye avidyām upāsate iti śruti virodhāt ca na anyathā upāsanam bhavet  na ca api ekatva vijñānāt ukta nyāyena mucyate iti sarvam pravijñāya sarvaiḥ tarka sat āgamaiḥ upāsīta harim nityam guṇaiḥ eva sva yogataḥ brahmā sarvai guṇaiḥ ca eva kriyā sāmānyatas ca gīḥ guṇa sāmānyatas  rudraḥ  dravya sāmānyatas  pare adhikāra viśeṣeṇa bhakti jñāna sukha ādibhiḥ viśeṣaḥ  devatā ādīnām mokṣe ca eva viśeṣataḥ na tāvatā virodhaḥ  asti nirdoṣa tvāt  samastaśas  ābhāsa tvāt  pareṣām tad avarāṇām ca sarvaśas  yatas  avarāṇām sarve api guṇāḥ sarvāḥ kriyā api niyamena eva pūrveṣām su prasāda nibandhanāḥ atas  sat śiṣyavat  teṣām na eva īrṣyādiḥ kathañcana na ca saṃsāri devānām kāleyat ta apare ime sūtre hi ārabdha mātrasya bhogena eva kṣayaḥ  dhruvaḥ anārabdha kārye bhogena tu itare iti coditaḥ paunaruktayena tena ete ukta arthe iti niścayaḥ uṣāḥ svāhā ca parjanyaḥ  mitraḥ  agniḥ varuṇaḥ  vidhuḥ pravahaḥ  aniruddha indrome rudraḥ  vāṇī ca mārutaḥ uttarottarataḥ tu ete guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ ca mukti gāḥ sūrya dharmau yathā somaḥ  manuḥ dakṣaḥ  bṛhaspatiḥ śacī ratiḥ ca aniruddha samāḥ tārā ca mitravat  somavat śatarūpā tu prasūtiḥ vahnivat  virāj  parjanyavat  vāruṇī ca tathā sañjñā ca rohiṇī dharmī ca mitravat tvena prāvahī parikīrtitā mitrapajarnya madhya sthau  aśvinau vighna vid tapau bhṛguḥ agni samaḥ  mitra tad madhye brahma putrakāḥ varuṇa agni antarā tatra nāradaḥ prāya indravat  kāmaḥ suparṇī comāvat  vi indraḥ  rudravat īritaḥ niṛtiḥ mitra sadṛśaḥ  viśvāmitraḥ kasūnuvat  vaivasvataḥ  manuḥ ca aśvi paścāt anye tatas  avarāḥ cyavanocathya vainyāḥ ca śaśabinduḥ ca haihayaḥ tadvat ca vipra rājanya viśeṣaḥ  atra api kaścana tadvat  priyavrataḥ ca api tad anyāḥ śata devatāḥ pajarnī amitra antarāḷe tad anye tu tatas  avarāḥ etebhyaḥ  abhyadhikā śrīḥ astu sadā muktā viśeṣataḥ tad samaḥ  na asti paramaḥ  hariḥ eva naca aparaḥ saṃhitāyām bṛhatyām tu svayam bhagavatā uditam tad etad akhilam prāṇa āhaṅkārika eva ca indrāt anantaraḥ  dṛṣṭiḥ api yogya anusārataḥ samyak  guru prasādaḥ ca mukhyataḥ dṛṣṭi kāraṇam śravaṇa ādi ca kartavyam na anyathā darśanam kvacid  guṇa adhikam gurum prāpya tad hīnam na āpnuyāt kvacid  viparyayaḥ tu kartavyaḥ sarvathā muktim icchatā same vikalpa eva syāt  pūrva anujñā ca sarvathā tad uttama guru prāptyai pūrva anujñā na mṛgyate guru barrahma akhilānām ca vidyā ca eva sarasvatī devatā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarveṣām aviśeṣatas  tad prasādena muktiḥ syāt na anyathā tu kathañcana sva uttamāḥ tu krameṇa eva sarveṣām guravaḥ śrutāḥ upadeśaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ tu sarveṣām eva muktaye sādhanebhyaḥ  adhikā bhaktiḥ na eva anyat  tādṛśam kvacid  bhaktiḥ ca eva harau  eva mukhyān yatra yathākramam svādhikā tu eva sarvatra sva uttameṣu krameṇa ca anuvartate ca sā bhaktiḥ muktau  ānanda rūpiṇī tad pūrva ka upāsana evam kartavyā muktaye guṇaiḥ evam utpanna nirdoṣa bhagavat darśanāt  sadā apekṣita phala prāptiḥ ārabdhasya anatikramāt deva ṛṣi mānuṣa ādīnām tad tad jāti anusārataḥ jaimini uktam mānuṣāṇām tad viśeṣāḥ ca kecana sāmānyam bhagavat proktam deva ādīnām viśeṣataḥ balavat virodhi sadbhāve jaiminyāt yuktiḥ iṣyate vikarma lepaḥ  na eva asti samyak dṛṣṭimatām kvacid  guṇa hāniḥ ca na eva asti brahmaṇaḥ tu avikarmataḥ devānām api na prāyas  kḷptasya tu kathañcana prāpta hrāsaḥ  bhavet  kvāpi mahatā tu vikarmaṇā tathā api tad  kḷptam eva tasmāt na niyama ujkhitiḥ candra sugrīvayoḥ ca eva sva ucca dāra parigrahāt prāpta hāniḥ abhūt na eva kḷpta hāniḥ yathañcana hrāsaḥ  api mānuṣa ādīnām ānandasya vikarmaṇā bhavet muktau viśeṣeṇa sva uccānām aparādhataḥ jñāna uttarasya pāpasya caturthe alepa ucyate aśucitva ādikam tasya na bhavet iti tad phalam atra jñāna phalasya eva mukteḥ niyata tā ucyate prārabdha karma jasya eva viṣa bhakṣāt mṛteḥ iva prāptasya api anivarti asya kiñcid  bhuktasya saṃvidā upamarda iha proktaḥ  deva ādīnām yathākramam sarva ātmanā tu abhogaḥ  hi prārabdhasya eva karmaṇaḥ na brahma darśinaḥ  api syāt  phala hrāsaḥ tu vidyate sarva ātmanā phala hrāsaḥ  yadi na ārabdha karmaṇaḥ syāt  kāmya vidhi vaiyarthyam iti ukta niyamaḥ  bhavet  evam adya api samproktam tantra bhāgavate sphuṭam tāratamyam phale naḥ ced  brahma ādīnām katham śrutiḥ avṛjinaḥ  akāma hata iti muktim nigadya ca ānanda tāratamyam ca teṣām brūyāt  pṛthak  pṛthak  saṃsāra eva ced etad  tāratamyam na mukhyatas  akāma hata śabda arthaḥ  avṛjina tvam ca naḥ bhavet  kāmasya yatra āptāḥ kāmāḥ tatra mām amṛtam kṛdhi iti yad lakṣaṇam mukteḥ śrutiḥ āha balīyasī kāma āhatiḥ kutaḥ anyatra prāpta kāmasya sā bhavet  aprayatnena kāmānām avāptiḥ sā yadā bhavet  tadā eva akāma hatatā kuta eva anyathā bhavet  cetanasya tu asuptasya kutra dṛṣṭā hi akāma tā avyaktiḥ eva kāmānām na na āśaḥ moha suptayoḥ yad kāmaḥ svāpam āpnoti tad eva utthāpitaḥ kutas  avaśaḥ api vyāharati kutas  supta avakāma tā sarva kāmān avāpnoti brahmaṇā saha mukti gaḥ paryeti tatra jakṣan  ca krīḍan ratim avāpnuvan kāmānnī kāmarūpī san  imān lokān  ca sañcaran āste gāyan sāma mukta ityādi śruti sat balāt akāmaḥ syāt  katham muktaḥ kāmā ye asya hṛdi śritāḥ iti antaḥkaraṇa sthānām kāmānām mokṣam eva hi āha śrutiḥ hṛdi iti eva na ced  vyartham viśeṣaṇam hṛdi eṣa teṣām śrayaṇam iti pakṣaḥ  na bhāsate muktānām kāmitām āha pṛthak śākhāsu yad śrutiḥ atas  akāma hata tvam tu muktānām eva mukhyatas  mukhya arthasya vṛthā tyāgaḥ  māyinām eva bhūṣaṇam apāpa tvam aduḥkha tvam ca āvṛjina tvam iha uditam apriyam vṛjinam duḥkham akam toda iti iya ṛte tad kāraṇa tvāt pāpam vā vṛjinam nāma kathyate iti uktaḥ svayam īśena nāma arthaḥ śabda nirṇaye apāpa tvam ca na eva asti yāvat saṃsāram asya hi ārabdha pāpam asti eva duḥkham ca jñāninaḥ  api hi tasmāt  tasmāt akāma tvam iti ca aśruta kalpanā akāma hata iti ukteḥ śruta hāniḥ api sphuṭā kutracid  kāminaḥ puṃsaḥ kāma abhāvāt kvacid  kvacid  indra ādi sukha bhogaḥ  asti iti anubhūtiḥ hi kupyati tasmāt amukta sukha gam tāratamyam pṛthak  pṛthak  uktvā yaḥ ca iti muktānām tāratamyam sukhe śrutiḥ āha iti peśalam tad ca caśabdāt eva gamyate rāddhaḥ saṃsiddha  iti eva mukta eva avagamyate sādhunā viṣṇunā yuktaḥ  muktaḥ sādhu yuvā mataḥ yauvanam nityam etasya muktasya iti yuvā sa ca phalam adhyayanasya āptam tena adhyāyaka īritaḥ nirhrāsa ānanda samprāptyā ca āśiṣṭa iti gīyate sthitasya ananyathā prāpteḥ dṛḍhiṣṭha iti coditaḥ baliṣṭhaḥ ca svabhāvena muktaḥ  bhavati kevalam tasya iyam pṛthivī ityādi pūrva bhāva vyapekṣayā sa eka iti saṃsāra gata muktavā sukham punar  śrotriyasya iti vadati muktāt śataguṇa ātma tām saṃsāra gāt ca saṃsāra gatasya eva śata adhikam muktān muktasya yuktam syāt śruti uktam abhivīkṣitaḥ yuktam ca sādhana ādhikyāt sādhya ādhikyam sura ādiṣu na ādhikyam yadi sādhye syāt  prayatnaḥ sādhane kutas  yatnaḥ ca dṛśyate teṣām mahān eva mahātmanām yatra sādhana bāhulyam sādhya bāhulyam atra ca dṛṣṭam niyamataḥ  naḥ ced na yatnam kurya rañjasā kṛcchreṇa sādhanāt eva na muktavat udīryate daśa kalpam tapaḥ cīrṇam rudreṇa lavaṇa arṇave tyaktavā sukhāni sarvāṇi kliṣṭena lavaṇa ambhasā śakreṇa varṣakoṭiḥ ca dhūmaḥ pītaḥ  ati duḥkhataḥ varṣa ayutam ca sūryeṇa tapaḥ  avākchirasā kṛtam su duḥkhena sukham tyaktavā dharmeṇa ākāśa śāyinā pītā mayīcayaḥ  varṣa sāhasram ati sādaram ati kṛcchreṇa kurvanti yatnam brahma vidaḥ  api hi iti etad akhilam mokṣa viśeṣa abhāvataḥ katham daivī sampad  vimokṣāya nibandhāya āsurī matā iti mokṣa viśeṣaḥ ca svayam bhagavatā uditaḥ tam eva yūyam bhajata ātma vṛttibhiḥ manaḥ vacaḥ kāya guṇaiḥ sva karmabhiḥ amāyinaḥ kāmadughā aṅghri paṅkajam yathā adhikāra avasita artha siddhaye akṣaṇvantaḥ karṇavantaḥ sakhāyaḥ  manojaveṣu asamā babhūvuḥ ādaghnāsa upakakṣāsa u tve hradā iva snātvā u tve dadṛśre ityādīni ca vākyāni tāratamyam vimukti gam vyaktam vadanti tad  kena sāmyam mukteṣu gamyate duḥkha ādi abhāva sāmyam ca sāmya vākya artha īyate bhaktayā ādi guṇa sadbhāve hi atulya tvam ca bhārate uktam sādhana vaiśeṣyam api sarvatra kathyate durjñeyam ghora rūpasya trailokya dhvaṃsinaḥ prabhoḥ daivataiḥ munibhiḥ siddhaiḥ mahā yogibhiḥ eva ca nitya yuktaiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ vimukta kleśa sādhvasaiḥ mahā utsāhaiḥ mahā dhairyaiḥ sattva sthaiḥ vyavasāyibhiḥ atīta anāgata jñāna prabhava apyaya vedibhiḥ śauca svādhyāya santoṣa tapassatya dayā anvitaiḥ kim u martyaiḥ bhaya bhrānti dhvaṃsa moha rujā anvitaiḥ alpa āyuḥ vīrya dhī sattva vyavasāya śruti vrataiḥ kaḥ tam madāmadam devam mad anyaḥ  jñātum arhati brahmā eva kiñcid jānāti na tad anyaḥ  hi kaścana muktānām api siddhānām nārāyaṇa parāyaṇaḥ su durlabhaḥ praśānta ātmā koṭiṣu api mahāmate iyam visṛṣṭiḥ yata ā babhūva yadi vā dadhe yadi vā na yaḥ  asya adhyakṣaḥ parame vyoman tsaḥ aṅga veda yadi vā na veda yaḥ sva ātma māyā vibhavam svayam gataḥ  na aham nabhasvān  tam atha apare kutas  brahmā api yam vetti na eva iha samyak anye kutaḥ deva muni indra martyāḥ namaḥ te amita tattvāya dharma ādīnām ca sūtaye nirguṇāya ca sat kāṣṭhām na aham veda apare kutas  na aham para āyuḥ  ṛṣayaḥ  na marīci mukhyā jānanti yad viracitam khalu sattva saṅgāḥ yad māyayā muṣita cetasa īśa daitya martya ādayaḥ kim uta śaśvat abhadra vṛttāḥ aham mahā indraḥ  nirṛtiḥ pracetāḥ somaḥ  agniḥ īśaḥ pavanaḥ  arkaḥ  viriñcaḥ āditya viśve vasavaḥ  atha sādhyā marut gaṇā rudra gaṇāḥ sa siddhāḥ anye ca ye viśvasṛjaḥ  amara īśā bhṛgu ādayaḥ  aspṛṣṭa rajaḥ tamaskāḥ yasya īhitam na viduḥ spṛṣṭṛ māyāḥ sattva pradhānā api kim tatas  anye sa varsya ādau smṛtaḥ  brahmā tasmāt  devāt anantaraḥ jānāti deva pravaram bhūyas ca atas  adhikam nṛpa na tvām atiśayiṣyanti muktau  api kathañcana mad bhakti yogāt jñānāt ca sarvān atiśayiṣyasi yathā bhakti viśeṣaḥ  atra dṛśyate puruṣottame tathā mukti viśeṣaḥ  api jñāninām liṅga bhedane sāyujyam samanuprāptā api deva ādayaḥ  akhilāḥ tāratamyāt hi tiṣṭhanti tāratamyam hi sādhane manuṣyāṇām sahasreṣu kaścid  yatati siddhaye yatatām api siddhānām kaścid mām vetti tattvataḥ ya imam paramam guhyam mad bhakteṣu abhidhāsyati bhaktim mayi parām kṛtvā mām eva eṣyati asaṃśayaḥ na ca tasmāt manuṣyeṣu kaścid me priya kṛttamaḥ bhavitā na ca me tasmāt anyaḥ priya taraḥ  bhuvi adhyeṣyate ca ya imam dharmyam saṃvādam āvayoḥ jñāna yajñena tena aham iṣṭaḥ syām iti me matiḥ śraddhāvānana sūyuḥ ca śṛṇuyāt api yaḥ  naraḥ saḥ  api muktaḥ śubhān lokān prāpnuyāt  puṇya karmaṇām dhyānena ātmani paśyanti kecid ātmānam ātmanā anye sāṅkhayena yogena karma yogena ca apare anye tu evam ajānantaḥ śrutvā anyebhya upāsate te api ca atitaranti eva mṛtyum śruti parāyaṇāḥ su sūkṣmaiḥ api aśeṣaiḥ ca viśeṣaiḥ saha paśyati sva ātmānam bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sarva rūpaḥ  api sarvadā savartra ca anyat api evam tena adṛṣṭam na hi kvacid  sarvatra sarva daiva īśam paśyati eva ramā api tu na tu sarvaiḥ viśeṣaiḥ tam paśyanti api anyatas  adhikam sva ātmānam anyat ca aśeṣam paśyati eva hi sarvadā brahmā tu sarva gam paśyet  guṇān api atas adhikam na tu sarveṣu kāleṣu tathā paśyati amukti gaḥ muktaḥ tu sarvadā paśyet  sarvaga tvena ca api tu na ramāvat  viśeṣāṇām darśanam śaknuyāt  kvacid  sva ātmānam anyat ca sadā viśeṣaiḥ akhilaiḥ api paśyanti añjaḥ tathā vāṇī viśoṣān  tāvataḥ  na tu traiguṇyāt  paratas  paśyet  vyāptam śataguṇam harim giriśaḥ  garuḍaḥ ca eva tamaḥ mātra gatam harim paśyet  viśeṣān api hi vāṇī dṛṣṭān na paśyati umā suparṇī ca mahat tattvam yāvat  prapaśyati rudra dṛṣṭān viśeṣān  ca na eva paśyet  kadācana svarūpam anya rūpam ca muktā devāḥ samastaśas  jānanti indraḥ ca kāmaḥ ca brahma yāvat ahaṅkṛtiḥ paśyantaḥ  manudakṣa ādyā buddhi tattva sthitam harim paśyanti soma sūryau tu mana stham parameśvaram anye bhūta sthitam viṣṇum devāḥ paśyanti sarvadā bahu sāhasra varṣeṇa mahat tattve kvacid  kvacid  anye ca eva yathāyogya maṇḍa antar vartinam harim śvetadvīpa patim ca eva hṛdi eva anye tu kecana kadācid eva tatra api kecid  paśyanti keśavam umā yāvat ananta aṃśān pūrva dṛṣṭebhya eva tu viśeṣān vāsudevasya paścāt uktā vicakṣate śakra kāma ādayaḥ ca eva viśeṣān brahmaṇi sthitān umā ādibhiḥ prabuddhebhyaḥ śata aṃśān eva cakṣate ityādi veda smṛti gavacanebhyaḥ  yathārthataḥ tāratamyam vimuktānām sādhanānām ca dṛśyate sādhya sādhana vairūpyam adṛṣṭam kena kalpyate vaiṣamyam nirghṛṇa tvam ca tena syātām parasya ca sa apekṣa tvāt iti ca tau vidyā adhīśena vāritau tāratamyāt  sādhanānām sādhya tāt ṛktavam īśataḥ avaiṣamyādi hetuḥ syāt  sadā eva parameśvare svātantrye vidyamāne api sādhana ādau pareśituḥ apekṣya anādi vaicitṛyam na doṣa iti tad vacaḥ nānā ādi tvāt iti hi uktam upapadyata iti api apekṣya upāya vaiṣamyam upeyasya tathā sthitiḥ mayā kayā viruddhā syāt  rājā ādau  api dṛśyate tyāgaḥ  dṛṣṭasya ca adṛṣṭa kalpanā iti su duṣkarau māyibhyaḥ  anyena kena api tad  kim anyaiḥ ca vādibhiḥ māyinaḥ  atra anugamyante śruta hānyaśruta grahau api atra māyinām liṅge tad  ke doṣāḥ tatas  adhikāḥ niśśeṣa gata doṣāṇām bahubhiḥ janmabhiḥ punar  syāda aparokṣyam hi hareḥ dveṣa īrṣyādiḥ tatas  kutas  bhaveyuḥ yadi ca īrṣi ā ādyāḥ sameṣu api kutaḥ na te tapyamānāḥ samān dṛṣṭvā dveṣa īrṣyā ādi yutā api dṛśyante bahavaḥ  loke doṣā eva atra kāraṇam yadi nirdoṣa tā tatra kim ādhikyena dūṣyate yadi anya darśana abhāvādīrṣi ādiḥ vinivāryate adarśanāt arati ādiḥ katham tena nivāryate brahmaṇaḥ  api aratiḥ dṛṣṭvā pūrvam ekākinaḥ śrutau na eva reme sa ca ekākī tasamān na ramate kvacid  dvitīyam aicchat  tena asau  iti śrutaya ūdire yadi icchā tatra na eva asti iti eva tad  kalpyate mṛṣā śruti ukta nirdoṣa tā eva kim na aṅgīkriyate svayam tāratamyam ca kāmam ca śrutam eva atihāya tu aśrutā sama tā kena kalpyate yukti māninā kim tad mānam sama tve te muktānām upalabhyate vṛthā ayam āgrahaḥ kena śruta hānyaśruta grahe mokṣe api tāratami itas cetana tvāt  purā yathā iti ukta uttaram kim te kalpanā mātra vādinaḥ na ca duḥkha ādikam kalpyam nirduḥkhatva śruteḥ balāt  śokam tarati ātma vettā tīrṇaḥ sarvān aduḥkha bhāj  yena ānandyeva bhavati na śocati kadācana kilbiṣa spṛt  pituṣaṇiḥ aram hita iha īśvaraḥ yam yam antam abhiprepsuḥ sa saṅkalpāt  bhavet iha ityādi śrutayaḥ  mānam nirduḥkhatva ādi sampadi atas  duḥkha ādi anumayā na avakāśaḥ  atra labhyate tāratamya anumā tena bhavet na ati prasaṅginī śruti yukti balāt evam tāratamyam vibhāvyate muktau  api tatas  ke atra virodham kartum īśate anādi yogyatām ca eva kali vāṇi īśvara avadhim kaḥ  nivārayitum śaktaḥ  yuktayā āgama bala uddhatām brahmaṇaḥ  anyatra ādhikya yuktaḥ kālaḥ  vivādavān kālaḥ  hi ayam yathā ityādi mā anumāmāninaḥ  bhavet  anya śabdaḥ  hari śrī svasamebhyaḥ  anya vivakṣayā prayuktaḥ  na eva doṣāya rudra ādiṣu ca yuktitaḥ uttama tvam tu muktānām api na brahmaṇaḥ  bhavet  vyaktiḥ sukhasya tu bhavet natu ādhikyam sukhasya ca bala jñāna adhika tvam ca tebhyaḥ  hi brahmaṇaḥ sadā ādhikyasya tu anitya tve na kiñcid mānam īyate śṛṇve vīra ugram ugram damāyan  anyam anyam atinenīyamānaḥ edhamāna dviḷu bhayasya rājā coṣkūyate viśa indraḥ  manuṣyān parā pūrveṣām sakhyā vṛṇakti vitarturāṇaḥ  aparebhiḥ eti anānubhūtīrava dhūn vānaḥ pūrvītindraḥ śaradastartarī iti divedive sadṛśīḥ anyam ardham kṛṣṇā asedhat apa sat manaḥ  jāḥ ahan dāsā vṛṣabhaḥ vasnayanta udavra je varcinam śambaram ca tam bhūtiḥ iti devāḥ  upāsāñcakrire te babhūvuḥ tasmāt ha api etarhi suptaḥ  bhūbhrūḥ iti eva praśvasiti abhūtiḥ iti asurāḥ te ha parābabhūvuḥ tad  yathā peśaskarī peśasaḥ  mātrām apādāya anyat   avataram kalyāṇataram rūpam tanu ta evam eva ayam ātmā idam śarīram nihatya avidyām gamayitavān yad navataram kalyāṇataram rūpam kurute pitṛyam pitṛyam vā gāndharvam vā daivam vā prājāpatyam vā brāhmam vā anyeṣām vā bhūtānām prayānti paramām siddhimaihikā amuṣmikīm drutam yā na prāpya asuraiḥ sarvaiḥ akṣayā kleśa varjitā na tām gatim prapadyante vinā bhāgavatān narān avajānanti mām mūḍhā mānuṣīm tanum āśritam param bhāvam ajānantaḥ  mama bhūta maheśvaram mogha āśā mogha karmāṇaḥ  mogha jñānā vicetasaḥ rākṣasīm āsurīm ca eva prakṛtim mohanīm śritāḥ mahātmānaḥ tu mām pārtha daivīm prakṛtim āśritāḥ bhajanti ananya manasaḥ  jñātvā bhūtādim avyayam abhayam sattva saṃśuddhiḥ jñāna yoga vyavasthitiḥ dānam damaḥ ca yajñaḥ ca svādhyāyaḥ tapa ārjavam ahiṃsā satyam akrodhaḥ tyāgaḥ śāntiḥ apaiśunam dayā bhūteṣu alolu tvam mārdavam hrīḥ acāpalam tejaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ śaucam adrohaḥ  na ati mānitā bhavanti sampadam daivīm abhijātasya bhārata ḍambhaḥ  darpaḥ  atimāḥ ca krodhaḥ pāruṣyam eva ca ajñānam ca abhijātasya pārtha sampadam āsurīm mām ātma para deheṣu pradviṣantaḥ  abhyasūyakāḥ tān aham dviṣataḥ krūrān saṃsāreṣu nara adhamān kṣipāmi ajasram aśubhān āsurīṣu eva yoniṣu āsurīm yonim āpannā mūḍhā janmani janmani mām aprāpya eva kaunteya tatas  yānti adhamām gatim dvividhaḥ  bhūta sargaḥ  atra daiva āsura eva ca viṣṇu bhakti paraḥ  daivaḥ  viparītaḥ tathā asuraḥ devānām paramaḥ  dharmaḥ sadā yajña ādikāḥ kriyāḥ svādhyāyaḥ tattva vedi tvam viṣṇu pūjā ratiḥ smṛtiḥ daityānām bāhuṣāḷi tvam mātsaryam yuddha satkriyā nīti śāstra praveditvam śiva pūjā ratiḥ smṛtiḥ varṇa āśrama ācāravat tvam svādhyāyaḥ  bhaktiḥ acyute śive sūrye tathā devyām svabhāvaḥ  mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ anādi vaiṣṇavā eva devatāḥ tu svabhāvataḥ viparītāḥ tatas  daityāḥ sadā eva anādi kālataḥ mānuṣā miśra matayaḥ  vimiśra gatayaḥ api ca ityādi vākya sandarbhe jñāyate anādi yogya tā yadi anādiḥ viśeṣaḥ  na sāmpratam katham eva saḥ adṛṣṭāt eva ca adṛṣṭam svīkṛtam sa varva ādibhiḥ ākasmikaḥ  viśeṣaḥ ced adṛṣṭe kvacid iṣyate sarvatra ākasmika tvam sya at na adṛṣṭa apekṣa tā bhavet  adṛṣṭāḥ ced  viśeṣaḥ  ayam anādi tvam kutaḥ na tad  nacānya bhedavat  viṣṇau bhedaḥ tad darśinām api dṛśyate pratyabhijñā eva bahu rūpeṣu dṛśyate bahu tvam ca viśeṣeṇa na bhedena kathañcana pratyabhijñā ca yeṣām na te api tad muṣya dṛṣṭayaḥ bhedam na eva prapaśyanti bhedam anyebhya eva ca paśyanti evam hariḥ teṣām sandarśayati na anyathā evam bṛhatsaṃhitāyām vacanam na purāṇa gam loka darśana vādi ā iva veda rodhāya śaknuyāt  aparīkṣita dṛṣṭiḥ ca parīkṣā pūrva darśanam niṣeddhum śaknuvādi eva veda rodhāya śaknuyāt  na ca niścita bhedasya darśane asti purāṇa gam vākyam kvacid hi sammugdha darśanam tatra gamyate aparīkṣitam eva atra vedha ādikam adhīśituḥ parīkṣā darśane na eva dṛśyate kenacid  kvacid  nirdoṣam eva tam brahmā dadarśa aśeṣa rūpiṇam nirdoṣam eva rudraḥ  adrāṅ nirdoṣam tam purandaraḥ nirdoṣāṇi asya rūpāṇi dṛṣṭāni evam sura uttamaiḥ anye sa doṣāḥ sarve api nirdoṣaḥ  harirekalaḥ iti barku śruteḥ ca eva sa doṣam na asya darśanam aviddhaḥ  viddhavat  viṣṇuḥ ajātaḥ  jātavat mṛṣā abaddhaḥ  baddhavat ca eva darśayati amita dyutiḥ iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ ca eva prāha nirdoṣa tām hareḥ aparīkṣita dṛṣṭayā eva sa doṣaḥ  dṛśyate hariḥ parīkṣā darśane na eva dṛśyaḥ  doṣaḥ  hareḥ kvacid  iti paiṅgiśrutiḥ ca āha pramāṇam hi parīkṣitam na parīkṣā anavasthā syāt  sākṣi siddhe tu asaṃśayāt mānase darśane doṣāḥ syuḥ navai sākṣi darśane su dṛḍhaḥ  nirṇayaḥ  yatra jñeyam tad  sākṣi darśanam icchā jñānam sukham duḥkha bhaya abhaya kṛpa ādayaḥ sākṣi siddhā na kaścid hi tatra saṃśayavān kvacid  yad  kvacid  vyabhicārī syāt  darśanam mānasam hi tad  manaḥ cakṣuḥ darśana ādeḥ api yatra eva sākṣiṇā prāmāṇyam su gṛhītam syāt  tad  parīkṣita darśanam na jñāna dṛṣṭi mātreṇa prāmāṇyam tasya dṛśyate niyamena sukha ādyeṣu prāmāṇyam sākṣi gocaram sva prāmāṇyam sadā sākṣī paśyati eva su niścayāt  jñānasya grāhakeṇa eva sākṣiṇā mānatā amiteḥ doṣa abhāve pramāṇa tvam doṣa abhāvasya sākṣiṇā niścita tvam kvacid ca eva svatas  prāmāṇyam iṣyate atas  na sarva mānānām prāmāṇyam niścitam bhavet  sākṣiṇā niścitam yatra tad  prāmāṇya sva lakṣaṇam na hi kaścid  sukha ādyeṣu saṃśayam kurute janaḥ na ca eva akhila mānāni niścinoti akhilaḥ  janaḥ tasmāt anubhava ārūḍham kimartham upalapyate doṣa abhāva ādikam ca eva sākṣī samyak  prapaśyati tad  parīkṣita mānena na doṣaḥ  viṣṇavi kvacid  aparīkṣita dṛṣṭiḥ tu kasmin  arthe na vidyate tad  pratyakṣa viruddha arthe na āgamasya api mānatā upajīvyam akṣa jam yatra tad anyatra viparyayaḥ laukike vyavahāre atra pratyakṣasya upajīvyatā avatāra ādi daṣṭau syāt āgamasya upajīvyatā āgamena hi viṣṇu tvam jñātvā doṣaḥ  atra kalpyate na ced  syāt  doṣavān anyaḥ śāstra siddham hi lakṣaṇam kasyacid  doṣavat tvam syāt iti mātre akṣa jam bhavet  na viṣṇoḥ deṣavat tve hi pratyakṣam vartate svatas  kecid  paśyanti doṣān iti atra api syāt na cākṣa jam paurāṇam vākyam eva atra tad śrutyā eva viruddhayate purāṇasya upajīvyaḥ ca veda eva naca aparaḥ tad virodhe katham mānam tad  tatra ca bhaviṣyati aparīkṣita dṛṣṭiḥ ca katham eva akṣa jam bhavet  yadi evam deva datta ādi bhramaḥ kim na akṣa jam bhavet  yāvat śakti parīkṣāyām upajīvyasya bādhane doṣaḥ  na aśodhite doṣa upajīvya tvam asvalam bhrame api abhrama bhāgaḥ  asti tanmātram upajīvya hi bādhaka jñāna vṛttiḥ syāt na ca evam su parīkṣite sarvam tad upajīvya eva pramāṇam vartate yatas  katham brahma iti tad jñeyam sarvajñatva ādi lakṣaṇam vihāya yasmāt kasmāt cid  svarūpasya eva ced  yadi upajīvya tvam etasmāt  vyāvṛttam yāvatā bhavet  tāvatā eva upajīvya tvam svarapasya eva na kvacid  sarva lakṣaṇa yuktam tu svarūpam yadi bhaṇyate astu naḥ na eva hāniḥ syāt  sva pakṣaḥ ca ayam añjasā yasmāt anvita eva arthaḥ śabdānām api sarvaśas  viśeṣa sāmanyatayā svarūpam akhilam bhavet  puras vartitva pūrvāṇi devadatta ādika bhrame vyāvartayanti tad rūpam caitra mātra d vinā eva hi brahmaṇaḥ  nirviśeṣa tvāt  vyāvartayati kim punar  yasmāt kasmāt cid api arthāt tāvat ced  siddha sādhanam cit mātra tvam ca naiveṣyam aviśeṣatva vādinaḥ tāvat mātram yadīṣyam syāt  sarvajña tvam kutaḥ na tad  cit mātra abheda sādhye api siddham tad  prativādinaḥ sva abheda aṅgīkṛteḥ eva cit tvam svasya api yad matam sarva apekṣa tayā sarvajña tvam iti eva tad na hi iti ced cetana tvam ca jña tvam na jñeya varjitam sva jñeya tvam ca na eva asau manyate sa viśeṣatas  sva śabdaḥ  api para apekṣaḥ tasmāt  vyāvṛttiḥ eva hi sva śabda artha iti proktaḥ svarūpam nāma kim na ced  rūpa śabdena pūrṇa tvāt  tad ca sāmānya tā vacaḥ na svarūpa abhidhāyi syāt  vaiyarthyam svaravasya yad  cetanasya svabhāvaḥ  hi caitanyam iti gīyate tasmāt  viśeṣa bāhulyam caitanyasya viśeṣataḥ na jñeya jñātṛ hīnam hi jñānam nāma kvacid  bhavet  jñeya jñāna vihīnaḥ ca jña iti atra ca na pramā jñātṛ jñeya vihīnam ca jñānam ced  bhoktṛ bhojyataḥ hīnam bhojanam eva syāt  tāḍanam kartṛ tāḍyataḥ nitya tvāt  tādṛśam ca syāt iti ced nitya vāc api vācya vaktṛ vihīnā syāt na hi sā ca eva tādṛśī draṣṭāraḥ  veda vācaḥ  hi santi vācyāni ca añjasā nityaḥ  draṣṭā ca vācyaḥ ca bhagavān eva ca svayam na hi vaktṛ vihīnā ca vācya hīnā api vāc  kvacid  jñātṛ jñeya vihīnam ca jñānam evam na tad  bhavet  na hi nityaḥ  api vaktā asti vākya vācya vivarjitaḥ jñāna jñeya vihīnaḥ ca jñaḥ  api evam na eva vidyate kiñca sarva vilopaḥ ca kena mānena gamyate sarveṇa saha tad  vākyām arthaḥ ca yadi gṛhyate tad abhāvena sarvasya na apalāpaḥ  bhavet  tadā na gṛhyate ced  tad nyāyāt apalāpaḥ  na hi kvacid  upapatti vihīnasya vākyasya arthaḥ  na gamyate upakrama ādi liṅgānām balīyaḥ  hi uttarottaram śruti ādau pūrva pūrvam ca brahma tarka vinirṇayāt  pratyakṣam upapattiḥ ca bahavaḥ ca āgamā yadā viruddhayante naca arthaḥ  asti yatra liṅga virodhitā sa eva arthaḥ katham grāhya upapanne avirodhinī mukhya arthe vidyamāne tu kva sāvarjñyam niṣiddhayate atas  sarva guṇaiḥ yuktam brahma aṅgīkāyarmā iva hi apalāpaḥ  api sarvasya na kathañcana yujyate anādi yogya tā ca uktā tena grāhyā eva sarvathā muktānām tāratamyam ca mānaiḥ uktaiḥ na cālyate jñāninaḥ  api yatas  nityam kurvanti śubham eva hi tāratamyam tu muktau ca tena eva adhyavasīyate tāratamyam na ced muktau kutas  kuryuḥ śubham punar  kṛcchreṇa api tapaḥ  jñānam karma api ete caranti hi bibhyati sma aśubhāt nityam sa kāmāḥ ca śubhe sadā na ca svabhāva eva ayam bhaya pūrva pravṛttitaḥ kṛcchreṇa ācaraṇāt ca eva śubhasya eva punar  punar  tādṛśaḥ  api svabhāvaḥ ced ajñasya api bhavet  tathā phalavat tve pramāṇam ced  tatra jñasya samam hi tad  niṣkāmam jñāna pūrvam ca nivṛttam iha ca ucyate nivṛttam sevamānaḥ tu brahma abhyeti sanātanam śubhena ānanda vṛddhi syāt ghrāsaḥ ca eva aśubhena hi jñāninaḥ  api yatas tena kartavyam śubham eva taiḥ upāste sa ya ātmānam kṣīyate na asya karma ha asmāt hayā iva ātmanaḥ  yad yad kāmayet  sṛjate ca tad  avidvān bahu karmā api hi antavat  phalam āpnuyāt  yad eva vidyayā kuryāt  tad eva hi ati vīryavat  ityādi vākya sāmarthyāt  tāratamyam vimukti gam na cātra upāsakasya eva phalam akṣayam ucyate na hi jñānam vinā kvāpi phalasya akṣayatā bhavet  jñāna dvāreṇa ced  tasya na asmad pakṣa pratīpa tā jñāna uttarasya evam api hi akṣaya tvam naca anyathā pūrva bhāvi śubhānām hi jñānena eva kṛtārtha tā prārabdhānām tu bhogena tad jñāna uttara karmaṇām muktau  anupraveśaḥ syāt anyathā tad kṛtiḥ nahi jñānāt  pūrvāṇi sarvāṇi śubhāni jñāna siddhaye akāmyāni niṣiddhāni jñāna rodhāya bhuktaye yogyatāyā balāt  yad ca śubha bāhulyam āditas  jñāna bāhulyam eva etad  kuryāt na anyasya kāraṇam jñānasya bhakti bhāga tvāt  bhaktiḥ jñānam iti īryate jñānasya eva viśeṣaḥ  yad  bhaktiḥ iti abhidhīyate parokṣatva aparokṣa tve viśeṣau jñāna gau yathā sneha yogaḥ  api tadvat  syāt  viśeṣaḥ  jñāna gocaraḥ iti ābhiprāyataḥ prāyaḥ jñānam eva vimuktaye vadanti śrutayaḥ saḥ  ayam viśeṣaḥ  api hi udīryate bhaktiḥ jñānam iti kvāpi na hi dveṣa yutā dṛśiḥ puruṣa arthāya bhavati sarva śruti virodhataḥ cetanasya dvayam bhogyam saṃsāraḥ  muktiḥ eva ca saṃsāraḥ trividhaḥ tatra svargaḥ  madhyam adhas tathā muktiḥ ca dvividhā tatra sukham nityam tathā aparam nitya duḥkham iti jñeyam sādhanam saṃsṛtau  api kāmyam karma niṣiddham ca sa ajñānam iti niścayaḥ dveṣaḥ  bhaktiḥ ca muktau tu mukti dvaya vidhāyakam iti paiṅgi śruteḥ dveṣaḥ  na eva sat mukti kāraṇam asat mukteḥ kāraṇam ca muktau  iti atra
