keśavaḥ mukti śabda uditaḥ  mokṣam sva bhaktānām karoti yad  dveṣataḥ  api vimuktiḥ ced mahātātparya rodhanam bhaktayā prasannataḥ  devān muktiḥ iti eva tad guṇān vadanti śrutayaḥ sarvāḥ purāṇāni āgamā api yadi dveṣeṇa muktiḥ syāt  vaktavyaḥ  doṣa sañcayaḥ smartavyaḥ  bhagavān nityam iti arthena eva hi kvacid  dveṣāt iva guṇān āha purāṇe kruddha vākyavat  yathā kruddhaḥ pitā putram mara iti ākṣepa pūrvakam proktasya anyasya kṛti artham vadati evam purāṇa gam vākyam śruti virodhena sva virodhena ca añjasā bahu āgama virodhāt ca na dveṣāt mukti vācakam tamaḥ  dveṣeṇa saṃyānti bhaktayā muktim tathā eva ca viṣṇau viṣṇu prasādena viloma tvena ca añjasā iti ṣāḍguṇya vacanam api ukta artha niyāmakam mahātātparya rodhe ca katham vākyam pramāṇa tām yāti sarva artha rūpam hi mahātāt paryam iṣyate vācaka tvam hi tātparyam yad arthā akhilā ravāḥ saḥ  arthaḥ katham parityājya eka śabdasya saṃśaye atas  vijñāna bhaktibhyām puruṣa arthaḥ paraḥ  bhavet  yasya deve parā bhaktiḥ yathā deve tathā gurau tasya ete kathitā hi arthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ bhaktyā jñānam tatas  bhaktiḥ tatas  dṛṣṭiḥ tatas ca sā tatas  muktiḥ tatas  bhaktiḥ sā eva syāt  sukha rūpiṇī bhaktayā prasannaḥ  bhagavān dadyāt jñānam anākulam tayā eva darśanam yātaḥ pradadyāt muktim etayā na aham vedaiḥ na tapasā na dānena naca ijyayā śakya evaṃvidhaḥ  draṣṭum pradadyāt muktim etayā bhaktayā tu ananyayā śakya aham evaṃvidhaḥ  arjuna jñātum draṣṭum ca tattvena praveṣyum ca parantapa ityādi vākyataḥ ca eva saḥ  ayam ukta artha īyate na ca prasādam āpnoti dveṣāt  bhaktyā tam āpnuyāt  iti dṛṣṭa anusāri tvam api asmin  artha īyate ye pṛthak  vihitā viṣṇoḥ guṇā vedena sādaram ta eva dṛṣṭa vailomyāt aṅgīkāryā naca aparam anyat  dṛṣṭa anusāreṇa vāsudeve api gṛhyate doṣa abhāvāḥ ca ye vedaiḥ uditā avihāya tān anuktā apica grāhyā mahātātparya śaktitaḥ evam bṛhat saṃhitā vāc  siddhāntaḥ  hi tad īritaḥ tāratamyena tad bhakteṣu api bhaktiḥ viniścayāt  kartavyā eṣā api tad bhaktiḥ loka veda anusārataḥ yaḥ  hi bhaktaḥ pradhāne syāt  tadīyeṣu api bhaktimān dṛśyate asau niyamataḥ  viparītaḥ  viparyaye vyabhicāraḥ  yadi kvāpi bhakti hrāsaḥ  atra kalpyate bhakti doṣaḥ  hi asau yad na tad bhakteṣu api bhaktimān tāratamyena teṣu addhā bhaktiḥ dṛṣṭa anusārataḥ viṣṇu prasāda anusārāt  kāryā doṣaḥ tad anyathā sva prīti anusṛtau prītiḥ loke api addhā eva dṛśyate tāratamya parijñānam api etena eva sādhanam lakṣmī viriñca vāṇi īśa girija indra aṅgirassutāḥ sūrya ādayaḥ ca kramaśas  bhagavat prīti gocarāḥ teṣu bhaktiḥ krameṇa eva kāryā nityam mumukṣubhiḥ sarve api guravaḥ ca ete puruṣasya sadā eva hi tasmāt  pūjyāḥ ca namyāḥ ca dhyeyāḥ ca paritas  harim iti ṣāḍguṇya vacanāt api eṣaḥ  arthaḥ  avasīyate hari bhaktiḥ krameṇa eva tadīyeṣu harismṛtiḥ hari stutiḥ tad smṛtiḥ ca tad stutiḥ hari pūjanam tad pūjā vihita tyāga iti mukteḥ krameṇa hi niyamāt  sādhanāni eva nitya sādhyāni ca akhilaiḥ iti pravṛtta vacanam sādhanasya vinirṇaye pravṛtte pañca rātre hi sādhanasya ati niścayaḥ haridveṣaḥ  na śubha da  sat dveṣa tvāt  yathā guroḥ kramāt  bhaktiḥ hari prīti kāraṇam tad priya aupagā bhaktiḥ yatas  yathā svasmin  itya ādyā yuktiḥ atra ca prādhānya tāratamya anusāriṇī bhaktiḥ uttamā prīti daiva hareḥ yasmāt  bhaktiḥ sā sva upagā yathā iti vā jñāna karma ādi phalam ca eṣu krama upagam svātantrya tāratamyena phalam hi phalinām bhavet  aśubham tu aśubhe api eṣām svātantryāt  prītitaḥ  hareḥ ājñayā ca anya gam na eva bhogāya bhavati kvacid  puṇyam eva amum āpānoti na devān pāpam āpnuyāt  ityādi śrutayaḥ  māna mukte arthe yuktayaḥ aparāḥ upāsana adharma phalam yatas  deha antare sthitiḥ vāsudeva ājñayā ca eva pūrva karma anusārataḥ prerayanti hi te jīvān puṇya pāpeṣu nityaśas  arāga dveṣataḥ ca eva katham doṣān avāpnuyuḥ haryājñā karaṇāt eva puṇyam ebhiḥ avāpyate hari pūjā iti ca uddeśāt  katham na śubham āpnuyuḥ atas  yathākramam dharma jñānayoḥ phalam añjasā sarva prāṇi gatam devāḥ prāpnuvantyā viriñcataḥ devāḥ  eva hi devānām viśiṣṭā viniyāmakāḥ brahmā tu akhila devānām narāṇām ca niyāmakaḥ atas  sarva guṇān eṣa prāpanoti adhikam anyatas  dravya svātantrya vijñāna prayatnaiḥ adhikam phalam devānām anya gam ca api teṣu yad  brahmaṇaḥ  hi tad  bṛhat tantra uditam vākyam hariṇā phala nirṇaye loke api etādṛśa guṇaiḥ phala ādhikyam hi dṛśyate evañca kali pūrvāṇām asurāṇām mahat  phalam aśubheṣu sadā eva syāt mithyājñāna ādikeṣu hi śubha aśubha phalam devāḥ  asurāḥ ca samāpnuyuḥ krameṇa eva yathāśakti yathā ye ye prayojakāḥ prerakā api pāpānām na devāḥ pāpam āpnuyuḥ iti prakāśikāyām hi provāca hariḥ añjasā yadi api evam surāṇām ca daityānām ca mahat  phalam śubha aśubhebhya evañca kartuḥ ca syāt  yathā uditam tasmāt niraya mānuṣya svarga mukti upabhoginaḥ mānuṣa uttamam ārabhya devāḥ tu nirayam vinā asurāḥ tu vinā muktim tamaḥ  andham api ca āpnuyuḥ iti tattva viveka uktam svayam bhagavatā vacaḥ jñāna dā apica ācāryā viśeṣāt  phalam āpnuyuḥ muktau  aṣṭaguṇam śiṣyād guruḥ āpanoti śobhanam tad guruḥ dviguṇam tasmāt  sārdham tāvat  tatas  apare devāḥ sahasra guṇitam kramāt  tasmāt  yathottaram brahmā mahā ogha guṇitam evam phala vinirṇayaḥ iti āha bhagavān śāstre guru vṛtta abhidhe svayam yuktam ca tad na godātā gaḥ mātra phalam āpnuyāt ya imam paramam guhyam mad bhakteṣu abhidhāsyati bhaktim mayi parām kṛtvā mām eva eṣyati asaṃśayaḥ na ca tasmāt manuṣyeṣu kaścid me priya kṛttamaḥ bhavitā na ca me tasmāt anyaḥ priya taraḥ  bhuvi iti āha bhagavān evam api pātram apekṣyate evam eva avirodhena prārabdhasya eva karmaṇaḥ jñānam dṛṣṭa phalam proktam muktiḥ ca iha eva labhyate samanvaya avirodhābhyām siddhe vastuni sādhane vicāriteṣu aśeṣeṣu sādhaneṣu viśeṣataḥ nityaśas  kāryam atyantam avaśyam bhāvi sādhanam cintyate prathamam tatra śravaṇa ādi sakṛt kriyā āvṛttiḥ vā iti sandehe kartavyā avṛttiḥ eva hi upadeśaḥ  atat  tvam asi iti ādiḥ hi asakṛt eva yad  liṅgāt lātavyataḥ pūrva mṛjobarrahma tvataḥ śatāt  śuśrāva ugra tapā nāma yogyaḥ  rudra padasya yaḥ sārddham parārddham viṣṇoḥ tu guṇān bhaktayā sadā udyataḥ tad tri bhāgam upāsām ca cakre sambhṛta mānasaḥ daśaman vantaram śakra pada yogyaḥ  garutmataḥ pada yogyāt  sumanasaḥ sunandaḥ  nāma ca aśṛṇot  upāsām cakra udyuktaḥ  manvantara catuṣī ayam sūryācandramasoḥ ca eva pada yogyau su tejasau surūpaḥ śānta rūpaḥ ca manvantara catuṣī ayam aśṛṇvatām sumanasaḥ  manvantaram upāsatām tatas  proktāḥ tu te sarve bhaktayaḥ gratapaa ādayaḥ apaśyan paramam viṣṇum tad prasādedhitāḥ sadā iti uktam viṣṇunā sākṣāt  granthe sattatva sañjñite ātmā iti nāma kathitam sākṣāt nārāyaṇasya hi ātmā brahma mahān  tāraḥ parameśaḥ śuciśravāḥ viṣṇuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ  ananta iti śrīpatiḥ īryate iti piṅga śrutiḥ ca eva tathā eva parama śrutiḥ oma ātmā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ ātma ānandaḥ  akṣaraḥ svarāj  viśva trātā nṛsiṃhaḥ  ajaḥ  nārāyaṇa urukramaḥ anasūyā tathā eva atreḥ jajñe putrān akalmaṣān dattam durvāsasam somam ātma īśa brahma sambhavān iti bhāgavate ca eva tasmāt ātmā janārdanaḥ tasmāt upāsyaḥ  viṣṇuḥ iti jñātavyaḥ sat janaiḥ sadā tathā eva upāsate santaḥ tathā eva upadiśanti ca ādāna artha tvataḥ ca ayam ātma śabdaḥ patim vadet  svāmī me viṣṇuḥ iti eva nityadā upāsyam añjasā svāmī viṣṇuḥ iti dhyānam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyataḥ kartavyam sarvathā eva etad na kathañcana vismaret  iti sat tattva vacanam ṣāḍguṇya vacanam param mama svāmī hariḥ nityam sarvasya patiḥ eva ca iti dhyeyaḥ sarvadā eva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ pratīka viṣaya tvena na kāryā viṣṇu bhāvanā pratīkam na eva viṣṇuḥ yad mithyā upāsā hi anathardā yaḥ  anyathā santam ātma īśam anyathā pratipadyate kim tena na kṛtam pāpam coreṇa ātma apahāriṇā yaḥ  anyathā santam ātmānam anyathā pratipadyate kim tena na kṛtam pāpam coreṇa īśa apa hāriṇā yaḥ  anyathā eva sthitam viṣṇum anyathā pratipadyate kim tena na kṛtam pāpam coreṇa brahmacāriṇā sva ātmānam pratimām vā api devatā antaram eva vā cetana acetanam vānyat  dhyāyet  yaḥ keśavaḥ tu iti kim tena na kṛtam pāpam cāreṇa īśa apa hāriṇā yaḥ  anyat  viṣṇuḥ iti dhyāyet jānīyāt  vā harim tathā andhe tamasi majjet  sa yatra na eva utthitiḥ kvacid  yaḥ  anyat  viṣṇuḥ iti dhyāyet  viṣṇuḥ anyat iti sma vā anyathā dhyāna doṣeṇa mahātamasi majjati yaḥ  anyat  viṣṇuḥ iti dhyāyet  viṣṇuḥ anyat iti sma vā mahātamasi magnasya tasya na eva utthitiḥ kvacid  yad kiñcid anyathā saṃstham anyathā dhyātam añjasā dhyātuḥ mahā doṣa karam kim u sarva īśvaraḥ  hariḥ yad kiñcid anyathā saṃstham anyathā jñātam añjasā mahā doṣa karam viṣṇuḥ kim u sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ yad kiñcid anyathā saṃstham anyathā jñātam añjasā anartha kāraṇam loke kim u sarva īśvara īśvaraḥ na kiñcid anyathā jñeyam dhyeyam vā tena kutracid  kim u sarva uttamaḥ  viṣṇuḥ jñeyaḥ  nīca tayā kvacid  tasmāt  vastu yathārūpam jñeyam dhyeyam ca sarvadā kāraṇam puruṣa arthasya na anyathā bhavati kvacid  iti śruti purāṇa ukti balataḥ  na pratīkatā dhyeyā viṣṇoḥ kvacid  yasmāt mithyājñānam anartha dam iti abhipretya na hi sa iti āha bhagavān prabhuḥ pratīka saṃsthita tvena dhyeyaḥ  viṣṇuḥ naca anyathā brahma iti ca sadā dhyeyaḥ  bhagavān viṣṇuḥ añjasā utkṛṣṭaḥ  brahma śabda arthaḥ pūrṇa tvam brahma tā yatas  ādhi vyādhi nimittena vikṣipta manasaḥ  api tu dhyeyā eva brahma tā nityam viṣṇoḥ bhaktayā nirantaram iti prakāśikāyām ca vacanam viṣṇunā īritam na ātmā iti sūtram īśasya jīva tvapratipādakam ātma śabdam yatas  hetum kṛtvā jīvam nyavārayat  sva śabdāt  prāṇabhṛt ca eva na ukta iti eva veda rāj  yadi ātma śabdaḥ  jīve api katham sa vinivārayet  ātma śabda uditaḥ tasmāt  viṣṇuḥ eva naca aparaḥ ātma brahma ādayaḥ śabda astam ṛte viṣṇum avyayam na vadanti yatas  na āptā kvāpi taiḥ guṇa pūrṇa tā nārāyaṇa adhyātma gatam iti yad  vaiṣṇavam vacaḥ yadi jīveśayoḥ veda patiḥ aikyam ca manyate ātma śabdam katham tasmāt nivārayati yuktitaḥ bhedasya vyapadeśam ca sthitim cādanam eva ca bheda dārḍhye hetum āha satātparyam jagatpatiḥ vyāvahārika bhedaḥ ced  kva asau  avyāvahārikaḥ vyāvahārikam iti eva vacanam vyāvahārikam uta na iti vikalpe tu yadi syāt  vyāvahārikam tasya api bādhya tā ced  syāt  bhedaḥ syāt  pāramārthikaḥ avyāvahārika tvam ced  bhedaḥ  ayam satyatām gataḥ ekasya asatya tāyām hi dvayoḥ eva viruddhayoḥ anyasya satyatā eva syāt iti kena nivāryate asatyam na uktam iti ukte satyam uktam iti prajāḥ jānanti uktam tu naḥ satyam iti ukte asatya tām api na svapne api dvayam mithyā tatra ekam satyam eva hi bhāva abhāvau  ubhau tatra katham mithyā bhaviṣyataḥ bhāvasya hi niṣedhe tu na abhāvasya niṣedhanam sva vācaḥ  asatya tā ced  syāt  tasmāt  bhedasya satyatā tasmāt jīveśayoḥ bheda ukta nyāyena gamyate etasmāt ātma śabdaḥ  ayam paramātmā abhidhā bhavet  pratīka viṣaya tvena viṣṇu dṛṣṭiḥ na tad  bhavet  pratīke viṣṇuḥ iti eva tasmāt  kāryā hi upāsanā na ca viṣṇuḥ pratīkam yad  tasmāt na ātmā iti upāsanā iti pakṣaḥ  yadā brahma dṛṣṭiḥ ca atra viruddhayate sa na iti yuktiḥ tatra api sameti ukta viruddha tā yadi api utkarṣa mātreṇa hi atad bhave api upāsanā utkarṣa ātmanaḥ  api syāt cetana tvāt acetanāt  tasamāda tattvam na upāsyam iti veda vidaḥ  matam utkarṣāt  brahma tā dhyāne yadi syāt  phalam añjasā brahmaṇaḥ  nīca tā dhyānāt anarthaḥ kim na jāyate acetanasya brahmatva dhyāne tuṣyiḥ nahi kvacid  nīcasya sva ātma tā dhyāne kupyati brahma lokavat  caṇḍālaḥ  nṛpa iti ukte nṛpaḥ caṇḍāla iti api kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ parijñāte nṛpeṇa syāt  kathañcana puratas  naradevasya caṇḍālaḥ  yadi pūjyate rājavat  kim na kopaḥ syāt  rājñaḥ  loke hi paśyati rājñaḥ tu puratas  prokte caṇḍālam nṛpa iti api ātmānam sa iti proktam itivat dhayā iva kupyati abhede na etayoḥ dhyāne kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ  vacasi api ayam rājā tvam iti ukte caṇḍāle atha nṛpe api ca caṇḍāla iti tu prokte samam eva hi dūṣaṇam dhyāte tu ekasya tad bhāve tad bhāvaḥ  anyasya kim na tad  naca eva tad avijñātam sarvajña brahmaṇā kvacid  tasmāt apeśalam sarvam anyasya brahma tā vacaḥ tasmāt  yathā ukta mārgeṇa brahma upāsyam mumukṣubhiḥ tathā upāsya añjasā dṛṣṭam brahma pāpam ca bhasmasāt  karoti nikhilam pūrvam pāścāttyasya api asaṅga tām karoti tad dviṣaḥ ca evam puṇya nāśaḥ  api asaṅga tā yad eva vidyayā iti atra pūrva uktāt hi viśiṣṭate pūrvam svarga ādi labdhi artham vīryavat tvena coditam karma vidyā yutam paścāt mokṣe vīrya pradam tu iti tatas  bhogena puṇyam ca kṣapayitvā itarat  tathā brahma dviṣ  brahmadarśī ca tamaḥ mokṣau  avāpnutaḥ brahmāṇam śata kālāt tu pūrvam ārabdha saṅkṣayaḥ brahmaṇaḥ tu eva tāvat tvam pañcāśat  brahmaṇaḥ tathā rudrasya viṃśat eva syāt indrasya arka ādike daśa anyeṣām brahma mātrasya tu anta ārabdha saṅkṣayaḥ brahmaṇā eva sahātas ca param nārāyaṇam vrajet  iti sat tattva vacanam svayam bhagavatā uditam devānām ca manuṣyāṇām etāvat  samam eva hi utkrānti mārgau devānām na prāyeṇa bhaviṣyataḥ karma kṣaya sa tatha utkrāntiḥ mārgaḥ  bhogaḥ catuṣyayam phalam mokṣa iti proktaḥ kramāt  pādeṣu coditaḥ sraṣṭṛṣu eva tu sṛjyānām praveśaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  laye devānām mārga uddiṣṭaḥ  na arcirādiḥ naca utkramaḥ sraṣṭuḥ tu grāsa bhūtasya dehaḥ tatra layam vrajet  yatas  sṛjyasya devasya na eva utkrāntiḥ tatas  bhavet  layāt ca eva arcirādīnām lokānām api sarvaśas  katham mārgaḥ  bhavet  teṣām viśatām uttamam svatas  jātānām mānuṣe loke devānām ca kadācana utkrānti mārgau bhavataḥ  na tadā muktiḥ iṣyate anyeṣām api sākṣāt tu muktiḥ prāpya api tam harim saha eva brahmaṇā bhūyāt iti śāstrasya nirṇayaḥ kṣmā ambhaḥ nala anila viyat ma nā aindriya artha bhūta ādibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ pratisañjighṛkṣuḥ avyākṛtam viśati yarhi guṇatraya ātmā kālam param svam anubhūya paraḥ svayambhūḥ evam paretya bhagavantam anupraviṣṭā ye yoginaḥ  jita marut manasaḥ  virāgāḥ tena eva sākam amṛtam puruṣam purāṇam brahma pradhānam upayānti agata abhimānāḥ bhagavantam anuprāptā api tu brahmaṇā saha paramam mokṣam āyānti liṅga bhaṅgena yoginaḥ prāptā api param devam saha eva brahmaṇā punar  ānanda vyaktiyāyānti pūrṇām liṅgasya bhaṅgataḥ iti śruti purāṇa ukti balāt  vijñāyate ca tad  bhogaḥ tu sarva devānām nara ādīnām ca vidyate tatra praveśaḥ  devānām uttarottarataḥ kramāt  ucyate deha gānām ca vṛttīnām evam eva tu tatra mokṣa svarūpam tu vādinaḥ pratibhā āśrayāt  nānā vadanti puṃsām hi matayaḥ  guṇa bhedataḥ pṛthak  pṛthak  prajāyante tamasā eva anyathāmatiḥ rajasā miśra buddhi tvam sattvena eva yathā matiḥ guṇa atītā vimuktānām matiḥ śuddha citiḥ yatas  sāmyageva atha nityā ca tad tad māhātmya yogataḥ bahaḷā ca ati viśadā spaṣṭā ca eva śriyaḥ  matiḥ mahā śuddha citi tvena tatas  api ati mahā acitiḥ aśeṣa uru viśeṣāṇām ati spaṣṭa tayā dṛśiḥ nityam eka prakārā ca nārāyaṇa matiḥ parā sūrya prabhāvat akhilam bhāsayanti nirantarā nirlepā vīta doṣā ca nityam eva avikāriṇī viśeṣa aṃsa tad gatān  tyaktavā prāyas tad lakṣaṇā śriyaḥ tathā eva spaṣṭa tā bhāvāt tad tantra tvāt ca kevalam na tādṛśī brahmaṇaḥ tu prāya eva śriyaḥ  yathā muktānām tu tad anyeṣām samudrataraḷā upamā agni jvālāvat eva syāt  smṛti gānām dṛśaḥ  bhavaḥ evaṃvidheṣu jñāneṣu tamasā muṣya dṛṣṭayaḥ khadyota sadṛśa ati alpa jñāna tvāt anyathā dṛśaḥ vadanti vādinaḥ  mokṣam nānā mata samāśrayāt āśritya pratibhām āha jinaḥ tatra atitāmasīm jñānāt  karma kṣayāt mokṣaḥ  bhavet  deha ākhya pañjarāt  pañjara unmukta khagavat alākā kāśa gocaraḥ nityam ūrdhvam vrajati eva pudgalaḥ  hasta pādavān iti tad  kena mānena mokṣa rūpam pradṛśyate gatiḥ ūrdhvā ca duḥkhetāḥ  gati tvāt laukikī yathā iti ukte ca anumāna eka śaraṇasya kim uttaram anūrdhva gati tā tatra yadi upādhiḥ khagasya ca dūra ūrdhva gamane duḥkham iti sādhya anugaḥ na saḥ pratisādhana rūpasya na anumānasya dūṣaṇam upādhiḥ pratirūpam hi sādhanam tad na ca aparam atha api sa śarīra tvam ca atra upādhiḥ na vai bhavet  gati tvam yatra dehi tvam iti yad  sādhana anugam āgamān anusāri tve prasaṅgaḥ  ayam yatas tatas  na apasiddhānta tā doṣaḥ prasaṅge yadi sā bhavet  tadā eva atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt na pasaṅgaḥ kvacid  bhavet  loka ākāśa gati tvam ced upādhiḥ sādhana anugaḥ saḥ  api iti ukte vadet  kim sa tasmāt  veda uditaḥ  bhavet  mokṣa evam svayam viṣṇuḥ yadi api īśaḥ  hi aśeṣa vid  cakāra saugata matam mohāya eva cakāra yad  asurāṇām ayogyānām vedamārge pravartatām atas  asura adhikāra tvāt na grāhyam tad matam kvacid  catuṣprakāram tad ca uktam śūnyam vijñānam ekalam anumeya bahis tattvam tathā pratyakṣa bāhya gam iti tatra tu ye śūnyam vadanti ajñāna mohitaḥ te mokṣam tādṛśam brūyuḥ niśśaṅkam māyinaḥ  yathā na kiñcina mukta yavasthāyām ātmā ātmīyam atha api vā ekasmin saṃsṛteḥ mukte na kiñcid avaśiṣyate tad saṃvṛtyā eva bhedaḥ  ayam cetana acetana ātmakaḥ dṛśyate saṃvṛteḥ dhvaṃse nirviśeṣa eva śūnyatā na sattvam na eva ca asattvam śūnya tattvasya vidyate na sukha tvam na duḥkha tvam na viśeṣaḥ  api kaścana nirviśeṣam syayambhātam nirlepam ajara amaram śūnyam tattvam asambādham nānā saṃvṛti varjitam aśeṣa doṣa rahitam manaḥ vācām agocaram mokṣa iti ucyate asadbhiḥ nānā saṃvṛti dūṣitam saṃsṛti avastham vijñeyam saṃvṛtya eva viśeṣyate sthitayā dhvastayā ca eva saṃsṛtiḥ mokṣa iti api kecid  teṣu anyathā prāhuḥ saṃvṛtya eva tu anekadhā avacchinnam mahā śūnyam nānāna pudgala śabditam yasya śūnya eka rasa tā jñānāt  sā tu apagacchati sa pudgalatva nirmuktaḥ  mahā śūnya tvam eṣyati saṃvṛtya anyaḥ tu avacchinnaḥ duḥkhāni anubhavati alam iti evam māyinaḥ ca āhuḥ eka jīvatva vādinaḥ bahu jīva matāḥ ca iti māyā teṣām tu saṃvṛtiḥ nirviśeṣatva vācā eva śūnyam brahmā eva naḥ bhidā saccit sukha ādikam ca eva kim kutaḥ akhaṇḍa vādinaḥ vyāvartya mātra bhedaḥ tu vidyate śūnya vādinaḥ anṛta ādeḥ apoham tu svayam eva hi manyate nirviśeṣa tvataḥ  na eva viśeṣaḥ  brahma śūnyayoḥ prāmāṇya ādi ca vedasya phalataḥ samam eva hi atattva avedakam yasmāt  pramāṇam tena kathyate atattva āvedaka tvam yad aprāmāṇyam satām matam dīrgha bhrānti karī ced  syāt atattva āvedaka pramā rajju sarpa ādi vijñānāt api ādhikya adamāna tā syāt āgamasya anivartya mahā moha pradatvataḥ talanailya ādi vijñānam ākāśe mānatāṃ vrajet  chatra ākāratva vijñānaṃcandra prādeśa tā matiḥ nirbheda tvam tu śūnyasya tena api aṅgīkṛtam sadā sattva asattva ādi dharmāṇām abhāva ubhaya ūḥ mataḥ na hi sat pratiyogi tvam śūnya tvam tena ca iṣyate na ca duḥkha virodhi tvāt anyā hi ānandata iṣyate māyinā śūnya pakṣe api jñānam jāḍya virodhi ca dharmaḥ te api na santi eva kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ tatas tayoḥ etādṛśānām pakṣāṇām dūṣaṇam prabhurā kṛtam sva pakṣa sādanena eva na abhāva iti ca uktitaḥ ātma abhāve pum arthaḥ ka iṣṭasya ātma avadhiḥ yatas  yadi na ātma avadhiḥ mokṣaḥ  mokṣaḥ syāt  ghaṭa śūnyatā kalpita tvāt  viśeṣāṇām māyinaḥ  api samam hi tad  dṛśyamāne viśeṣe api yadi ced aviśeṣa tā ghaṭa abhāvaḥ  aviśeṣaḥ syāt  pāścātyaḥ ca id anāgataḥ na mokṣaḥ  vimataḥ  yasmāt adehaḥ  ghaṭa śūnyatā yathā iti ukte vadet  kim sa yaḥ  anumā mātra mānakaḥ na ca māyī vadet  tatra pūrva uktena eva vartmanā amāna tvāt śruteḥ tasya nacā dehatva vādinī śrutiḥ kācid adeha tvam aprākṛta śarīra gā mokṣe bhogam yatas  brūte jakṣan krīḍan  iti śrutiḥ nirduḥkha tvāt na tad mokṣaḥ pratipannam yathā iti ca anumādūṣaṇam kim syāt  vādinoḥ śūnya māyinoḥ duḥkham duḥkhāt abhinna tvāt mokṣaḥ  api syāt asaṃśayam bhede sa dvaita tā eva syāt iti ādi amita doṣataḥ heyam māyā matena eva saha śūnya matam budhaiḥ evam vijñāna vādaḥ  api jñāna mātra viśeṣataḥ tasya api bhaṅguratva ādi viśeṣam apahāya hi advaitatā matam sākṣāt ukta doṣaḥ tatas  bhavet  kālaḥ  na kevala jñānī kāla tvāt  pratipannavat  etayā anumayā rodhāt na tādṛś mokṣa rūpa tā yadi kālaḥ  api na iti āha kadā iti praśna uttaram kim vakṣyati yadā avasthām vadet  sā pakṣatām vrajet  avasthā tvāt iti hi eva hetuḥ sā api kadā iti ca pṛṣṭe kālaḥ ca vaktavyaḥ  na akāla tvam tatas  bhavet  na kāla iti sāmānya niṣedhe kālaga pramā niruṇaddhi vaktavyaḥ  na akāla tvam tatas  bhavet  eka jīvatva pakṣe tu kāla abhāvāt iyam pramā kupitā kālam ādāya dvaitam eva upapādayet vimataḥ prapañcavān kālaḥ kāla tvāt  pratipannavat  iti ca anya anuma eka tvam jīvasya vinivārayet  kāla śabda īśvara ekatva matāni api evam eva hi nirākṛtāni teṣām ca sama tvāt  pakṣa doṣayoḥ jñānam svarasa bhaṅgayā iva nitya santām iṣyate bauddhābhyām aparābhyām tu tatra api ukta anumā ripuḥ mokṣaḥ  na śuddha vijñāna santānī kāla gatvataḥ pratipannaḥ  yathā iti etad anumānam tad uttaram anumānāni sarvāṇi pratisādhana yogataḥ niṣiddhāni ukta bhaṅgayā eva śrutayaḥ ca asmad ukti gāḥ sāṅkhaya naiyāyika ādyāḥ ca prāhuḥ mokṣam tu nissukham icchā dveṣa prayatna ādeḥ api sarva ātmanā layam tatra āhuḥ na etad api atra śobhanam śrutayaḥ yatas  mahānandam ca bhogam ca niyamena vadanti hi prākṛta priya hāniḥ tu priyā spṛṣṭiḥ iti īryate apriyam pratikūlam tad aviśeṣeṇa śabditam na asti hi aprākṛtam duḥkham sataḥ  jīvasya kutracid  priyam svarūpam eva asya bala ānanda ādi vākyataḥ heya tvāt apapriyasya eva priya hāneḥ aniṣṭhataḥ na samasta priya abhāvaḥ  mokṣe prokte tu yujyate apriyasya svarūpa tvam asureṣu eva hi śrutam asurā na evam evam ca na evam ca akhila mānuṣāḥ iti ātma priya hānāya kaḥ  yateta ca buddhimān sañjñā na asti iti api hi asya na amukta jñeyata iti hi dharmān ucchittim eva asya yatas  vaktayuttara śrutiḥ āśaṅkayā asya jñāna hānim maitreyyā moham āha mām bhavān iti uktavatyā hi na aham moham vadāmi te iti uktavā yājñavalkyaḥ  hi svarūpa anāśam ūcivān jñāna rūpasya vijñāna anāśaḥ tad nāśa eva yad  iti śūnya mata ucchittyai punar ānanda pūrvakān dharma ān āha api anucchinnān  tārkikaiḥ vinivāritān mātrā saṃsargam api āha tathā mādhyandina śrutiḥ ācikṣepa matam tad ca yasmin na viṣayādanam ghrāṇa ādi bhoga abhāvasya tu aniṣṭatva hṛdā śrutiḥ yena idam akhilam veda vijñātāram svam eva ca kena tam ca vijānīyāt iti aniṣṭam hi sarvathā na akhila jñāpakaḥ  viṣṇuḥ ajñeyaḥ  niyamena hi tad jñāna artham hi vedānām akhilānām pravartanam pratyakṣa āgama ātma vijñāna avirodha anubhavāt api na sva vijñānitāyām ca virodhaḥ kaścaneyate kartṛ karma virodhaḥ ca nitya anubhava virodhataḥ katham eva padam gacchet  virodhaḥ  dṛṣṭa bādhanam saḥ  aśnute sarva kāman  ca kāmānnī kāmarūpyatha iti ādi śrutayaḥ ca uktam artham eva vadanti hi asvātantryāt iva iti uktam na dvaita abhāvataḥ kvacid  ātmā eva abhūt iti hi asmāt aviśeṣa prasaṅgataḥ asvātantrya upamā bheda bhedeṣu iva udīritaḥ śabda tattva  iti proktam maitreyī ukta uttaram ca kim sukha ādi dharma hānau tu mukteḥ kiñca prayojanam yadi arthaḥ  duḥkha hāniḥ syāt anarthaḥ sukha nāśanam tayoḥ ca duḥkha hānāt hi sukha nāśaḥ  adhikaḥ  bhavet  prāpya api duḥkham su mahat  sukhaleśa āptaye janaḥ yatate sukha hānau hi kaḥ  mokṣāya yatet  pumān alpāt ca sukha anāśāt hi bibheti atitarām janaḥ mahat ca duḥkham āpnoti sukha nāśa nivṛttaye na ca rāga nimittam tad  vīta rāgā api sphuṭam nārada ādyāḥ sukha arthāya sahante duḥkham añjasā yuddha ādi darśanam yasmāt  su duḥkhena api kuvarte yadā indra vairocanayoḥ brahmāstrābhyām su tāpitāḥ api na eva ajahuḥ yuddha rasāt te nārada ādayaḥ iti skānda vacaḥ tasmāt  sukha abhāvasya kaḥ  yatet  vimataḥ  duḥkha yuj  yasmāt cetanaḥ san sukha ujkhitaḥ pratipannaḥ  yathā iti eva ca anumā kena vāryate sarva śruti purāṇeṣu sukha bhāva uktitaḥ tathā muktau na grāhyam eva etad  sukha abhāva matam budhaiḥ saḥ  anānandāt  vimuktaḥ sanna ānandī bhavati sphuṭam nirguṇe brahmaṇi mayi dhārayan viśadam manaḥ parama ānandam āpnoti yatra kāmaḥ  avasīyate na viṣṇu sadṛśam daivam na mokṣa sadṛśam sukham na veda sadṛśam vākyam na varṇaḥ  akāra sammitaḥ yatra ānandāḥ ca modāḥ ca mudaḥ pramuda āsate kāmasya yatra āptāḥ kāmāḥ tatra mām amṛtam kṛdhi iti śruti purāṇāni tatra tatra vadanti hi atas  mokṣe sukha abhāva iti yad kiñcid eva hi śiraḥ kara ādi abhāvaḥ ca na muktasya bhavet  kvacid  śrutayaḥ ca purāṇāni mānam atra bahūni ca na vartate yatra rajaḥ tamaḥ tayoḥ sattvam ca miśram na ca kāla vikramaḥ na yatra māyā kim uta apare hareḥ anuvratā yatra sura asura arcitāḥ śyāma avadātāḥ śatapatra locanāḥ piśaṅga vastrāḥ su rucaḥ supeśasaḥ sarve catur bāhava unmiṣat maṇi praveka niṣka ābharaṇāḥ suvarcasaḥ pravāḷa vaiḍūrya mṛṇāḷa varcasām parisphurat kuṇḍala mauli mālinām bhrājiṣṇubhiḥ yaḥ paritas  virājate lasat vimāna āvalibhiḥ mahātmanām vidyotamāna pramadā uttamābhiḥ sa vidyut abhra āvalibhiḥ yathā nabhaḥ śrīḥ yatra rūpiṇī uru gāya pādayoḥ karoti mānam bahudhā vibhūtibhiḥ ṛcām tvaḥ poṣam āste pupuṣvān gāyatram tvaḥ  gāyati śakvarīṣu brahmā tvaḥ  vadati jāta vidyām yajñasya mātram vimibhīta u tvaḥ kāma anna rūpī carati iti pūrva śrutyā purāṇa uktibhiḥ api adoṣaḥ dehaḥ svarūpa ātmaka eva teṣām muktim gatānām api ceyate hi śiraḥ kara ādyaiḥ api mukti bhājaḥ  yuktā yatas te puruṣā idānīm yathā iti pūrvā anumāḥ ca jīva svarūpam aṅga ādi yugāpayanti na brahma rūpa tvam amuṣya dehinaḥ  muktau  api syāt  pramayā kathañcid  sa brahmaṇā sahitaḥ  aśeṣa bhogān bhuṅkte tathā upetya sukha arṇavam tam yad tad param jyotiḥ upetya jīvaḥ  nija svara pūtvam avāpya kāmān bhuṅkte sa daivam puruṣottamaḥ  aja ātmā iti ca uktaḥ  guṇa pūrti hetoḥ setuḥ sa devaḥ  akhila mukti bhāgāmuta amṛtasya iṣya iha īśitā yad  ityādi vākyaiḥ bhagavat vaśaḥ san bhuṅkte akhilān mukti gataḥ  api bhogān kālaḥ  api asau na aikya yutaḥ pareṇa jīvasya kālaḥ  yata eṣa yadvat  iti ādikā api anumāḥ pramāṇam muktau ca jīvasya paratva rodhe katham ca yaḥ pūrvam asau na paścāt  bhavet  sa eva iti api yuktim eti yatas  na dṛṣṭam yad abhūt na pūrvam paścāt  tadāsā iti kutas ca kiñcid  naca eva muktau tu hareḥ pṛthaktavam aikyam tathā syāt iti yuktim eti yatas  na kutra api bhidā abhidā ca dṛṣṭā citaḥ cetanayā kutaścid  ittham matāni bhrama jāni yasmāt mokṣam samuddeśyam api bhrameṇa viduḥ na samyak  yad api iha laukikāḥ sukham mama syāt ca sadā iti jānate audāryam uccāvaca śaktiḥ ātma svara pūda arḍhyam ca nija svabhāvaḥ svātantryam āpūrṇa viśeṣa yogya tā virodha hāniḥ ca caturtha pāde vyavasthitiḥ tu aviśeṣaḥ sthitiḥ ca niṣedha sāmānya vidhi kriyāṇām vibhakta tā ca atvarayā eva siddhiḥ vipakṣa samprāpti viruddha hetavaḥ su śakya tā śaśvat ati prasiddhi viveka vinyāsa vicāra sañjñāḥ nānā pravṛttiḥ kṛtakṛtya tā ca vipakṣa tarkāḥ samatīta pāde mahā phala tvam pravivikta tā ca sandhi grahaḥ sādhanam āpta kṛtyam viśeṣa kāryam kṛti saṃsthitiḥ ca su yuktayaḥ nirṇaya gāḥ sva pakṣe vyāmiśratā kārya kara tvam artha kḷptiḥ su dārḍhyam paratantra tā ca samāna dharmaḥ kṛta śeṣa tā ca lokopamā pūrva mata anusārāḥ viśeṣa sāmya śrutiḥ āḍhya tā ca samāna lopaḥ  mahimā viśeṣaḥ kṛtārtha tā śaśvat anupravṛttiḥ siddhānta nirṇīti viśiṣṭa hetavaḥ pradhāna vāyuḥ tu iha vāyu nāmā bhūteṣu iti prokta gataḥ  api yuktayā yasmāt śrutau pavate ca iti bhūri proktaḥ  yatas  bhūta mānī ca saḥ  api mahāmānī tu alpa mānī ca yasmāt  tad śabdena api ucyate tena saḥ  api tasmin layam yānti bhūtāni aśeṣa krama avirodhena sa eva viṣṇau indra ādīnām tatra layaḥ kramam tu proktam viśeṣāt anusṛtya na anyat  tasmāt aśeṣā girijām praviśya tayā eva rudram saha tena vāṇīm tayā patim prāpya saha eva tena layam harau yānti samasta jīvāḥ somaḥ tu vāri īśa yutaḥ  aniruddham viśati asau kāmam asau ca vāruṇīm sā śeṣa devam sa giram ca sā eva vāyum viśati añja iti iha nirṇayaḥ umā girīśau  api bhāra tīrau  iti sma vāc  veda gatā bravīti ahi indra patnīm ahipam viriñca patnīm viriñcam ca vimukti kāle ta eva yad  tad padam āpnuvanti tad kāla etān samupāsya jīvāḥ brahmatva kāle praviśanti ca etāni iti sma vāc  tādṛśatām upaiti sūryaḥ  agni yuktaḥ  gurum āpya tena śakram saha enena suparṇa patnīm tayā suparṇam saha tena vāṇīm brahmāṇam etad gata eva yāti indrapraveśaḥ tu yadā ucyate atra tadā hi umā iti eva suparṇa patnī uktā suparṇaḥ ca girīśa nāmnā tatas  virodhaḥ ca na kaścana atra bhṛgu ādayaḥ  dakṣam avāpya tena prāpya indram etena suparṇa patnīm viśanti ye manavaḥ  rāja mukhyā manum praviśya atra gatā mahā indram ākāśa urvī ca gurum praviśya tena eva yātaḥ puruhūta devam sa nādayaḥ yatayaḥ kāmam eva viśanti śiṣṭā api havyavāham varṇa āśrama ācāra ratā manuṣyā dharmam manum saḥ  api sameti kāle tam eva sarve pitaraḥ sura anugāḥ sarve kuberam sa ca somam eva vimukti kāle praviśanti abhīkṣṇam bhogān  ca tad deha gatāḥ prabhuñjate ānandasu vyaktiḥ amutra teṣām bhavati atas ca iṣyata eva nirgatāḥ krīḍanti bhūyas ca samāviśanti tān eva sāyujyam idam vadanti sāyujya hīnāḥ ca laye tu sarve proktena mārgeṇa viśanti sṛṣṭau bahis ca niryānti tatas  anyadā api sāyujya bhājām bhavati praveśaḥ uktam samastam parama śrutau hi proktam tu sarga kramataḥ  viparyayaḥ muktau laye yadvat athaḥ layaḥ ca viparyayeṇa iti avadat  girām patiḥ layaḥ  yatas  muktiḥ iyam surāṇām bhogaḥ  viśeṣeṇa ca yam vadiṣyati uktaḥ ca bimba pratibimba bhāvaḥ piṅga śrutau  uktalayā anusārataḥ bimbe layaḥ  yad niyataḥ ca muktau cit ātmanām tad vaśatā ca sarvadā tejaḥ  abhidhām tu śriyam āpya viṣṇum agre tatas  putra tayā eva vāyuḥ āptaḥ prasūtaḥ punar eva viṣṇum praviśya muktaḥ praḷaye atra tiṣṭhati sarve api te mukta gaṇā amanda sāndram nija ānandam aśeṣatas  api bhuñjanta eva āsata īśa dehe laye atha sarge bahis eva yānti prayāti dharmam nirṛtiḥ tu śakram marut gaṇāḥ pārṣadāḥ tathā eva sarve aniruddham pṛtanā adhipa ādyāḥ tura śrutiḥ hi ittham iyam vimuktiḥ utkrānta mārgaḥ ca vimukta gamyam pāda uditam su krama vikramau ca sāntānikam prāptiḥ abhīṣyatā ca saukayarmiti anya matasya tarkāḥ viśeṣa samprāptiḥ uru tvam āptiḥ krama anurāgaḥ kathita anuvṛttiḥ siddhānta nirṇīti karāḥ pratīkam deha ādikam tad gatam eva ye narāḥ upāsate te puratas  samāpnuyuḥ brahmāṇam asmān matim āpya viṣṇum prāpsyanti atas  anye api tam āpya tasmāt harim gatā mukti bhājaḥ para ante atikrama uktiḥ kṛtiḥ artha lābhaḥ parā gatiḥ pāra gatiḥ tad okaḥ samasta kāryam vaśitā ca viśva sambhāvanā yuktayaḥ tu anya pakṣe sāmānya rūpam pratibhāna muktiḥ āścarya tā kṛtrima tā asta doṣaḥ viśeṣa kḷptiḥ kṛta niḥśramaḥ ca māhātmyam iti eva su nirṇaya arthāḥ ananya bhṛtya tvam iha uditabhyaḥ tu anyasya bhṛtyatva nivāraṇāya patim yad eṣām api viṣṇum āha hi uta amṛta tvasya patitva vāc dhareḥ ete api cā anya adhipatitva yuktā viṣṇu anya cittvena yathā pumāṃsaḥ prasiddhi bhājaḥ tu iti ca anumā eva hi abhīṣya siddhayai bhavati iha niścayāt  mukta svakīyā varayan tṛtā asti muktau  api brahma purassarāṇām anena devena tathā amunā ca hīṣye parārvāktana lokinām iti phalam śrutiḥ jñānata āha muktau  etad ca sarva aśubha nāśa liṅgāt  loka ādhipatyam ca vidhātuḥ eva sarva ātmanā iti āha tura śrutiḥ ca sarve balim deva gaṇā vahanti iti etad ca na anyasya hi yuktim eti lokā iti iha api tu lokinām vacaḥ  lokā iti hi eva ravaḥ prajāsu prayujyate sarva janaiḥ sadā eva tad māninaḥ  loka padena ca uktāḥ tad gāḥ tu muktā iha loka śabdā anyonya nāthā iti paiṅginām śrutiḥ aloka śabdena vimukti bhājaḥ  vācyāḥ padam tādṛś api iha yuktam loka abhidhāḥ ca api yatas  hi muktāḥ prakāśa rūpāḥ satatam ca sarve brahmā eva loka adhipatiḥ vimuktaḥ  bhavet iti prāha tura śrutiḥ ca naca iha vijñāna phalam samuktam loka ādhipatyam ravi bimbataḥ harau uktam pṛthak  tad ca purā eva yasmāt  bhedaḥ  amunā ityādi ca samyak uktaḥ tu apratyayam ca api atihāya na eva rūpeṇa tena iti bhavet iha arthaḥ bhavati asau  iti aṇu śabdam atra vihāya vākyāni bahūni doṣaḥ atas  jagat vayāpṛtimanta eva brahma ādayaḥ pūrṇa guṇāḥ krameṇa amandam ānandam ajasram eva bhuñjanta ātmīyam ajāt  samāsate namaḥ  namaḥ  aśeṣa viśeṣa pūrṇa guṇa eka dhāmne puruṣottamāya bhakta anukampāt ati śuddha saṃvid dātre anupādhi priya sat guṇa ātmane yasya trīṇi uditāni veda vacane rūpāṇi divya analam baṭ tad  darśatam ittham eva nihitam devasya bhargaḥ  mahat  vāyaḥ rāma vacaḥ nayam prathamakam pṛkṣaḥ  dvitīyam vapuḥ madhvaḥ  yad tu tṛtīyam etad anumā granthaḥ kṛtaḥ keśave niḥśeṣa doṣa rahita kalyāṇa akhila sat guṇa bhūti svayambhu śarva ādi vandyam tvām naumi me priyam
